4.17.3	idhmasaṃnahanaṃ hutam anumantrayate vedir barhiḥ śritaṃ havir idhmaḥ paridhayaḥ srucaḥ / ājyaṃ yajña ṛco yajur yājyāś ca vaṣaṭkārāḥ / saṃ me saṃnatayo namantām idhmasaṃnahane hute // iti
4.17.4	anūyājānām iṣṭam anumantrayate barhiṣo 'haṃ devayajyayā prajāvān bhūyāsam ity etaiḥ pratimantram
4.17.5	srucau vyūhyamāne vājatībhyām abhimantrayate vājasya mā prasaveneti dvābhyām
4.17.6	paridhīn ajyamānān abhimantrayate vasūn devān yajñenāpriprem / rudrān devān yajñenāpriprem / ādityān devānyajñenāpreprem iti
4.18.1	prastaram ajyamānam abhimantrayate samaṅktāṃ barhir haviṣā ghṛtena samādityair vasubhiḥ saṃ marudbhiḥ / sam indreṇa viśvebhir devebhir aṅktāṃ divyaṃ nabho gacchatu yat svāhā // iti
4.18.2	yatrābhijānāty agnir idaṃ havir juṣateti tan nigadāṃnigadāṃ devatām anumantrayate 'gner aham ujjitim anūjjeṣam ity etair mantrair yathādevatam
4.18.3	yarhi hotā yajamānasya nāma gṛhṇīyāt tarhi brūyād emā agmann āśiṣo dohakāmā iti
4.18.4	purastād apāttaṃ tṛṇam anuprahriyamāṇām anumantrayate divaḥ khīlo 'vatataḥ prthivyā adhyutthitaḥ / tenā sahasrakāṇḍena dviṣantaṃ śocayām asi / dviṣan me bahu śocatv oṣadhe mo ahaṃ śucam // iti
4.18.5	paridhiṣu prahriyamāṇeṣv āhavanīyam abhimantrayate vi te muñcāmi raśanā vi raśmīn iti
4.18.6	śaṃyuvākam abhimantrayate viṣṇoḥ śaṃyor ahaṃ devayajyayā yajñena pratiṣṭhāṃ gameyam iti
4.18.7	saṃsrāvabhāgān iṣṭāh anumantrayata iṣṭo yajño bhṛgubhir draviṇodā yatibhir āśīrdā vasubhir āśīrvānarthavabhiḥ / aṅgiraso māsya yajñasya prātar anuvākari ahauṣuḥ / tasya gacchatv ado ma āgamyād iti / yat kāmayate tasya nāma gṛhṇāti
4.19.1	antarvedi vedaṃ nidhāyābhimṛśati vedo 'si vittir asi videyety etair mantraiḥ
4.19.2	videyety ato 'nantaraṃ yad yad bhrātṛvyasyābhidhyāyet tasya nāma gṛhṇīyāt
4.19.3	patnīsaṃyājānām iṣṭam anumantrayate / somasyāhaṃ devayajyayeti prathamam / tvaṣṭur ahaṃ devayajyayeti divitīyam
4.19.4	rākāyā ahaṃ devayajyayā prajāvān bhūyāsam iti rākām / sinīvālyā ahaṃ devayajyayā paśumān bhūyāsam iti sinīvālīm / kuhvā ahaṃ devayajyayā puṣṭimān paśumān bhūyāsam iti kuhūm / etā eva tisraḥ patny anumantrayate mantāṃś ca saṃnamayati
4.19.5	uttamau patnīsaṃyājāv iṣṭāv anumantrayate devānāṃ patnīr agnir gṛhapatir yajñasya nithunaṃ tayor ahaṃ devayajyayā mithunena pra bhūyāsam iti
4.19.6	ājyeḍām anumantrayata iḍāsmān anu vastāṃ ghṛtena yasyāḥ pade punate devayantah / vaiśvānarī śakvarī vāvṛdhān apo yajñam asthita vaiśvadevī // iti
4.19.7	yā sarasvatī viśobhagīnā tasyāste bhaktivāno bhūyāsmeti phalīkaraṇahome hute mukhaṃ vimṛṣṭe
4.19.8	hute samiṣṭayajuṣi yajamānabhāgaṃ prāśnāti saṃ yajñapatir āśiṣeti
4.19.9	yadi yajamānaḥ pravaset prajāpatir vibhān nāma lokas tasmiṃs tvā dadhāmi saha yajamāneneti dhruvāyāṃ yajamānabhāgam avadhāya samiṣṭayajuṣā saha juhuyāt
4.20.1	purā pūrṇapātrāñ japati yajña śaṃ ma upa ca yajña śivo me saṃtiṣṭhasva sviṣṭo me saṃtiṣṭhasvāriṣṭome saṃtiṣṭhasva // yajña namas te yajña namo namaś ca te yajña / saṃtiṣṭhasva syonena me saṃtiṣṭhasva subhūtena me saṃtiṣṭhasva brahmavarcasena me saṃtiṣṭhasva yajñasyārddhim anu saṃtiṣṭhasva / upa te yajña nama upa te nama upa te nama iti
4.20.2	antarvedi praṇītā āsannā abhimṛśati ko vo 'yokṣīt sa vo vimuñcatv iti
4.20.3	athāsūpariṣṭāt saṃtatām udakadhārāṃ srāvayati sad asi san me bhūyā iti
4.20.4	athaināṃ pratidiśaṃ vyutsiñcati prācyāṃ diśi devā ṛtvijo mārjayantām ity etair mantrair yathārūpam
4.20.5	avaśiṣṭā antarvedi ninayati samudraṃ vaḥ prahiṇomi svāṃ yonim apigacchata / acchidraḥ prajayā bhūyāsaṃ māparāseci mat payaḥ // iti
4.20.6	mukhaṃ vimṛṣṭe yad apsu te sarasvati goṣv aśveṣu yan madhu / tena me vājinīvatī mukham aṅdhi sarasvati // iti
4.20.7	dakṣiṇe vedyante dakṣiṇena padā prāṅ viṣṇukramān krāmati viṣṇoḥ kramo 'sīty etais tribhir mantraiḥ / tiṣṭhaṃś caturthaṃ japati
4.20.8	tata ādityam upatiṣṭhate 'ganma suvaḥ suvar aganmeti pratipadya saṃ jyotiṣābhūvam ity antena
4.21.1	udyann adya mitramahaḥ saptnān me anīnaśaḥ / divainān vidyutā jahi nimrocann adharān kṛdhi // udyann adya vi nobhaja pitā putrebhyo yathā / dīrghāyus tvasya heśiṣe tasya no dehi sūrya // udyann adya mitramaha ārohann uttarāṃ divam / hrdrogaṃ mama sūrya harimāṇaṃ ca nāśaya // śukeṣu me harimāṇaṃ ropaṇākāsu dadhmasi / atho hāridraveṣu me har
4.21.2	pradakṣiṇam āvartate 'indrīm āvṛtam anvāvarte puṇyā bhavantu yā lakṣmīḥ parābhabantu yāḥ pāpīr iti
4.21.3	yady abhicared idam aham manuṣyām uṣyāyaṇasya śucā prāṇaṃ niveṣṭayāmīti dakṣiṇasya padaḥ pārṣṇyā niveṣṭayet
4.21.4	anvāhāryapacanam abhimantrayate 'gne vahne svaditaṃ nastanaye pituṃ paca / śaṃ tokāya tanuve syonaḥ // iti
4.21.5	tejo 'si ity abhiparyāvṛtyāhavanīyam abhimantrayate sam ahaṃ prajayā saṃ mayā prajeti
4.21.6	samiddho agne me dīdihi sameddhā te agne dīdyāsam ity upasamidhya vasumān yajño vasīyān bhūyāsam ity upasthāya gārhapatyam abhimantrayate 'gna āyuṃṣi pavasa iti pratipadya śataṃ himā ity antena
4.21.7	putrasya nāma gṛhṇāti tām āśiṣamā śāse tantave jyotiṣmatīm ity ajātaputraḥ / tām āśiṣamā śāse 'muṣmai jyotiṣmatīm iti jātaputraḥ
4.21.8	atha yadi bahuputraḥ syāt sarveṣāṃ nāmāni gṛhṇīyāj jyotiṣe tantave tveti
4.22.1	antarvedy āsīno 'tīmokṣān japati ye devā yajñahana ity etān
4.22.2	sarvaṃ vihāram abhimantrayate kas tvā sa tvā vi muñcatv iti
4.22.3	atraike yajamānabhāgasya prāśanaṃ samāmananti
4.22.4	sāṃnāyyayor api brāhmaṇo yajamānaḥ prāśnīyāt / idaṃ haviḥ prajananaṃ me astu daśavīraṃ sarvagaṇaṃ svastaye / ātmasani prajāsani paśusany abhayasani lokasani vṛṣṭisani // agniḥ prajāṃ bahulāṃ me karotv annaṃ payo reto asmāsu dhatta / rāyaspoṣam iṣam ūrjam asmāsu dīdharat // iti śṛṭasya / dadhikrāvṇo akāriṣam iti
4.22.5	tato vrataṃ visṛjate
4.22.6	dakṣiṇatas tiṣṭhann āhavanīyam abhimantrayate 'gne vratapate vratam acāriṣam iti
4.22.7	sa eṣa brāhmaṇasyaiva syān netarayor varṇayoḥ
4.22.8	vāyo vratapata iti vāyum upatiṣṭhate / āditya vratapata ity ādityam / vratānāṃ vratapata ity āhavanīyam
4.22.9	yajñasya punarālambhaṃ japati yajño babhuva sa ā babhūveti
4.22.10	prāṅ utkramya brūyād gomāṃ agna ity etām
4.22.11	yathānvavetam upaniṣkrāmann āha brāhmaṇāṃs tarpayitavā iti
4.22.12	tat khalv idaṃ yajamānaṃ na pravasato vidyata ity āśmarathyaḥ / athālekhanaḥ / evaṃvihitam evāsya pravasato yājamānaṃ bhavati / etāvan nānā / yāni saṃspṛśya karmāṇy adhvaryus tāni kuryāt
4.22.13	yajamānaḥ kāle tāṃ diśam abhimukho mantrān japet / prāṅmukhas tv eva viṣṇukramān gomatīm iti brūyād gomatīm iti brūyāt
5.1.1	agnīn ādhāsyamāno yo 'śvatthaḥ śamīgarbho bhūmiṃ mūlenāspṛṣṭas tasyāraṇī āharet / anāspṛṣṭa ity ekeṣām
5.1.2	yo aśvatthaḥ śamīgarbha ity etayā
5.1.3	uttarayā vā
5.1.4	brāhmaṇavyākhyātāḥ saṃbhārāḥ sapta pārthivāḥ sapta vānaspatyāḥ
5.1.5	tān āharati vaiśvānarasya rūpaṃ pṛthivyāṃ parisrasety etair mantrair yathārūpam
5.1.6	yaṃ tvā samabharaṃ jātaveda ity etayā saṃbhṛtaṃ saṃbhṛtaṃ yajamāno 'bhimṛśati
5.1.7	kṛttikāsu brāhmaṇa ādadhīta yaḥ kāmayeta mukhyo brahmavarcasī syām iti
5.1.8	rohiṇyām ādadhīta yaḥ kāmayeta sarvān rohān rohayeyam iti
5.1.9	mṛgaśīrṣa ādadhīta yaḥ kāmayeta śrīmāṇ syām iti
5.1.10	yaḥ purā bhadraḥ san pāpīyān syāt sa punar vasvor ādadhīta
5.1.11	yaḥ kāmayeta dānakāmā me prajāḥ syur iti sa pūrvayoḥ phalgunyor ādadhīta
5.1.12	yaḥ kāmayeta bhagī syām iti sa uttarayor ādadhīta
5.1.13	viparītam ekek samāmananti
5.1.14	hasta ādadhīta yaḥ kāmayeta pra me dīyeteti
5.1.15	yo bhrātṛvyavān syāt sa citrāyām ādadhīta
5.1.16	citrāyāṃ rājanya ādadhītety ekeṣām
5.1.17	viśākhayor ādadhīta prajākāmo 'nurādheṣv ṛddhikāmaḥ proṣṭhapadeṣu pratiṣṭhākāma iti vijñāyate
5.1.18	sūryanakṣatra eva syād ity ekeṣām
5.2.1	vasante brāhmaṇa ādadhīta
5.2.2	grīṣme hemante vā rājanyaḥ
5.2.3	śaradi vaiśyaḥ
5.2.4	varṣāsu rathakāraḥ
5.2.5	śiśiraḥ sārvavarṇikaḥ
5.2.6	atha yadi somena yakṣyamāṇaḥ syān na rtūn sūrkṣen na nakṣatram / yasminn eva kasmiṃś cid ṛtāv ādadhīta
5.2.7	amāvāsyāyāṃ vaiva paurṇamāsyām ādadhīta
5.2.8	yā pūrvābhyāṃ phalgunībhyāṃ paurṇamāsī syān na tasyām ādadhīta
5.2.9	vidyate caturthasya varṇasyāgnyādheyam ity ekam / na vidyata ity aparam
5.2.10	na jīvapitur agnyādheyaṃ vidyata ity ekam / vidyata ity aparam
5.2.11	udavasāyāgnīn ādhadhīta śālīnaḥ / na yāyāvara ādriyeta
5.2.12	prācīnapravaṇaṃ devayajanam adhyavasyate 'peta vīteti
5.2.13	tasminn udīcīṃ śālāṃ mītvāgreṇa madhyamaṃ vaṃśaṃ gārhapatyāyatanaṃ karoti
5.2.14	agreṇa gārhapatyāyatanam āhavanīyāya
5.2.15	aṣṭāsu prakrameṣu brāhamaṇo 'gnim ādadhīta / ekādaśasu rājanyaḥ / dvādaśasu vaiśyaḥ
5.2.16	caturviṃśatyām ādheya iti vijñāyate
5.2.17	aparimita ity ekeṣām
5.2.18	cakṣurnimita ity ekeṣām
5.2.19	dakṣiṇataḥ purastād vitṛtīyadeśe nedīyasi gārhapatyāyatanād dakṣiṇāgner āyatanaṃ karoti
5.2.20	agreṇāhavanīyāyatanaṃ samyaṃ minvati
5.2.21	agreṇa sabhyam āvasatham
5.2.22	tato yajamānaḥ keśaśmaśru vāpayate
5.2.23	kṣaume vasānau jāyāpatī agnim ādadhīyātām
5.2.24	te dakṣiṇākāle 'dhvaryave dattaḥ
5.2.25	purastād brāhmaudanikāt paridadhīyātām ity ekam / purastāt saṃbhāranivapanād ity apāram
5.2.26	yasmin nakṣatre 'gnim ādhāsyamānaḥ syāt tasya purastāt saṃvatsare dvādaśāhe caturahe tryahe dvyahe vaikāhe vā
5.3.1	adhivṛkṣasūrya aupāsanād agnim āhṛtyāpareṇa gārhapatyāyatanaṃ brahamaudanikam ādadhāti
5.3.2	niśāyām carmaṇi pājake vā brahmaudanaṃ catuḥśarāvaṃ tūṣṇīṃ nirvapati
5.3.3	api vā devasya tvā savituḥ prasave 'śvinor bāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇo hastābhyāṃ brahmaṇe prāṇāya juṣṭaṃ nirvapāmīti prathamam
5.3.4	brahmaṇe 'pānāyeti dvitīyam
5.3.5	brahmaṇe vyānāyeti tṛtīyam
5.3.6	brahṃaṇa iti caturtham / nirupya kṣīre śrapayati
5.3.7	caturṣu vodapātreṣu
5.3.8	na nirṇenekti nāvasañcatīty ekeṣām
5.3.9	jīvataṇḍulam iva śrapayitvoddhṛtya juhoti pra vedhase kavaya iti
5.3.10	athainaṃ caturdhā vyuddhṛtya sarpiṣopasicyān abhyucchindann iva caturbhya ārṣebhya upaharati
5.3.11	tebhyaḥ prāśitavadbhyaḥ samānaṃ varaṃ dadāti
5.3.12	brahmaudanaśeṣa ājyam ānīya citriyasyāśvatthasya samidhas tisra ārdrāḥ sapalāśāḥ stibhikavatīḥ prādeśamātrīr brahmaudane vivṛtyādadhāti
5.3.13	samidhāgniṃ duvasyateti gāyatrībhir brāhmaṇasya triṣṭugbhī rājanyasya jagatībhir vaiśyasya
5.3.14	sa etad vrataṃ caret
5.3.15	āgnyādheyān na māṃsam aśnīyān na striyam upeyāt
5.3.16	nāsyāgniṃ gṛhādd hareyur nānyata āhareyuḥ
5.3.17	naiṣo 'gnir anugaccchet
5.3.18	na prayāyāt
5.3.19	yady anu vā gacchet prayāyādevam eva brahmaudanaṃ paktvaiva samidha ādhāya bharaṇaśeṣaṃ samāpyāgnīn ādadhīta
5.3.20	yady enaṃ saṃvatsare nopanamed evam eva kuryāt
5.3.21	yas taṃ śvo 'gnim ādhāsyansyāt sa etāṃ rātriṃ vrataṃ carati
5.3.22	na māṃsam aśnāti na striyam upaiti noparyāste / jugupsetānṛtāt
5.3.23	adhvaryur eva vrataṃ cared ity ekam / sarva ity aparam
5.4.1	gārhapatyāyatane kalmāṣam ajaṃ badhnāti prajā agne saṃvāsayety etayā
5.4.2	vīṇātūṇavair etāṃ rātriṃ yajamānaṃ jāgarayanti puṇyaiś ca nīthyaiḥ
5.4.3	śalkais tāṃ rātrim agnim indhīta śalkair agnim indhānety etayā
5.4.4	tasminn upavyuṣam araṇī niṣṭapej jātavedo bhuvanasya reta iti dvābhyām
5.4.5	anugamayaty etam agnim
5.4.6	yajamānāyāraṇī prayacchaty agnī rakṣāṃsi sedhatīti
5.4.7	te yajamānaḥ pratīkṣate mahī viśpatnī sadane ṛtasyeti
5.4.8	ārohataṃ daśatam ity etayā pratigṛhyottarābhyām abhimantrayate
5.4.9	tato vācaṃ yacchaty anṛtāt satyam upaimīti
5.4.10	vāgyata āsta āgner manthanāt
5.4.11	tata ātmany agniṃ gṛhṇāte adhvaryur yajamānaś ca mayi gṛhṇāmy agre agnim iti dvābhyām
5.4.12	agnyāyatanāny uddhanty uddhanyamānam asyā amedhyam iti
5.4.13	uddhatyāvokṣati śaṃ no devīr abhiṣṭaya ity etayā
5.4.14	śuṣkeṣūpavāteṣu saṃbhārān nivapati
5.4.15	dvaidhaṃ vibhajyārdhān pūrveṣv ardhān aparayoḥ
5.4.16	agner bhasmāsy agneḥ purīṣam asīti gārhapatyāyatane sikatā nivapati
5.4.17	evam anvāhāryapacanāyatana evam āhavanīyāyatane evaṃ sabhyāvasathyayoḥ
5.4.18	evam anupūrvāṇy evaiṣv ata ūrdhvaṃ karmāṇi kriyante
5.5.1	ekaikaśaḥ pārthivān nivapati
5.5.2	saṃjñānam asi kāmadharaṇam ity ūṣān
5.5.3	nivapan yad adaś candram asi kṛṣṇaṃ tad ihāstv iti manasā dhyāyati
5.5.4	udehy agna ity ākhūtkaram
5.5.5	yat pṛthivyā anāmṛtam iti gārhapatyāyatane valmīkavapāṃ nivapati
5.5.6	yad antarikṣasyānāmṛtam ity anvāhāryapacanāyatane
5.5.7	yad divo 'nāmṛtam itītareṣu
5.5.8	ut samudrād iti sūdam
5.5.9	iyaty agra āsīr iti varāhavihatam
5.5.10	ado devīti śarkarāḥ
5.5.11	śarkarā nivapan yaṃ dviṣyāt taṃ dhyāyet
5.5.12	uttareṇa saṃbhārān sauvarṇān hiraṇyaśakalānupāsyati yās te śivās tanuvo jātaveda iti
5.5.13	ekaikam ādhāyādhāya rajataṃ dveṣyāyāti prayacchati
5.5.14	yadi dveṣyaṃ nādhigacched atipravidhyet
5.5.15	evaṃ saṃsṛjya vānaspatyān nivapati puṣkaraparṇam aśvattham udumbaraṃ palāśaṃ śamīṃ vikaṅkatam aśanihatasya vṛkṣasya kāṣṭham itaḥ prathamaṃ jajñe agnir ity etayā
5.5.16	sarvān saṃbhārān saṃprayauti saṃ yā vaḥ priyās tanuvaḥ // saṃ vaḥ sṛjāmi hṛdayānīti dvābhyām
5.6.1	brāhmaudanikasya bhasmāpodūhya daśahotrāraṇī samavadhāyopatiṣṭhaty aśve 'gniṃ manthati sahāgne 'gninā jāyasveti
5.6.2	mathyamāne caturhotṝn yajamānaṃ vācayati
5.6.3	jāte varaṃ dadāti
5.6.4	jātam abhiprāṇiti prajāpates tvā prāṇenābhiprāṇimīti
5.6.5	athainaṃ hastābhyāṃ parigṛhṇāty ajījanann amṛtaṃ martyāsa iti
5.6.6	tataḥ prāñcam uddhṛtyānuditaṃ āditye rathantare gīyamāna āsīnaḥ saṃbhāreṣu gārhapatyam ādadhāti
5.6.7	bhṛgūṇāṃ tvā vratapate vratenādadhāmīti bhārgavasyādadhyāt / aṅgirasāṃ tvā vratapate vratenādadhāmīti yo brāhmaṇa āṅgirasaḥ syāt / ādityānāṃ tvā devānāṃ vratapate vratenādadhāmīty anyāsāṃ brāhmaṇīnāṃ prajānām / varuṇasya tvā rājño vratapate vratenādadhāmīti rājñaḥ / indrasya tvendriyeṇa vratapate vratenādadhāmīti rājanyasya
5.6.8	saṃbhāreṣv eva sarvān agnīn ādadhāti
5.7.1	yatha rṣyādhānenādhāya vyāhṛtībhyām adadhāti bhūr bhuva iti
5.7.2	tataḥ sarparajñībhyāṃ bhūmir bhūmnety etayā ca dvitīyayā ca
5.7.3	etābhyām evāhitaṃ yajamāna upatiṣṭhate
5.7.4	tato gharmaśirasā gharmaḥ śira iti
5.7.5	etenaivāhitaṃ yajamāna upatiṣṭhate
5.7.6	tata etābhir antata ādadhāti
5.7.7	ṛtaṃ stṝṇāmi purīṣam // sugārhapatya iti caitābhyām
5.7.8	ahaṃ tvad asmīty āhitaṃ yajamāna upatiṣṭhate
5.7.9	tato 'śvasya dakṣiṇe karṇe 'gnitanūr yajamānaṃ vācayati yā vājinn agneḥ pavamānā paśuṣu priyā tanūs tām āvaha // yā vājinn agneḥ pāvakāpsu priyā tanūs tām āvaha // yā vājinn agneḥ sūrye śuciḥ priyā tanūs tām āvaha // iti
5.7.10	gārhapatya idhmam ādīpyāhavanīyam udyacchata ojase balāya tvodyaccha iti
5.7.11	uddhriyamāṇe vāmadevyaṃ gāyati
5.7.12	uparīvāgnim udgṛhṇīyād uddharan
5.7.13	nāsyadaghnam atiharet
5.7.14	udyatam idhmam upayataṃ dhārayanti
5.7.15	athānvāhāryapacanaṃ yataḥ kutaś cāhṛtyordhvañjur ādadhāti
5.7.16	araṇībhyāṃ vā mathitvā
5.7.17	yatha rṣyādhānenādhāya vyāhṛtyādadhāti bhuva iti
5.7.18	tataḥ sarparajñībhyāṃ bhūmir bhūmnety etayā ca tṛtīyayā ca
5.7.19	etābhyām evāhitaṃ yajamāna upatiṣṭhate
5.7.20	tato gharmaśirasā vātaḥ prāṇa iti
5.7.21	etenaivāhitaṃ yajamāna upatiṣṭhate
5.8.1	tato 'śvaprathamāḥ prāñco 'bhipravrajati prācīm anu pradiśaṃ prehi vidvān ity etayā / divaḥ pṛthivyāḥ pary antarikṣād ity etābhiś catasṛbhiḥ
5.8.2	jānudaghne 'gre haraty atha nābhidaghne 'thāsyadaghne
5.8.3	nāgniṃ cādityaṃ ca vyaveyāt
5.8.4	pūrvam agniṃ harati paścād anveti
5.8.5	dakṣiṇato brahmā rathaṃ vartayati rathacakraṃ vā bṛhaspate pari dīyā ratheneti
5.8.6	etāṃ vāpratirathasya rcaṃ brahmā japatīty ekeṣām
5.8.7	tathā rathaṃ vartayati yāvac cakraṃ triḥ parivartate
5.8.8	yaḥ sapatnavān bhrātṛvyavān syāt tasya punaś cakraṃ triḥ parivartayet
5.8.9	samayādhve varaṃ dadāti
5.8.10	samayādhve hiraṇyaṃ nyasyātikrāmati nāko 'si bradhnaḥ saṃkramaṇaḥ pratiṣṭhā yajamānasyeti
5.8.11	uttareṇa saṃbhārān dakṣiṇena padā prāñcam aśvam ākramayaty abhyasthād iti
5.8.12	etasminn eva pade pradakṣiṇam āvartyottarayā pratyañcam ākramayati
5.8.13	pārśvata ākramayed yathāhitasyāgner aṅgārāḥ padam abhyavavarteran
5.8.14	yady aśvo na syād balīvarda evaitat karma kuryāt
5.8.15	ajasya pada ādheya iti vijñāyate
5.8.16	kamaṇḍalupada ity ekeṣām
5.8.17	aśvam upasaṃgṛhya purastāt pratyaṅmukhaḥ prahvas tiṣṭhan bṛhati gīyamāne
5.9.1	ardhodite sūrya āhavanīyam ādadhāti
5.9.2	sarvodite brahmavarcasakāmasyādadhyāt
5.9.3	yatha rṣyādhānenādhāya vyāhṛtībhir ādadhāti bhūr bhuvaḥ suva iti
5.9.4	tataḥ sarparāñjībhyāṃ bhūmir bhūmna ity etayā ca caturthyā ca
5.9.5	etābhyām evāhitaṃ yajamāna upatiṣṭhate
5.9.6	tato gharmaśirasy arkaś cakṣur iti
5.9.7	etenaivāhitaṃ yajamāna upatiṣṭhate
5.9.8	prāṇaṃ tvāmṛta ādadhāmīti ca dvābhyām
5.9.9	antata ādhāyopatiṣṭhata ānaśe vyānaśa iti
5.9.10	nihite vārvavantīśyaite gāyati
5.9.11	nāhitam agnim anabhihutam upaspṛśet / ājyena cauṣadhībhiś ca śamatiyatavya iti vijñāyate
5.9.12	yā te agne paśuṣu pavamānā priyā tanūr yā pṛthivyāṃ yāgnau yā rathaṃtare yā gāyatre chandasīdaṃ te tām avarundhe / tasyai te svāhā // yā te agne 'psu pāvakā priyā tanūr yāntarikṣe yā vāyau yā vāmadevye yā traiṣṭubhe chandasīdaṃ te tām avarundhe / tasyai te svāhā // yā te agne sūrye śuciḥ priyā tanūr yā divi yāditye yā bṛhati yā jāgate chandasī
5.10.1	ājyena cauṣadhībhiś ca śamayitvāhavanīyāt sabhyāvasathyau yatha rṣyādhānenādadhāti
5.10.2	araṇībhyāṃ vā mathitvā
5.10.3	sabhāyāṃ sabhyam āvasatha āvasathīyam
5.10.4	dakṣiṇāgnau sabhyāvasthyayor iti vijñāyate
5.10.5	yajñāyajñiyaṃ gāyed ity ekam / sarveṣv ity aparam
5.10.6	brahmāgnyādheye sāmāni gāyed iti vijñāyate
5.10.7	nāgnyādheye sāmāni gāyed ity ekeṣām
5.10.8	agnipavamānībhis tisṛbhis tisra āśvatthyīḥ samidha ādadhāty agna āyūṃṣi pavasa ity etābhis tisṛbhiḥ
5.10.9	śamīmayyas tisraḥ samidho ghṛtānvaktā ādadhāti samudrād dūrbhir ity etābhis tisṛbhiḥ
5.10.10	preddho agne dīdihi puro na ity audumbarīm / vidhema te parame janmann agna iti vaikaṅkatīm / tāṃ savitar vareṇyasya citrām iti śamīmayīm
5.10.11	sarveṣv ekaikām
5.10.12	prātar agnihotrasyāvṛtā tūṣṇīm agnihotraṃ juhoti
5.10.13	araṇye 'nuvākyābhir ghorābhis tanūbhir yajamāna āhavanīyam upatiṣṭhate yās te agne ghorās tanuvas tābhir amuṃ gaccheti brūyād yaṃ dviṣyāt
5.11.1	tiraḥ pavitram ājyaṃ nirupyotpūya sruvaṃ ca juhūṃ ca niṣṭapya saṃmṛjya caturgṛhītena sruvaṃ pūrayitvā dvādaśagṛhītena vā pūrṇāhutiṃ juhoti / sapta te agne samidhaḥ sapta jihvā ity etām anudrutya svāhākāraṇe juhoti
5.11.2	hutāyāṃ pūrṇāhutau varaṃ dadāti
5.11.3	evam evāta ūrdhvaṃ darvihomeṣu nirvapaty utpunāti niṣṭapati saṃmārṣṭy antataḥ svāhākāraṃ dadhāti
5.11.4	yān pratinigadya juhoty ete darvihomā bhavanti yāṃś ca juhotīti codayet
5.11.5	tato yajamāna āhavanīyam upatiṣṭhate ye te agne śive tanuvau virāṭ ca svarāṭ cety anuvākaśeṣeṇa
5.11.6	tata etām āhutiṃ ye agnaye divo ye pṛthivyā iti
5.11.7	bhāsvato virājakramair upatiṣṭhate 'tharva pituṃ me gopāyety anvāhāryapacanam / narya prajāṃ me gopāyeti gārhapatyam / śaṃsya paśūn me gopāyety āhavanīyam / sapratha sabhāṃ me gopāyeti sabhyam / ahe budhnaya mantraṃ me gopāyety āvasathīyam / pañcāgnīn iti ca sarvān
5.12.1	āgneyasya tantraṃ prakramayati
5.12.2	samānamā nirvapaṇāt
5.12.3	āgneyam aṣṭākapālaṃ nirvapati
5.12.4	niruptaṃ havir upasannam aprokṣitaṃ bhavaty atha sabhyāvasathyayor madhye 'dhidevanam uddhatyāvokṣyākṣān nyupyākṣeṣu hiraṇyaṃ nidhāya vyūhya samūhya juhoti niṣasāda dhṛtavratety etayā
5.12.5	śataṃ yajamānāyākṣān prayacchann āha vrīhibhyo gāṃ dīvyatāhiṃsantaḥ parvāṇi viśasateti
5.12.6	tad yajamānaḥ kṛtaṃ vijityottiṣṭhati
5.12.7	gāmasya tad ahaḥ sabhāyāṃ dīvyeyuḥ
5.12.8	tasyāḥ paruṃṣi na hiṃsyuḥ
5.12.9	tāṃ sabhāsadbhya upaharet
5.12.10	tayā yad gṛhṇīyāt tad ubhayam annaṃ saṃskṛtya brāhmaṇān bhojayet
5.12.11	āvasathe madhye pariṣado hiraṇyaṃ nidhāyābhijuhoti pra nūnaṃ brahmaṇaspatir ity etayā
5.12.12	tato yajamāno 'gnīn upatiṣṭhate kalpetāṃ dyāvāpṛthivī // ye agnayaḥ samanasa iti dvābhyām
5.12.13	samānamā dakṣiṇākālāt
5.12.14	vardhamānā dakṣiṇā deyeti vijñāyate

5.12.16	ajaṃ cāśvaṃ brahmaṇe
5.12.17	dhenuṃ hotre
5.12.18	anaḍvāham adhvaryave
5.12.19	mithunau gāvau vāso ratham iti sarvebhyaḥ

5.12.21	sahādiṣṭadakṣiṇābhiḥ saṃcakṣītety ekam
5.13.1	anyatrādiṣṭadakṣiṇābhya ity aparam
5.13.2	yady anāḍhyo 'gnīn ādadhītāpy ekāṃ gāṃ dakṣiṇāṃ dadhyāt
5.13.3	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
5.13.4	sāyam agnihotraṃ hoṣyan daśahotāraṃ manasānudrutyāhavanīye sagrahaṃ juhoti
5.13.5	dvādaśāham ajasreṣv agnihotraṃ juhoti
5.13.6	vratacārī bhavati

5.13.18	tato 'gnaye pāvakāyāgnaye śucaye / triṃśanmānacatvariṃśanmāne hiraṇye dakṣiṇā
5.13.19	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate

5.13.21	kāmam ardhamāse māsy ṛtau saṃvatsare / sadya ity ekeṣām
5.13.22	samānatantrāṇi vāgneyena syuḥ
5.13.23	vijñāyate na somena yakṣyamāṇaḥ
5.14.1	purā saṃvatsarāt tanuhaviṃṣi nirvapet
5.14.2	api vāgnaye pavamānāyāgnaye pāvakāyāgnaye śucaya ājyāhutīr hutvā somadevatābhyo vā nirvapet
5.14.3	upariṣṭāt tanuhavirbhyo 'gnīṣomīyam ekādaśakapālam anunirvapaty aindrāgnam ekādaśakapālam adityai ghṛte carum
5.14.4	agnīṣomīyo brāhmaṇasyaiva syān netarayor varṇayoḥ
5.14.5	samānam ā phalīkaraṇāt

5.14.7	sahetarān pinaṣṭi
5.14.8	samānamā kapālopadhānāt
5.14.9	aindrāgnasya kapālāny upadhāya prathamena kapālamantreṇa carusthālīm upadadhāti
5.14.10	dhruvo 'sīti mantraṃ saṃnamati / dhruvāsīti vā
5.14.11	piṣṭānām āvṛtā taṇḍulān saṃvapaty utpunāti
5.14.12	yajuṣājyam utpūya carusthālyām ānayati
5.14.13	yathādhikaraṇaṃ mantraṃ namati
5.14.14	adhiśrayaṇamantreṇa caravyān āvapati
5.14.15	sthālyaiva carum āsādayati
5.14.16	eṣa evāta ūrdhvaṃ carūṇāṃ kalpo bhavaty anyatrājyagrahaṇāt
5.14.17	saptadaśa sāmidhenyo bhavanti
5.14.18	samānam ā haviṣāṃ pradānāt
5.15.1	ādityaṃ hutam anumantrayate 'ditya ahaṃ devayajyayā yajñena pratiṣṭāṃ gameyam iti
5.15.2	evam eva sarvān ādityān anumantrayate
5.15.3	ādityasya havir ucchiṣṭaṃ caturdhākaraṇakāle sarvaṃ brahmaṇe pariharati
5.15.4	taṃ catvāra ārṣeyā ṛtvijaḥ prāśnanti
5.15.5	tebhyaḥ prāśitav adbhyo dhenuṃ varaṃ dadāti
5.15.6	upāṃśudevatā āgnyādheyikā iṣṭayo bhavantīty ekeṣām
5.15.7	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
5.15.8	darśapūrṇamāsāv ārapsyamāṇaḥ sārasvatau homau purastāj juhuyāt purṇā paścāt // yat te devā adadhur iti dvābhyām
5.15.9	anvārambhaṇīyām iṣṭiṃ nirvapati
5.15.10	āgnavaiṣṇavam ekādaśakapālaṃ sarasvatyai caruṃ sarasvate dvādaśakapālam
5.15.11	agnaye bhagine puroḍāśam aṣṭākapālaṃ caturthaṃ nirvaped bhagakāmaḥ
5.15.12	samānam ā haviṣāṃ pradānāt
5.15.13	sārasvataṃ hutam anumantrayate sarasvatyā ahaṃ devayajyayā vācam annādyaṃ puṣeyam iti
5.15.14	evam eva sarvān sarasvatīdevatān anumantrayate
5.15.15	tasya purastāt sviṣṭakṛto jayān juhoti cittaṃ ca cittiś ceti dvādaśa / prajāpatir jayān indrāya vṛṣṇe prāyacchad iti trayodaśīṃ juhuyāt
5.16.1	agne baladeti caturdaśīṃ brahmavarcasakāmasya
5.16.2	citraṃ tasya janatāyāṃ bhavati / śavalam iva tv asyātmana jāyate
5.16.3	mithunau gāvau dakṣiṇā
5.16.4	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
5.16.5	darśapūrṇamāsāv ārabhamāṇaś caturhotāraṃ manasānudrutyāhavanīye sagrahaṃ juhoti
5.16.6	darśapūrṇamāsāv ārabhate
5.16.7	paurṇamāsīṃ pūrvam
5.16.8	amāvāsyāyām ādadhānasyaitad avikṛtam
5.16.9	paurṇamāsyāṃ tu pūrvasmin parvaṇi seṣṭi sānvārambhaṇīyaṃ sadyo 'pavṛjya
5.16.10	śvo bhūte paurṇamāsena yajate
5.16.11	athaitāny āhitāgnivratāni bhavanti
5.16.12	nānṛtaṃ vadet
5.16.13	nāsya brāhmaṇo 'nāśvān gṛhe vaset
5.16.14	sūryoḍḍham atithiṃ vasatyai nāparundhyāt
5.16.15	na sāyam ahute 'gnihotre 'śnīyāt
5.16.16	na prātar ahute
5.16.17	na naktam anyad annādyād dadyāt
5.16.18	naktam annaṃ dadann adayīta
5.16.19	na rjīṣapakvasyāśnīyāt
5.16.20	klinnaṃ dāru nādadhyāt
5.16.21	antarnāvyāpastāsāṃ nāśnīyāt
5.16.22	svakṛta iriṇe nāvasyet
5.16.23	rajataṃ hiraṇyaṃ barhiṣi na dadyāt
5.16.24	tūṣṇīṃ hiṃkṛtya striyam upeyāt
5.17.1	punarādheyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
5.17.2	tasyāgnyādheyena kalpo vyākhyātaḥ
5.17.3	vikārān anukramiṣyāmaḥ
5.17.4	yo 'gnyādheyena nadhnoti sa punarādheyam ādhatta iti vijñāyate
5.17.5	jyānyāṃ putram artyāyāṃ yadaivāhitāgnir aṅgena vidhur atāmiyād athādadhītety ekeṣām
5.17.6	prajākāmaḥ punarādadhīta paśukāmaḥ punarādhītān nādyakāmaḥ punarādadhīta pratiṣṭhākāmaḥ punar ādadhīteti vijñāyate
5.17.7	yāvaj jīvaṃ punarādheyasya kālo nātyetīty āśmarathyaḥ / saṃvatsaram ity ālekhanaḥ
5.17.8	āgneyam aṣṭākapālaṃ nirvaped vaiśvānaraṃ dvādaśakapālam agnim udvāsayiṣyan
5.17.9	tasya purastāt sviṣṭakṛṭa etā āhutir juhoti yā te agne utsīdataḥ pavamānā paśuṣu priyā tanus tayā saha pṛthivīm āviśa / rathantareṇa sāmnā gāyatreṇa chandasā svāhā
5.18.1	yā te agna utsīdataḥ pāvakāpsu priyā tanūs tayā sahāntarikṣam āviśa / vāmadevyena sāmnā traiṣṭubhena chandasā / tato na iṣam ūrjam ākṛdhi gṛhamedhaṃ ca vardhaya svāhā // yā te agna utsīdataḥ sūrye śuciḥ priyā tanūs tayā saha divam āviśa / bṛhatā sāmnā jāgatena chandasā / tato na vṛṣṭyāvadhi svāhā // yās te agne vibhaktīr indraḥ sūkara ābharat
5.18.2	paurṇamāsyāṃ jvalato 'gnīn udvāsayati
5.18.3	saṃvatsaram avasṛṣṭāgniḥ syād ity ekam / aparimitam ity aparam
5.19.1	athaitāni punarādheyanakṣatrāṇe rohiṇī punarvasū anūrādhā iti
5.19.2	varṣāsu śaradi vādadhīta
5.19.3	madhyaṃdina ādheya iti vijñāyate
5.19.4	sarvān madhyaṃdina ādadhītety ekam / āhavanīyaṃ sabhyāvasathyāv ity aparam
5.19.5	samānam ā gārhapatyasyādhānāt
5.19.6	sarvābhiḥ sarparajñībhir gārhapatyam ādadhāti
5.19.7	samānam āhavanīyasyodyamāt
5.19.8	upolavā darbhā bhavanti parukṇāḥ saṃvatsarapravātāḥ / teṣām idhmam ādīpyāhavanīyam udyacchate
5.19.9	yat tvā kruddhaḥ parovapety anvāhāryapacana ādadhāti
5.19.10	yat te manyuparoptasyety āhavanīyam
5.19.11	mano jyotir juṣatām ity āhitam āhitam upatiṣṭhate
5.19.12	samānam ā tūṣṇīm agnihotrāt
5.19.13	sapta te agne samidhaḥ sapta jihvā iti tūṣṇīm agnihotraṃ juhoti
5.19.14	samānam ā nirvapaṇāt
5.19.15	āgneyaṃ pañcakapālaṃ nirvapati
5.19.16	sa eṣo 'ṣṭākapalāsya sthānaṃ pratyeti
5.19.17	pañcadaśa sāmidhenyo bhavanti saptadaśa vā
5.19.18	yat prāg uttamād anūyājāt tenopāṃśu pracaranty anyatra sviṣṭakṛtaḥ
5.19.19	samānam ā prayojebhyaḥ
5.19.20	caturṣu prayājeṣu catasro vibhaktīr dadhāti
5.20.1	agnāgne 'gnāv agne 'gnināgne 'gnim agna iti
5.20.2	upariṣṭād yeyajāmahād dadhyād ity ekam / purastād āmantraṇīyāt padād ity aparam
5.20.3	yaṃ kāmayeta rdhnuyād iti tasyopariṣṭāt prayājānāṃ vibhaktīr dadhyāt purastād vaṣaṭkārāt
5.20.4	svayaṃsaṃpanna uttamaḥ prayājaḥ
5.20.5	samānam ājyabhāgābhyām
5.20.6	budhanvānāgneya ājyabhāgo bhavaty agniṃ stomena bodhayeti
5.20.7	pavamānavān saumyo 'gna āyūṃṣi pavasa iti
5.20.8	juṣāṇo agniḥ pavamāna ājyasya haviṣo vetv iti yajati
5.20.9	agnir mūrdheti saumyasya loke kuryāt prajākāmaḥ paśukāmo vā
5.20.10	agne tam adyeti paṅktyo yājyānuvākyā bhavanti / dve haviṣo dve sviṣṭakṛtaḥ
5.20.11	punar ūrjā // saha rayety abhitaḥ puroḍāśam āhutī juhoti
5.20.12	samānam ā dakṣiṇākālāt
5.20.13	ubhayīr dakṣiṇā dadāty āgnyādheyikīḥ paunar ādheyikīś ca
5.20.14	tā imāḥ punarādheyadakṣiṇāḥ
5.21.1	punar niṣkṛto rathaḥ punar utsyūtaṃ vāsaḥ punar utsṛṣṭo 'naḍvān śatamānaṃ hiraṇyam iti
5.21.2	samānam ānūyājebhyaḥ
5.21.3	dvayor anūyajayor dve vibhakti dadhāti deve agnau devo agnir iti
5.21.4	vyākhyāto vibhaktilokaḥ
5.21.5	svayaṃsaṃpanna uttamo 'nūyājaḥ
5.21.6	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
5.21.7	āgnivāruṇam ekādaśakapālam anunirvapati
5.21.8	sa eṣo 'gnīṣomīyasya sthānaṃ pratyeti
5.21.9	sarveṣāṃ vānunivapyāṇām
5.21.10	saṃtiṣṭhate punarādheyam
5.21.11	ya ūrdhvaṃ punarādheyād agnim ādadhīta sa etān homān juhuyād lekaḥ salekaḥ suleka iti
5.21.12	ta ima āgnyādheyikānāṃ darvihomānāṃ sthānaṃ pratiyanti
5.21.13	yad araṇyoḥ samārūḍho naśyet punarādheyaṃ kurvītety āśmarathyaḥ / agnyādheyam ity ālekhanaḥ
5.21.14	yasyobhāv anugatāv abhi vediyād abhi vāstamiyāt punarādheyam eva kurvīta
6.1.1	agnyupasthānaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
6.1.2	ādhānavelāyāṃ patnī ca yajamānaś ca vratacāriṇau bhavata ā homāt
6.1.3	unnīyamāne yajamāno 'nucaṅkramyata ā homāt
6.1.4	unnīyamāne stheyam ity ekeṣām
6.1.5	vidyud asi vidya me pāpmānam ṛtāt satyam upaimi śraddhā mayīti hoṣyann apa upaspṛśet
6.1.6	vṛṣṭir asi vṛśca me pāpamānam ṛtāt satyam upāgām apsu śraddheti hutvā
6.1.7	evam eva sarveṣu yajñakratuṣu yakṣyamāṇaś ceṣṭvā cāpa upaspṛśati
6.1.8	uttarām āhutim anutthāya kavātir yaṅṅ ivāhavanīyam upatiṣṭhata upaprayanto adhvaram ity etābhiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ
6.1.9	mamāgne varco vihaveṣv astv iti caitābhiś catasṛbhir aparapakṣe
6.1.10	atha pūrvapakṣa ubhā vām indrāgnī āhuvadhyā ity etām apohyetarābhir upasthāyānyaṃ divo mātar iśvā jabhārety etayāntata upatiṣṭhate
6.1.11	saṃvatsare saṃvatsara āgnipāvamānībhir gārhapatyam upatiṣṭhate
6.1.12	agna āyūṃṣi pavasa ity etābhiḥ ṣaḍbhir āhavanīyam upatiṣṭhate
6.2.1	āyur agne 'sy āyur me dehīti pratipadya citrāvaso svasti te pāramaśīyeti sāyam upatiṣṭhate / arvāg vasosvasti te pāramaśīyeti prātaḥ prātar avanekena
6.2.2	triś citrāvasunopatiṣṭhate trir arvāgvasunā
6.2.3	āhavanīye samidha ādadhāty agneḥ samid asy abhiśastyā mā pāhīti prathamām / somasya samid asi paraspā ma edhīti dvitīyam / yamasya samid asi mṛtyor mā pāhīti tṛtīyam / indhānās tvā śataṃ himā iti caturthīm ādhāyopatiṣṭhate saṃ tvam agne sūryasya varcasāgathā ity anuvākaśeṣeṇa
6.2.4	mukhaṃ vimṛṣṭe vayaṃ soma vrate tava manas tanūṣu bibhrataḥ / prajāvanto aśīmahi // iti
6.2.5	goṣṭham upatiṣṭhate saṃ paśyāmi prajā aham iti pratipadya bahvīr me bhūyāstety antena
6.2.6	antarāgnī tiṣṭhan japatīty ekeṣām
6.2.7	saṃhitāsi viśvarūpīr iti vatsam abhimṛśya gārhapatyam upatiṣṭhata upa tvāgne divediva ity etābhiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ
6.3.1	goṣṭham upatiṣṭhata ūrjā vaḥ paśyāmy ūrjā mā paśyatet pratipadya mayi vo rāyaḥ śrayantām ity antena
6.3.2	vatsam abhimṛśatīty ekeṣām
6.3.3	āhavanīyam upatiṣṭhate tat savitur vareṇyam iti pratipadya bhettāraṃ bhaṅgur āvata ity antena
6.3.4	gārhapatyam upatiṣṭhate 'gne gṛhapata iti pratipadya śataṃ himā ity antena
6.3.5	putrasya nāma gṛhṇāti
6.3.6	vyākhyāto jātaputrakalpaś cājātaputrakalpaś ca
6.3.7	tata āhācchinno daivyas tantur mā manuṣyaś chedi / divyād dhāmno mā chitsi mā mānuṣād iti
6.3.8	agnīn upasamidhya jyotiṣe tantave tvety antarāgnī upaviśati
6.3.9	evam eva sāyam agnyupasthānenopatiṣṭhate
6.3.10	prātar avanekena prātaḥ
6.3.11	adhiśrita unnīyamāne vā hastāv avanenijīta yā avanejanapravādā ṛcaḥ
6.3.12	avaśiṣṭābhir āhavanīyam upatiṣṭhate
6.3.13	purastād agnīṣomīyāyā vihavyasya catasra uttarā ṛco japed āgneyasya ca dve yājyānuvākye
6.3.14	vyāhṛtībhir agnyupasthānam eke samāmananti
6.4.1	bhartuṃ vā śakeyam ity eke
6.4.2	bhartuṃ vā śakeyam / śraddhā me mā vyagād ity eke
6.4.3	vātsapreṇety eke
6.4.4	māhitreṇa tṛcenety eke mahi trīṇām avo 'stu dyukṣaṃ mitrasyāryamṇaḥ / durādharṣaṃ varuṇasya // na hi teṣām amā cana nādhvasu vāraṇeṣv ā / īśe ripur adhaśaṃsaḥ // te hi putrāso aditeś chardir yacchanty ajasram / pra dāśuṣe vāryāṇi // iti
6.4.5	evaṃvihitam evāsya pravaso 'gnyupasthānaṃ bhavati
6.4.6	etāvan nānā yāni saṃspṛśya karmāṇy adhvaryus tāni kuryāt
6.4.7	yajamānaḥ kāle tāṃ diśam abhimukho mantrān japet
6.4.8	agnīn samādhehīty āha pravasatham eṣyan
6.4.9	bhāsvato virājakramair upatiṣṭhate yathāgnyādheye
6.4.10	āhavanīye samidham ādadhāti mama nāma prathamaṃ jātaveda ity etayā
6.4.11	antaragnī tiṣṭhan japatīmān me mitrāvaruṇā gṛhān gopāyataṃ yuvam / avaniṣṭan avihrutān pūṣainān abhirakṣatv āsmākaṃ punar āgamāt // iti
6.5.1	vāgyato 'bhipravrajati mā pra gāma patho vayaṃ mā yajñād indra sominaḥ / māntaḥ sthuno arātayaḥ // ud asmāṃ uttarān nayāgne ghṛtenāhuta / rāyaspoṣeṇa saṃmṛja prajayā ca bahūn kṛdhi // iti
6.5.2	sakāśe 'gnīnāṃ vācaṃ yacchaty asakāśe visṛjate
6.5.3	vratacārī pravasati
6.5.4	ṛtuṃ pratyupatiṣṭhate
6.5.5	yady anupasthitāgniḥ pravasate tatraiva sann upatiṣṭhata ihaiva san tatra sato vo agnayaḥ prāṇena vācā manasā bibharmi / tiro mā santam āyur mā prahāsīt / jyotiṣā vo vaiśvānareṇopatiṣṭhe // iti
6.5.6	samidhaḥ kṛtvāgnīn abhyaiti viśvadānīm ābharanto 'nātureṇa manasā / agne mā te prativeśā riṣām // namas te astu mīḍhuṣe namas ta upasadvane / agne śumbhasva tanvaḥ saṃ mā rayyā sṛja // iti
6.5.7	asakāśe 'gnīnāṃ vācaṃ yacchati sakāśe visṛjate
6.5.8	agnīn samādhehīty āha pravasathād etya
6.5.9	bhāsvato virājakramair upatiṣṭhate yathāgnyādheye
6.5.10	ajūgupa iti mantraṃ saṃnamati
6.6.1	imān me mitrāvaruṇā gṛhān ajūguptaṃ yuvam / avinaṣṭān avihrutān pūṣainān abhyarākṣīd āsmākaṃ punar āgamāt // iti
6.6.2	āhavanīye samidha ādadhāty agneḥ samid asīti tisraḥ
6.6.3	ādhāyopatiṣṭhate mama nāma tava ca jātaveda ity etābhiś catasṛbhiḥ
6.6.4	proṣuṣa āhutiṃ juhoti mano jyotir juṣatām ity etayā
6.6.5	nārvāg daśamyai juhuyāt
6.6.6	atha yatra navāvarārdhyā rātrīr uṣitvā sagṛhaḥ prayāyāt tat sarvaṃ samavadhāya sarvāṇy anyāni śakaṭāni yuktāni bhavanti
6.6.7	athāgniṣṭhasya dakṣiṇo yukto bhavati savyo 'yuktaḥ
6.6.8	atha vāstoṣpatīyaṃ juhoti
6.6.9	vāstoṣpate prati jānīhy asmān ity etām anudrutyottarayā juhoti
6.6.10	na huta ādadhāti
6.6.11	avakṣāṇāni saṃprakṣāpya pṛthag araṇīṣv agnīn samāropayate yāvanto nityā dhāryante 'yaṃ te yonir ṛtviya ity ekaikam
6.6.12	api vā yā te agne yajñiyā tanūs tayehyārohety ātman samāropayate
6.6.13	mathiṣyan japaty upāvaroha jātaveda ity etām
6.6.14	yady anovāhaḥ syāt pūrvaṃ taṃ pravaheyur apa voddhareyuḥ
6.6.15	yad dhīyeta tan na tv evānuhareyur iti vijñāyate na tv evānuhareyur iti vijñāyate
6.7.1	agnihotraṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
6.7.2	uddharāhavanīyam ity eva sāyaṃ yajamānaḥ saṃpreṣyati / uddharāhavanīyam iti prātaḥ
6.7.3	dhṛṣṭir asi brahma yacchety upaveṣam ādāyādhvaryur brahmacārī kṣīrahotā vā gārhapatyam abhimantrayate sugārhapatya ity etayā
6.7.4	athainam udbodhayaty udbudhyasvāgne prati jāgṛhyenam iṣṭāpūrte saṃsṛjethām ayaṃ ca / asmin sadhasthe adhyuttarasmin viśve devā yajamānaś ca sīdata // iti
6.7.5	purā chāyāsaṃbhedād gārhapatyāj jvalantam āhavanīyam uddharati vācā tvā hotrā prāṇenodgātrā cakṣuṣādhvaryaṇā manasā brahmaṇā śrotreṇāgnīdhaitais tvā pañcabhir daivyair ṛtvigbhir uddharāmīti
6.7.6	uddhriyamāṇe yajamāno japati bhūr bhuvaḥ suvar om uddhriyamāṇa uddhara pāpmano mā yad avidvān yac ca vidvāṃścakāra / ahlā yad enaḥ kṛtam asti pāpaṃ sarvasmān moddhṛto muñca tasmāt // iti sāyam / rātriyā yad enaḥ kṛtam asti pāpaṃ sarvasmān moddhṛto muñca tasmād iti prātaḥ
6.7.7	āhavanīyāyatane 'gniṃ pratiṣṭāpayaty amṛtāhutim amṛtāyāṃ juhomy agniṃ pṛthivyām amṛtasya jityai / tayānantaṃ kāmam ahaṃ jayāni prajāpatir yaṃ prathamo jigāya // agnim agnau svāhā // iti sāyam / sūryam agnau svāheti prātaḥ
6.8.1	svayaṃ yajamāna edhānāhṛtyāgniṣu mahata idhmānabhyādadhāti yad agne yāni kāni caitābhiḥ pañcabhiḥ pratimantram
6.8.2	āhavanīye varṣiṣṭham
6.8.3	nityo gārhapatyo dhāryate
6.8.4	sāyaṃ prātar āhavanīyam uddhareyuḥ
6.8.5	api vā sāyam uddhṛta eva syād ā prātar agnihotrāt
6.8.6	nityo gataśriya āhavanīyo dhāryate
6.8.7	āyuṣkāmasya vā
6.8.8	aharaharan vāhāryapacanam āhareyur mantheyur vā
6.8.9	nityo vā dhāryate
6.8.10	nityai sabhyāvasathyau
6.8.11	agnīn parisam ūhati / agne samrāṭ śundhasvety āhavanīyam / agne vahne śundhasvety anvāhāryapacanam / agne gṛhapate śundhasveti gārhapatyam
6.8.12	evam eva hutvā parisamūhati
6.8.13	agnīn paristṛṇāti / gārhapatyam agne 'thānvāhāryapacanam athāhavanīyam
6.8.14	agnihotrapātrāṇi prakṣālya dvandvaṃ prayunakty uttareṇa gārhapatyam / khadiraṃ sruvaṃ vaikaṅkatīm agnihotrahavaṇīm upaveṣam āryakṛtām agnihotrashtālīm urdhvakapālām acakravartām
6.8.15	astam ita āditye 'bhidhāya dakṣiṇato 'gnihotryā vatsam upasṛjati
6.8.16	athaināṃ prācīṃ vodicīṃ vāvartya sthālyā dohanena ca duhanti
6.8.17	na śūdro duhyād ity ekam / kāmam eva na śūdro duhyād ity aparam
6.8.18	agnihotraṃ tv eva na śūdro duhyāt / tadd hi pavitraṃ nātyetīti vijñāyate
6.9.1	pūrvau duhyāj jyeṣṭhasya jyaiṣṭhaneyasya yo vā purodhākāmo yo vā gataśrīḥ syāt / aparau duhyāt kaniṣṭhasya kāniṣṭhineyasya yo vā bubhūṣed yo vānujāvaraḥ syāt
6.9.2	pūrvau pūrvaṃ duhyāj jyeṣṭhasya jyaiṣṭhineyasya / aparau pūrvaṃ duhyāt kaniṣṭhasya kāniṣṭhineyasyety ekeṣām
6.9.3	yathākāmī nitye dohanakalpe
6.9.4	na saṃmṛśati
6.9.5	dugdhāharati
6.9.6	apareṇāhavanīyaṃ dakṣiṇātikramyopaviśati yajamāno yajamānāyatane / patnī patnīloke
6.9.7	tad ānīmas tam ita āditye nakṣatraṃ dṛṣṭvā pradoṣe vā sāyam agnihotraṃ juhoti
6.9.8	vyuṣṭāyām uṣasi vā prātar agnihotram / upodayam udite samayāviṣite vā / yarhi vāk pravadet tarhi hotavyam ity ekeṣām
6.9.9	yad udite juhoty agniṣṭomaṃ tenāvarunddhe / yan madhyaṃdina ukthyaṃ tena / yad aparāhṇe ṣoḍaśinaṃ tena / yat pūrvarātre jaghanyaṃ tena rātriparyāyam āpnotīti vijñāyate
6.9.10	sa na manyeta sarveṣv eteṣu kāleṣu hotavyam iti / āpadi hutam ity eva pratīyāt
6.9.11	agnīn pariṣiñcati / gārhapatyam agne 'thānvāhāryapacanam athāhavanīyam
6.10.1	ṛtaṃ tvā pariṣiñcāmīti sāyam / satyaṃ tvartena pariṣiñcāmīti prātaḥ
6.10.2	athaikeṣām / ṛtasatyābhyāṃ tvā pariṣiñcāmīti sāyam / satyartābhyāṃ tvā pariṣiñcāmīti prātaḥ
6.10.3	evam eva hutvā pariṣiñcati
6.10.4	gārhapatyāt prakramya saṃtatāṃ prācīm udadhārāṃ srāvayaty āhavanīyād yajñasya saṃtatir asi yajñasya tvā saṃtatyai nayāmi saṃtatyai tvā yajñasyeti
6.10.5	dhṛṣṭir asi brahma yacchety upaveṣam ādāya gārhapatyād udīco 'ṅgārān nirūhati bhūtakṛṭaḥ sthāpoḍhaṃ janyaṃ bhayam iti
6.10.6	vyantān kṛtvā teṣv agnihotram adhiśrayatīḍāyāḥ padaṃ ghṛtavac carācaraṃ jātavedo havir idaṃ juṣasva / ye grāmyāḥ paśavo viśvarūpās teṣāṃ saptānām iha rantir astu // iti
6.10.7	athainaṃ tṛṇenābhijvalayann avekṣata udbhavaḥ sthod ahaṃ paśubhir indriyeṇa bhūyāsam iti
6.10.8	yadā samuddhantaṃ bhavaty amnaradhiśritaṃ vātha sruveṇādbhiḥ prajanayati haras te mā vinaiṣam iti
6.10.9	apratiṣekyaṃ syāt tejaskāmasya brahmavarcasakāmasyāthābhicaratastitīrṣamāṇasyātho yaḥ kāmayeta vīro ma ājāyeteti
6.10.10	tathaiva tṛṇenābhijvālya triḥ paryagni karoty antar itaṃ rakṣo 'ntaritā arātaya iti
6.10.11	śrapayitvā karṣann ivodag udvāsayati gharmo 'si rāyaspoṣavanirihorjaṃ dṛṃheti
6.10.12	subhūtakṛtaḥ stha pratyūḍhaṃ janyaṃ bhayam iti gārhapatye 'ṅārān apisṛjya sāvitreṇa sruvam agnihotrahavaṇīṃ cādāya gārhapatye niṣṭapati pratyuṣṭaṃ rakṣaḥ pratyuṣṭā arātaya iti
6.10.13	niṣṭapya saṃmṛśaty ariṣṭo yajamānaḥ patnī ceti
6.11.1	yajamānam āmantrayata om unneṣyāmi havyaṃ devebhyaḥ pāpmano yajamānam iti sāyam / om unneṣyāmi havyaṃ devebhyaḥ pāpmano yajamānam iti prātaḥ
6.11.2	havir devānām asi mṛtyor me 'bhayaṃ svasti me 'stvabhayaṃ me stv ity upāṃśūktvā yajamāna om unnaya havyaṃ devebhyaḥ pāpmano mām ity uccaiḥ pratigṛṇāti
6.11.3	yadi yajamāno nānuṣyāt svayam evādhvaryuḥ pratigṛṇīyāt
6.11.4	caturaḥ sruvān pūrṇānunnayaty anūco vā / agnaye ca tvā pṛthivyai connayāmīti prathamaṃ sruvam unnayati / adbhyaś ca tvauṣadhībyaś connayāmīti dvitīyam / vātāya ca tvāntarikṣāya connayāmīti tṛtīyam / sūryāya ca tvā dive connayāmīti caturtham
6.11.5	ā hotor na cābhimīlayet
6.11.6	hutvā mahadabhivīkṣeta
6.11.7	unnītam agnihotraṃ daśahotrābhimṛśya sruvaṃ ca sthālīṃ ca saṃmṛśati sajūr devaiḥ sāyaṃyāvabhiḥ sāyaṃyāvāno mā devāḥ svasti saṃpārayantv iti sāyam / sajūrdevaiḥ prātaryāvabhiḥ prātaryāvāṇo mā devāḥ svasti saṃpārayantv iti prātaḥ
6.11.8	yatron nayet tat sādayet pratarāṃ vā paśūn me yaccheti
6.11.9	prādeśamātrīṃ pālāśīṃ samidham ādāya samayārcir gārhapatyasyāharati
6.11.10	uddravan daśahotāraṃ vyācaṣṭe
6.12.1	uparīva haraty urvantarikṣaṃ vīhīti
6.12.2	svāhāgnaye vaiśvānarāyeti madhyadeśe niyacchati
6.12.3	vātāya tvety udgṛhyāpareṇāhavanīyaṃ barhiṣy upasādayaty āyur me yaccheti
6.12.4	madhye 'gneḥ samidham ādadhāty eṣā te agne samit tayā vardhasva cā ca pyāyasva / vardhatāṃ ca te yajñapatir ā ca pyāyatāṃ svāheti
6.12.5	ādiptāyāṃ samidhi juhoty agnir jyotir jyotir agniḥ svāheti sāyam / sūryo jyotir jyotiḥ sūryaḥ svāheti prātaḥ
6.12.6	api vāgnir jyotir jyotiḥ sūryaḥ svāheti sāyam / sūryo jyotir jyotir agniḥ svāheti prātaḥ
6.12.7	iṣe tvety avācīnāṃ sāyaṃ lepam avamārṣṭi / ūrje tvety ūrdhvaṃ prātaḥ
6.12.8	varco me yacchety upasādya barhiṣi lepaṃ nimārṣṭy oṣadhībyas tvauṣadhīr jinveti
6.12.9	gārhapatyaṃ pratīkṣate 'gne gṛhapate mā mā saṃtāpsīr ātmann amṛtām adhiṣi prajā jyotir iti
6.12.10	atihāya pūrvam āhutiṃ tūṣṇīm uttarāṃ samidhi juhoti / prajāpataye svāheti vā
6.12.11	bahu hutvā bhūyo nimārṣṭi
6.13.1	bhūyo bhakṣāyāvaśinaṣṭi
6.13.2	rudra mṛḍānār bhava mṛḍa dhūrta namas te mā mā hiṃsīr iti triḥ srucāgnim atimārjayati
6.13.3	udag uddiśati
6.13.4	tathaiva lepam avamṛjya prajāṃ me yacchety upasādya prācīnāvītī dakṣiṇataḥ sthaṇḍile lepaṃ nimārṣṭi pitṛbhyas tvā pitṝn jinveti
6.13.5	apa upaspṛśya dvir aṅgulyā prāśnāty aśabdaṃ kurvan pūṣāsīti prathamam
6.13.6	apa ācamya garbhebhyas tvā garbhān jinveti dvitīyam
6.13.7	na dato gamayati
6.13.8	barhiṣopayamyodaṅ paryāvṛtya prācīnadaṇḍayodīcīnadaṇḍayā vā srucācāmaty āgneyaṃ retaḥ prajananaṃ me astv iti sāyam / sauryaṃ retaḥ prajananaṃ me astv iti prātaḥ
6.13.9	upaniṣkramyāgnihotrahavaṇīṃ mārjayitvā barhiṣi lepaṃ nimārṣṭi
6.13.10	adbhiḥ srucaṃ pūrayitvā prāṅ ninayati sarpebhyas tvā sarpān jinveti prathamam / sarpān pipīlikān jinveti dvitīyam / sarpetarajanān jinveti tṛtīyam
6.13.11	pradakṣiṇam āvartate
6.13.12	na barhir anupraharaty āhavanīye
6.13.13	agnihotrahavaṇīṃ niṣṭapati pratyuṣṭaṃ rakṣaḥ pratyuṣṭā arātaya iti
6.13.14	tasyāṃ hastam avadadhāti
6.13.15	hastaṃ vā pratāpyāgnihotrahavaṇyodag uddiśati saptarṣibhyas tvā saptarṣīn jinveti
6.14.1	adbhiḥ srucaṃ pūrayitvāpareṇāhavanīyaṃ ninayati pṛthivyāṃ tvāgnau vaiśvānare 'mṛtaṃ juhomi svāheti
6.14.2	evam evāpareṇa gārhapatyaṃ ninayati
6.14.3	patnyā apyañjalāvānayati gṛhebhyas tvā gṛhān jinveti vigrāhaṃ kanīyo 'gre 'tha bhūyaḥ
6.14.4	yadi patnī nānuṣyāt pṛthivyām eva dvir ninayet
6.14.5	etasmād evāgnihotraśeṣād dviś catur vā sruveṇa gārhapatye juhoty agne gṛhapate pariṣadya juṣasva svāheti
6.14.6	annapate 'nnasya no dehīty ānvāhāryapacane
6.14.7	nāparayor homo vidyata ity aparam
6.14.8	hutvoparasaminddhe dīdihi dīdidāsi dīdāyety ekaikam
6.14.9	vyākhyātaṃ parisamūhanaṃ pariṣecanam iti
6.14.10	dvayoḥ payasā paśukāmasyāgnihotraṃ juhūyāt
6.14.11	pūrvam adhiśrityottaram ānayet
6.14.12	ājyena juhuyāt tejaskāmasya payasā paśukāmasya
6.14.13	payo nityavad eke samāmananti
6.14.14	dadhnendriyakāmasya yavāg vā grāmakāmasya taṇḍulair ojaskāmasya sāṃsena yaśaskāmasya somena brahmavarcasakāmasya
6.14.15	ghṛtena brahmavarcasakāmo dvādaśarātraṃ juhuyāt
6.14.16	ājyena juhvata eṣa eva kalpaḥ / etāvan nānā / apāṃ pratyasanakāle darbhataruṇābhyāṃ pratyasyet
6.14.17	atha yadi dadhnā taṇḍulaiḥ somena vā juhuyād yad anyad adhiśrayaṇāt pratiṣecanād iti sarvaṃ tat kriyate
6.14.18	evaṃvihitam agnihotraṃ yāvaj jīvaṃ juhuyād yāvaj jīvaṃ juhuyāt
6.15.1	āgrayaṇaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
6.15.2	vrīhīṇām agrapākasya yajate
6.15.3	saptadaśa sāmidhenyo bhavanti
6.15.4	āmāvāsyaṃ tantraṃ bhavati
6.15.5	tatraiṣo 'tyantapradeśaḥ / sarveṣv iṣṭipaśubandheṣu dārśapaurṇamāsikā dharmā anuyanti
6.15.6	trayeṇāpi nivartante siddhyā pratiṣedhena pratyāmnāyeneti
6.15.7	tad yatra prākṛṭasya yajñāṅgasya sthāne vaikṛtam āmanet tat tasya dharmān labheta / yathā śaramayaṃ barhir barhiṣaḥ śyāmākā vrīhīṇāṃ sthālī kapālasya caruḥ puroḍāśasyeti
6.15.8	tatra yathārtham ūho bhavati
6.15.9	sāmānyād vikāraḥ / yathaikadevatā āgneyasya / dvidevato bahudevata ity agnīṣomīyasyaindrāgnasya vā
6.15.10	anyatra prakṛtidevatābhyaḥ / yathaindraḥ puroḍāśaḥ saumyaś carur iti
6.15.11	svayam eva sthānaṃ prākṛtyaḥ pratīyuḥ
6.15.12	atha yatra prākṛtyai devatāyā anyadd havir āmaned yathā vaiṣṇavaṃ puroḍāśaṃ havir eva svadhrmaṃ syāt
6.15.13	yadīṣṭyā yadi paśunā yadi somena yajetāmāvāsyāyāṃ vaiva paurṇamāsyāṃ vā yajeta
6.15.14	tatra siddhaṃ dve parve
6.15.15	pūrvāsyāṃ parva nidhāyottarasyām iṣṭyā yajeta
6.15.16	athaikaparve saṃsthāpya parva sadyaskālam iṣṭiṃ nirvapati
6.15.17	samānatantre vā
6.16.1	vikṛtiś ca darśapūrṇamāsau ca
6.16.2	darśapūṇamāsayor vikṛteś ca saṃnipāte darśapūrṇamāsau balīyāṃsau
6.16.3	yāni tv iṣṭipaśubandhānāṃ pratyakṣaśrutāṃnātāni tatra balīyāṃsi
6.16.4	trayoviṃśatidārum idhmaṃ karoti
6.16.5	tatraiṣo 'tyantapradeśaḥ / sāmidhenīvivṛddhau kāṣṭhāni vivardheran pratihvasamānāsu yathāprakṛti
6.16.6	samānam ā pātrāṇāṃ prayojanāt
6.16.7	trīṇi śūrpāṇi prayunakti
6.16.8	trīṇy ulūkhalāny adhivartayati dve dṛṣadau
6.16.9	samānam ā śūrpasyādānāt
6.16.10	veṣāya va iti śūrpāṇy ādatte
6.16.11	samānam ā nirvapaṇāt
6.16.12	āgneyam aṣṭākapālaṃ purāṇānāṃ nirupyaindrāgnam ekādaśakapālaṃ navānāṃ nirvapati
6.16.13	dvādaśakapālaṃ āgnedraṃ vā
6.16.14	vaiśvadevaṃ carum / payasi śṛto bhavati
6.16.15	saumyaṃ śyāmākaṃ caruṃ dyāvāpṛthivyam ekakapālam
6.16.16	api vā navāny eva nirvapet / nāgneyam
6.16.17	tantraṃ pratyabhimarśanamantro bhavati
6.16.18	āgrayaṇaṃ nirupyaitā āhutīr juhoti śatāyudhāya śatavīryāyeti pañca
6.16.19	samānam ā kṛṣṇājinās tṛṇāt
6.16.20	ekasmin kṛṣṇājine trīṇy ulukhalāny adhivartayati dve dṛṣadau
6.16.21	samānam ā vapanāt
6.16.22	sarvāṇi havīṃṣy opya haviṣkṛtam āhvayati
6.16.23	sarvāṇy avahatya dṛṣadupale samāhanti
6.16.24	anupūrvaṃ sarvāṇi havīṃṣy udvapati niṣpunāti vivinakti
6.16.25	api vaikasminn evolūkhale pūrvāparam avahanyāt
6.16.26	tatrāvapanaprabhṛtayo vivecanāntā mantrā bījaṃbījam abhyāvarteran
6.17.1	ādita eva haviṣkṛtam āhvayati
6.17.2	sarvāṇy avahatya vācaṃ visṛjate
6.17.3	sarveṣām antatas tuṣān upavapati
6.17.4	ā tantrībhāvād ekaikaṃ bījam apavarjayet
6.17.5	api vā samānajātīyenānusamīyāt
6.17.6	eṣa evāta ūrdhvaṃ nānābījānāṃ kalpo bhavati
6.17.7	samanām ā haviṣām udvāsanāt
6.17.8	ekakapālam udvāsyājyenābhipūrayati
6.17.9	tasya vaiśvadevikenaikakapālena kalpo vyākhyātaḥ
6.17.10	etāvan nānā / nāviḥpṛṣṭaṃ karoti na māsanāmabhir abhijuhoti
6.17.11	samānam ā haviṣaṃ pradānāt
6.17.12	vaiśvadevaṃ hutam anumantrayate viśveṣāṃ devānām ahaṃ devayajyayā prāṇaiḥ sāyujyaṃ gameyam iti
6.17.13	dyāvāpṛthviyaṃ hutam anumantrayate dyāvāpṛthivyor ahaṃ devayajyayā bhūmānaṃ pratiṣṭhāṃ gameyam iti
6.17.14	evam eva sarvān vaiśvadevān dyāvāpṛthivyān ity anumantrayate
6.17.15	samānam ā prāśnāt
6.17.16	bhadrān naḥ śreyaḥ samanaiṣṭa devā iti vrīhīṇāṃ prāśnāti
6.17.17	agniḥ prathamaḥ prāśnātu sa hi veda yathā haviḥ / śivā astabhyam oṣadhīḥ kṛṇotu viśvacarṣaṇiḥ // iti śyāmākānam
6.17.18	sarve mantreṇa prāśnīyur ity ekam / yajamāna eva yajamānabhāgam ity aparam
6.17.19	ye prāg ekāṣṭakāyā vatsā jāyante teṣāṃ prathamajaṃ dakṣiṇāṃ dadāti
6.17.20	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
6.18.1	atha yadi nānātantraṃ śyāmākaṃ kuryāc chyāmākeṣu pakveṣu saumyaṃ śyāmākaṃ caruṃ nirvapet
6.18.2	tasyaiṣa eva kalpaḥ
6.18.3	etāvan nānā / vāso dakṣiṇāṃ dadāti
6.18.4	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
6.18.5	yavānām agrapākasya yajate
6.18.6	teṣāṃ vrīhibhir eva kalpo vyākhyātaḥ
6.18.7	etāvan nānā / etam u tyaṃ madhunā saṃyutaṃ yavaṃ sarasvatyā adhimanāvacarkruśuḥ / inda āsīt sīrapatiḥ śatakratuḥ kīnāśā āsan marutaḥ sudānavaḥ // iti yavānāṃ prāśnāti
6.18.8	ya ūrdhvam ekāṣṭakāyā vatsā jāyante teṣāṃ prathamajaṃ dakṣiṇāṃ dadāti
6.18.9	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
6.18.10	navair evāmāvāsyāṃ paurṇamāsīṃ vā yajeta
6.18.11	navair vāgnihotraṃ juhuyāt
6.18.12	agnihotrīṃ vā navānādayitvā tasyāḥ payasā sāyaṃ prātar juhuyāt
6.18.13	api vā gārhapatye catuḥśarāvam odanaṃ paktvāgrayaṇadevatābhyaḥ sviṣṭakṛc caturthībhyo hutvā brāhmaṇān bhojayet
6.18.14	haritayavaśamīdhāny aśākānām aniṣṭe 'pi yāthākāmī
6.18.15	dānaprasavāni mūlapalāśakāni
6.18.16	vrīhibhir iṣṭvā vrīhibhir eva yajetā yavebhyaḥ / yavair eva iṣṭvā yavair eva yajetā vrīhibhyaḥ / api vā vrīhibhir eva yajeta
6.18.17	evam eva sasyesasye yāvajjīvaṃ yajate yāvajjīvaṃ yajate
7.1.1	paśubandhena yakṣyamāṇaḥ ṣaḍḍhotāraṃ manasānudrutyāhavanīye sagrahaṃ juhoti
7.1.2	sruveṇa yūpāhutiṃ juhoty uru viṣṇo vikramasvety etayā
7.1.3	yat sthālyām ājyaṃ pariśiṣṭaṃ tac ca sruvaṃ cādhvaryur ādatte / yat takṣaṇaśastraṃ tat takṣā
7.1.4	yasyāṃ diśi yūpam eśiṣyanto bhavanti tāṃ diśaṃ yanti
7.1.5	ta ete yūpyā vṛkṣāḥ palāśaḥ khadiro rauhitaka iti
7.1.6	bailvaṃ brahmavarcasakāmaḥ kurvīta
7.1.7	sa nityakāmaḥ
7.1.8	anakṣasaṅgaṃ vṛścet
7.1.9	yaṃ kāmayetāpratiṣṭhitaḥ syād ity ārohaṃ tasmai vṛścet / yaṃ kāmayetāpaśuḥ syād ity aparṇaṃ tasmai śuṣkāgraṃ vṛścet / yaṃ kāmayeta paśumān syād iti bahuparṇaṃ tasmai bahuśākhaṃ vṛścet / pratiṣṭhitaṃ vṛścet pratiṣṭhākāmasyeti vijñāyate
7.1.10	yo dakṣiṇāvṛn na taṃ vṛścet / ya udaṅṅāvṛn na taṃ na ghūrṇam / ya ṛjur ūrdhvaśalko yasyarjoḥ sat īṣadagram upāvanataṃ taṃ vṛścet / yaḥ prāṅ vā pratyaṅ vodaṅ vopāvanatas tam
7.1.11	upaspṛśya japaty aty anyān agām iti
7.1.12	sruveṇājyam ādāya paryaṇakti devas tvā savitā madhvānaktv iti
7.1.13	oṣadhe trayasvainam ity oṣadhim antardadhāti
7.1.14	svadhite mainaṃ hiṃsīr iti paraśunā hanti
7.1.15	yaḥ prathamaḥ śakalaḥ parapatet tam apayamya jānudaghne gulphadaghne vā vṛścati
7.2.1	athainaṃ prāñcaṃ pravāhayaty udañcaṃ vā divam agreṇa mā lekhīr antarikṣaṃ madhyena mā hiṃśīr iti
7.2.2	vanaspate śatavalśo virohety āvraścane juhoti
7.2.3	sahasravalśā vi vahaṃ ruhemety ātmānaṃ pratyabhimṛśati
7.2.4	anvagram adgān kalpayati yaṃ tvāyaṃ svadhitis tetijāna iti
7.2.5	etenaivāgrataḥ parivāsayati
7.2.6	ekaratniprbhṛtīni pramāṇāny ā trayastriṃśad aratner bhavanti
7.2.7	tryaratnir vaiva caturaratnir vā pālaśo nirūḍhapaśubandhayūpo 'athetare saumyasyādhvarasyety ekeṣām
7.2.8	athainaṃ nātisthūlaṃ nātyaṇum agre 'aṇīyāṃsam aṣṭāśriṃ karoti
7.2.9	mūlata uparam ataṣṭaṃ bhavati
7.2.10	agrataś caṣālaṃ pṛthamātram aṣṭāśriṃ madhye saṃnatam
7.2.11	yāvad uttamam aṅgulikāṇḍaṃ tāvad ūrdhvaṃ caṣālād yūpasyātirecayati / dvyaṅgulam ity ekeṣāṃ tryaṅgulam ity ekeṣām
7.2.12	avatakṣaṇānāṃ svaruṃ kṛtvāgnāvaiṣṇavam ekādaśakapālaṃ nirvapati
7.2.13	saptadaśa sāmidhenyo bhavanti
7.2.14	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
7.2.15	saiṣāgnyanvadhānasya sthānaṃ pratyeti
7.2.16	na paśviṣṭlyām agniṃ gṛhṇīyād ity aparam
7.2.17	tasyaṃ saṃsthitayāṃ śākhām āhṛtyāgreṇāhavanīyaṃ vediṃ karoti
7.2.18	ratheṣāmātrī prācī bhavati yugamātrī purastād akṣamātrī paścāt
7.2.19	yat prāguttarasmāt parigrāhāt tat kṛtvāpareṇa yūpāvaṭadeśaṃ śamyayottaravediṃ parimimīte
7.3.1	purastād udīcīnakumbāṃ śamyāṃ nidhāya sphyenābhyantaram udīcīṃ lekhāṃ likhati vittāyanī me 'asīti / evaṃdakṣinataḥ prāciṃ tiktāyanī me 'asīti / evaṃ paścād udīcīm avatān mā nāthitam iti / evam uttarataḥ prācīm avatān mā vyathitam iti
7.3.2	uttarasmād vedyaṃsād udañcaṃ prakramaṃ prakramya tathaiva śamyayā tūṣṇīṃ cātvālaṃ parimimīte
7.3.3	sāvitreṇābhrim ādāya parilikhati parilikhitaṃ rakṣaḥ parilikhitā arātaya iti
7.3.4	jānudaghnaṃ khatvā trivitastaṃ vā purīṣaṃ harati vider agnir iti
7.3.5	uttaravedyāṃ nivapati siṃhīr asi mahiṣīr asīti
7.3.6	evam eva dvitīyaṃ haraty evaṃ tṛtīyam / yo dvitīyasyām iti dvitīyaṃ harati / yas tṛtīyasyām iti tṛtīyam
7.3.7	tūṣṇīṃ caturthaṃ hṛtvā śamyāmātrīṃ prathayaty uru prathasvoru te yajñapatiḥ prathatām iti
7.3.8	dhruvāsīti saṃhatyādbhir avokṣati devebhyaḥ śundhasveti
7.3.9	yat prokṣaṇīnām ucchiṣyet tad dakṣiṇata uttaravedyām ekasphyāṃ niḥsāryopaninayed āpo ripraṃ nirvahateti
7.3.10	yaṃ dviṣyāt taṃ dhyāyet
7.3.11	sikatāḥ prakirati devebhyaḥ śumbhasveti
7.3.12	uttaravedyā antān kalpayati vibhrāḍ bṛhat pibatu somyaṃ madhvāyur dadhad yajñapatāv avihrutam / vātajūto yo abhirakṣatu tmanā prajāḥ piparti bahudhā virājati // iti
7.3.13	madhya uttaravedeḥ prādeśamatrīṃ catuḥsraktim uttaranābhiṃ kṛtvā
7.4.1	vedim uttaravediṃ ca saṃmṛśati catuḥśikhaṇḍe yuvatī kanīne ghṛtapratīke bhuvanasya madhye / tayor devā adhisaṃvasanta uttame nāka iha mādayantām // iti
7.4.2	athaināṃ pratidiśaṃ parikrāmaṃ prokṣatīndraghoṣas tvā vasubhiḥ purastāt pātv ity etair mantrair yathārūpam
7.4.3	tvaṣṭā tvā rūpair upariṣṭāt pātv ity upariṣṭāt
7.4.4	yat prokṣaṇīnām ucchiṣyeteti samānam
7.4.5	pūrvedyur agniṃ praṇayed ity ekaṃ, prokṣāntāṃ parivased ity aparam
7.4.6	āhavanīya idhmam ādīpya saṃpreṣyaty agnaye praṇīyamānāyānubrūhīti
7.4.7	trir anūktāyāṃ prathamāyām idhmam ādāya sikatā upayamanīḥ kṛtvodyatahomaṃ juhoti yat te pāvaka cakṛmā kaccid agaḥ pūrvaḥ sann aparo yad bhavāsi / ghṛtena tvaṃ tanuvo vardhayasva mā mā hiṃsīr adhigataṃ purastāt svāhā // iti
7.4.8	śeṣe hutvā prāñco 'abhipravrajanti
7.4.9	uparyagnau dhāryamāṇe pañcagṛhītenājyena hiraṇyam antardhāyākṣṇayottaravediṃ vyāghārayati / siṃhīr asi saptnasāhī svāheti dakṣiṇe 'aṃse / siṃhīr asi suprajāvaniḥ svāhety uttarasyāṃ śroṇyām / siṃhīr asi rāyaspoṣavaniḥ svāhety uttare 'aṃse / siṃhīr asy ādityavaniḥ svāheti dakṣiṇasyāṃ śroṇyām / siṃhīr asy āvaha devān deva
7.5.1	bhūtebhyas tveti srucam udgṛhyābhita uttaravediṃ pautudravān paridhīn paridadhati / viśvāyur asīti madhyamam / dhruvakṣid asīti dakṣiṇam / acyutakṣid asīty uttaram
7.5.2	nābhyāṃ saṃbhārān nivapati gulgulu sugandhitejanaṃ śvetāmūrṇāstukāṃ yā petvasyāntarā śṛṅge śvetasyācchinnastukasya / nācchinnastukasyety ekeṣām / agner bhasmāsi / agneḥ purīṣam asīti
7.5.3	etenaivottarata upayamanīr nivapati
7.5.4	yatrābhijānāti sīda hotaḥ sva u loka iti tat saṃbhāreṣv agniṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati yajña pratitiṣṭha sumatau suśevā ā tvā vasūni purudhā viśantu / dīrgham āyur yajamānāya kṛṇvann adhāmṛtena jaritāram aṅdhi // iti
7.5.5	nidhāyopasaminddhe yajñaḥ pratyaṣṭhāt // manuṣvat tvā nidhīmahi manuṣvat samidhīmahi / agne manuṣvad aṅgiro devān devāyate yajeti
7.5.6	atra saptavatyā pūrṇāhutiṃ hutvātimuktīr juhoty agnir yajñaṃ nayatu prajānan mainaṃ yajñahano vidan / devebhyo yajñaṃ prabrūtāt prapra yajñapatiṃ tira svāhā // vāyur ādityo yajño yajñaṃ nayatuprajānan mainaṃ yajñahano vidan / devebhyo yajñaṃ prabrūtāt prapra yajñapatiṃ tira svāhā // iti
7.5.7	atra pūrṇāhutim eke samāmananti
7.6.1	atra barhirādi karma pratipadyate yadi pūrvedyur agniṃ praṇayet / atha yadi prokṣāntāṃ parivaset tadānīm eva barhirādi karma pratipadyate
7.6.2	ikṣuśalāke vidhṛtī āśvavālaṃ prastaraṃ barhiṣy upasaṃnahyati
7.6.3	kārṣmaryamayān paridhīn idhme
7.6.4	trayoviṃśatidarum idhmaṃ karoti
7.6.5	samānam ā pātrāṇāṃ prayojanāt
7.6.6	vasāhomahavanīṃ dvitīyāṃ juhūṃ prayunakti pṛṣadājyadhānīṃ dvitīyām upabhṛtaṃ dve ājyasthālyau kumbhīṃ paśuśrapaṇīṃ kārṣmaryamayyau vapāśrapaṇyau dviśūlām ekaśūlāṃ ca hṛdayaśūlaṃ svaruṃ svadhitiṃ raśane plakṣaśākhām audumbaraṃ maitrāvaruṇadaṇḍaṃ yena cārthī bhavati
7.6.7	tatra ya upabhṛto dharmā ye ca dhruvāyāḥ pṛṣadājyadhānyām api kriyeran
7.6.8	ye sāṃnāyya ukahāyāḥ paśuśrapaṇyāṃ vapāśrapaṇyor hṛdayaśūle plakṣaśākhāyām iti kriyeran
7.6.9	sruvadharmāḥ svadhitau payodharmāḥ paśau
7.6.10	na praṇītāḥ praṇayati
7.6.11	agnīn paristīrya hastāv avanijya pātrāṇi prayujyoplaparājīṃ stīrtvā pavitre kṛtvā saṃpreṣyati yajamāna vācaṃ yaccheti
7.6.12	vāgyataḥ pātrāṇi saṃmṛśati
7.6.13	prokṣaṇīnām āvṛtā prokṣaṇīīḥ saṃskṛtya brahmāṇam āmantrya pātrāṇi prokṣya haviṣkṛtā vācaṃ visṛjya tata uttaraṃ parigrāhaṃ parigṛhṇāti
7.6.14	samānam ā saṃpraiṣāt
7.7.1	sruvasvadhitī ca srucaś ca saṃmṛḍḍḥi patnīṃ saṃnahyājyena dadhnā codehīti saṃpraiṣāntaṃ namati
7.7.2	samānam ājyanirvapaṇāt
7.7.3	ājyaṃ nirupya dvitīyasyām ājyasthālyāṃ dadhi nirvapati
7.7.4	tasyājyenaiva kalpo vyākhyāto 'anyatrādhiśrayaṇāt
7.7.5	samānam ājyānāṃ grahaṇāt
7.7.6	catur juhvāṃ gṛhṇāti catur upabhṛti
7.7.7	pañcagṛhītaṃ pṛṣadājyam / ājyena dadhi saṃsṛjya mahīnāṃ payo 'asīty etair mantraiḥ
7.7.8	yathāprakṛty eva dhruvāyāṃ gṛhṇāti
7.7.9	samānam ā srucāṃ sādanat
7.7.10	srucaḥ sādayitvāgreṇa dhruvāṃ vedaṃ sādayitvā sāvitreṇābhrim ādāyāgreṇāhavanīyaṃ yūpāvaṭaṃ parilikhaty ardham antarvedy ardhaṃ bahirvedi parilikhitaṃ raksaḥ parilikhitā arātaya iti
7.7.11	uparasaṃmitaṃ khātvā yūpaṃ prakṣālayati yat te śikvaḥ parāvadhīt takṣā hastena vāsyā / āpas tat sarvaṃ jīvalāḥ punantu śucayaḥ śucim // iti
7.7.12	yavamatībhiḥ prokṣaṇībhir yūpaṃ prokṣati / pṛthivyai tveti mūlam / antarikṣāya tveti madhyam / dive tvety agram
7.7.13	avaṭe śeṣam avanayati śundhataṃ lokaḥ pitṛṣadana iti
7.7.14	yavo 'si yavayāsmad dveṣa iti yavaṃ prāsyati
7.7.15	barhir avastṛṇāti pitṝṇāṃ sadanam asīti
7.7.16	svāveśo 'syagregā netṝṇām iti yūpaśakalaṃ prāsyābhijuhoti ghṛtena dyāvāpṛthivī ā pṛṇethāṃ svāheti
7.8.1	tataḥ saṃpreṣyati yūpāyājyamānāyānubrūhīti
7.8.2	devas tvā savitā madhvānaktv iti yūpasyagram anakti
7.8.3	aindram asīti sarvataś caṣālam aktvā pratimuñcati supippalābhyas tvauṣadhībhya ity amuto 'rvāk
7.8.4	yajamāno yūpaśakalenāntam anakti sarvataḥ parimṛśan
7.8.5	raśanāyāḥ kāle triḥ parimṛśati
7.8.6	āñjanaprabhṛti yūpaṃ yajamāno notsṛjaty ā parivyayaṇāt
7.8.7	tataḥ saṃpreṣyaty ucchrīyamāṇāyānubrūhīti
7.8.8	ucchrayaty uddivaṃ stabhānāntarikṣaṃ pṛṇeti
7.8.9	te te dhāmāny uśmasī gamadhya ity avaṭe 'vadadhāti
7.8.10	athainaṃ kalpayati viṣṇoḥ karmāṇi paśyateti dvābhyām
7.8.11	agrer ardhaṃ pratyupanataṃ yūpasya kūryād bahiṣṭān ninatam
7.8.12	anāvir uparaṃ minoti
7.8.13	taṃ pratyagnim agniṣṭāṃ mitvā pradakṣiṇaṃ purīṣeṇa paryūhati brahmavaniṃ tvā kṣatravanim iti
7.8.14	maitrāvaruṇadaṇḍena paridṛṃhati brahma dṛṃha kṣatraṃ dṛṃheti
7.8.15	unnambhaya pṛthivīm ity apo 'nupariṣicyedaṃ viṣṇur vi cakrama iti saraśanena pāṇinā yūpam unmārṣṭi
7.8.16	tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam iti yūpasyāgram udīkṣate
7.8.17	darbhamayyau raśane bhavataḥ / dviguṇā dvivyāyāmā triguṇā trivyāyāmā
7.8.18	tataḥ saṃpreṣyati
7.9.1	parivīyamāṇāyānubrūhīti
7.9.2	nābhidaghne madhyadeśe vā triguṇayā pradakṣiṇaṃ triḥ parivyayati parivīr asi pari tvā daivīr viśo vyayantām iti
7.9.3	uttaram uttaraṃ guṇam uttamaṃ karoti
7.9.4	upānte raśanāṃ vyatiṣajyāntaṃ praveṣṭayati
7.9.5	samāvantau kṛtvāṇimati sthavimat pravayati divaḥ sūnur asīti
7.9.6	svarum ādāya madhyame raśanāguṇe 'vagūhaty uttame sarveṣu vāntarikṣasya tvā sānāv ava gūhāmīti
7.9.7	athainaṃ paśuṃ snāpayanti anaṅgahīnam apannadantam ajaṃ lohaṃ tṛparaṃ dvirūpaṃ pīvānam
7.9.8	iṣe tveti barhiṣī ādatte
7.9.9	upavīr asīti plakṣaśākhām
7.9.10	yā bahuparṇā bahuśākhā tayopākuryāt paśukāmasya
7.9.11	agreṇa yūpaṃ purastāt pratyañcaṃ śākhayā barhirbhyāṃ paśum upākaroti / prajāpater jayāmānā iti dvābhyām / upo devān daivīr viśa iti pratipadya revatī ramadhvam indrāgnibhyāṃ tvā juṣṭam upākaromīty antena
7.9.12	agner janitram asīty adhimanthanaśakalaṃ nidadhāti / vṛṣaṇau stha iti prāñcau darbhau
7.9.13	urvaśy asīty adharāraṇim ādatte / purūravā ity uttarāraṇim
7.9.14	ghṛtenākte vṛṣaṇaṃ dadhāthām ity ājyasthālyā bile 'nakti
7.9.15	āyur asīty araṇī samavadhāya saṃpreṣyati
7.10.1	agnaye mathyamānāyānubrūhīti
7.10.2	trir anūktāyāṃ prathamāyāṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ trir manthati gāyatraṃ chando 'nu pra jāyasvety etair mantraiḥ
7.10.3	jāta āha jātāyānubrūhīti
7.10.4	prahariṣyan prahriyamāṇāyānubrūhīti
7.10.5	yatrābhijānāti pra devaṃ devavītaya iti tad agreṇottaraṃ paridhim anupraharati saṃdhinā vā bhavataṃ naḥ samasanāv iti
7.10.6	sruveṇājyam ādāyābhijuhoty agnāv agniś carati praviṣṭa ity etayā
7.10.7	sāvitreṇa raśanām ādāya paśoḥ pāśena dakṣiṇam ardhaśīrṣam abhidadhāty ṛtasya tvā devahaviḥ pāśenārama iti
7.10.8	athainaṃ purastāt pratyañcaṃ yūpe niyunakti dharṣā mānuṣān indrāgnibhyāṃ tvā juṣṭaṃ niyunajmīti
7.10.9	ye 'rvācīnam ekādaśinyāḥ paśava ālabhyante tān uttarato yūpasya niyunakti dakṣiṇata ekādaśinān
7.10.10	athainam upariṣṭāt prokṣaty adbhyas tvauṣadhībhya indrāgnibhyāṃ tvā juṣṭaṃ prokṣāmīti
7.10.11	pāyayaty apāṃ perur asīti
7.10.12	adhastād upokṣati svāttaṃ cit sadevaṃ havyam āpo devīḥ svadatainam iti
7.11.1	tataḥ saṃpreṣyaty agnaye samidhyamānāyānubrūhīti
7.11.2	samānam ā dhruvasamañjanāt
7.11.3	purastād dhruvāsamañjanāt paśuṃ samanakti / saṃ te prāṇo vāyunā gacchatām iti śirasi / saṃ yajatrair aṅgānīty aṃsayoḥ / saṃ yajñapatir āśiṣeti śroṇyoḥ
7.11.4	samānam ā pravarāt
7.11.5	prākṛtena varaṇena hotāraṃ vṛtvā punar āśrāvya maitrāvaruṇaṃ pravṛṇīte mitrāvaruṇau praśāstārau praśāstrād iti
7.11.6	samānam ā prayājebhyaḥ
7.11.7	juhūpabhṛtāv ādāyātyākramyāśrāvyāha samidbhyaḥ preṣyeti
7.11.8	vaṣaṭkṛte juhoti
7.11.9	āśrāvyāśrāvya preṣya preṣyeti evottarebhyaḥ saṃpreṣyati
7.11.10	caturthecaturtha aupabhṛtaṃ samānayate
7.11.11	sarvam aṣṭame
7.11.12	daśa preyājān iṣṭvaikādaśāyājyam avaśinaṣṭi
7.11.13	pratyākramya juhvā svarusvadhitī anakti / triḥ svaruṃ sakṛt svadhiter anyatarāṃ dhārām
7.11.14	tābhyāṃ paśuṃ samanakti ghṛtenāktau paśuṃ trāyethām iti
7.11.15	yāktā dhārā tayā paśuṃ samanakti
7.11.16	tayaiva haviṣaḥ śṛtasyāvadyatītarayā viśāsti
7.11.17	yāthākāmī viśasana ity aparam
7.12.1	punaḥ svarum avagūhati
7.12.2	śamitre svadhitiṃ prayacchann āhaiṣā te 'śriḥ prajñātāsad iti
7.12.3	tataḥ saṃpreṣyati paryagnaye kriyamāṇāyānubrūhīti
7.12.4	āhāvanīyād ulmukam ādāyāgnīdhraḥ paryagni karoti paśuṃ śāmitradeśaṃ cātvālaṃ yūpam āhavanīyam ājyānīti
7.12.5	paśum eva paryagni karotīty ekeṣām
7.12.6	paryagnau kriyamāṇe 'pāvyāni juhoti prajānantaḥ prati gṛhṇāti pūrva iti pañca
7.12.7	triḥ parītya nidhāyolmukaṃ triḥ punaḥ pratiparyeti
7.12.8	yupāt paśuṃ pramucya vapāśrapaṇībhyām anvārabhete adhvaryur yajamānaś ca
7.12.9	anvārabhyāśrāvya saṃpreṣyaty upapreṣya hotar havyā devebhya iti
7.12.10	yatrābhijānāti prāsmā agniṃ bharateti tad āhavanīyād ulmukam ādāyāgnidhraḥ pūrvaḥ pratipadyate
7.12.11	uttareṇa cātvālotkarāv udañcaṃ paśuṃ nayanti revatīr yajñapatiṃ priyadhā viśateti
7.12.12	nānā prāṇo yajamānasya paśunety adhvaryur yajamānam abhimantrayate
7.12.13	uttarata āgnīdhra ulmukaṃ nimṛdgāti
7.12.14	sa śāmitro bhavati
7.12.15	aparasmād gārhapatyād āharen nimanthyaṃ vā kuryāt
7.12.16	yābhyāṃ barhirbhyāṃ paśum upākaroti tayor anyatarad ācchyānārthaṃ nidhāya
7.13.1	dakṣiṇena śāmitram anyatarad upāsyati samasya tanuva bhaveti
7.13.2	tasmin paśuṃ pratyañcam udīcīnapādaṃ saṃjñapayanti
7.13.3	amāyuṃ kṛṇvantaṃ saṃjñapayatety uktvā parāḥ āvartate 'dhvaryuḥ paśoḥ saṃjñapyamānāt
7.13.4	pṛṣad ājyam avekṣamāṇāv āsate adhvaryur yajamānaś ceha prajā viśvarūpā ramantām asmin yajñe viśvabhṛto janitrīḥ / agniṃ kulāyam abhisaṃvasānā asmāṃ avantu payasā ghṛtena // yāsām ūdhaś caturbilaṃ madhoḥ pūrṇaṃ ghṛtasya ca / tā naḥ payasvatīḥ santv asmin goṣṭhe vayovṛdhiḥ // iti
7.13.5	saṃjñapte saṃjñaptahomaṃ juhoti yat paśur māyum akṛteti
7.13.6	paśoḥ pāśaṃ pramuñcati śamitar upetaneti
7.13.7	ekaśūlayā pāśa upatṛdya cātvāle 'pāsyaty utkare vāditiḥ pāśaṃ pra mumoktv iti

7.13.11	cātvāle patny apo 'vamṛśaty apo devīḥ śuddhā yuva iti
7.14.1	samutkramya sahapatnīkāś cātvāle mārjayante śuddhā vayaṃ pariviṣṭāḥ pariveṣṭāro vo bhūyāsmeti
7.14.2	patnī paśoḥ prāṇān āpyāyāyaty adhvaryur abhiṣiñcati
7.14.3	adhvaryur āpyāyayati patny abhiṣiñcatīty ekeṣām
7.14.4	vāk ta ā pyāyatām / prāṇas ta ā pyāyatām ity etair mantrair yathārūpam
7.14.5	yā te prāṇāñchug jagāmeti grīvāsu ninayati
7.14.6	yat te krūraṃ yadāsthitam iti samastaṃ paśum āpyāyayati
7.14.7	nābhis ta ā pyāyatām iti nābhim / pāyus ta ā pyāyatām iti pāyum / śuddhāś caritrā iti pādān
7.14.8	śam adbhyaḥ śam oṣadhībhyety avaśiṣṭā anupṛṣṭhaṃ ninīya dakṣiṇena nābhiṃ prāg agraṃ barhir nidadhāty oṣadhe trāyasvainam iti

7.14.18	urvantarikṣam anvihīty abhipravrajya
7.15.1	śāmitre vapāṃ pratitapati pratyuṣṭaṃ rakṣaḥ pratyuṣṭā arātaya iti
7.15.2	punar ulmukam ādāyāgnīdhraḥ pūrvaḥ pratipadyate

7.15.6	antareṇa cātvālotkarāv antareṇa yūpaṃ cāhavanīyaṃ ca vapām atyāhṛtya dakṣiṇata udaṅṅ āsinaḥ pratiprasthātāhavanīye vapāṃ śrapayati
7.15.7	adhastād vapāyā barhiṣo 'gram apāsyati vāyo vīhi stokānām iti

7.15.12	vaṣaṭkṛte juhoti

7.15.14	tata ājyabhāgābhyāṃ pracarati yady ājyabhāgau juhoti
7.15.15	tataḥ pūrvaṃ parivapyaṃ juhoti svāha devebhya iti
7.15.16	tataḥ saṃpreṣyati
7.16.1	indrāgnibhyāṃ chāgasya vapāyā medaso 'nubrūhīti
7.16.2	juhvām upastīrya hiraṇyaśakalam avadhāya sarvāṃ vapām avadyati
7.16.3	upariṣṭādd hiraṇyaśakalaṃ nidhāyābhighārayati
7.16.4	mā pajñāvattā bhavati
7.16.5	yady api caturavattī yajamānaḥ pañcāvattaiva vapā bhavati
7.16.6	yadi hiraṇyaṃ na syād ājyāt pratyavadyet
7.16.7	atyākramyāśrāvyāhendrāgnibhyāṃ chāgasya vapāyā medasaḥ preṣyeti
7.16.8	vaṣaṭkṛte juhoti jatāvedo vapayā gaccha devān ity etayā
7.16.9	tata uttaraṃ parivapyaṃ juhoti devebhyaḥ svāheti
7.16.10	vapāśrapaṇī praharati svāhordhvanabhasaṃ mārutaṃ gacchatam iti / prācīṃ dviśūlāṃ pratīcīm ekaśūlām
7.16.11	athaine saṃsrāveṇābhijuhoti
7.16.12	paśocchidram abhighārayati
7.16.13	samutkramya sahapatnīkāś cātvāle mārjayanta idam āpaḥ pravahatādyaṃ ca malaṃ ca yat / yac cābhidrudrohānṛtaṃ yac ca śepe abhīruṇam // nir mā muñcāmi śapathān nir mā varuṇād uta / nir mā yamasya paḍvīśāt sarvasmād devakilbiṣād athomanuṣyakilbiṣāt // āpo mā tasmād enaso viśvān muñcantv aṃhasaḥ // iti
7.16.14	hutāyāṃ vapāyāṃ varaṃ dadāti kanyām alaṃkṛtām anaḍvāhaṃ tisro vā vatsatarīḥ
7.17.1	paśupuroḍāśasya pātrāṇi prakṣālya prayunakti yāny auṣadhakāritāni bhavanti
7.17.2	pavitre kṛtvā saṃpreṣyati yajamāna vācaṃ yaccheti
7.17.3	vāg yataḥ pātrāṇi saṃmṛśati
7.17.4	vrīhim ayaṃ samānadevataṃ paśunā paśupuroḍāśam ekādaśakapālaṃ nirvapati dvādaśakapālaṃ vā
7.17.5	haviṣkṛtā vācaṃ visṛjya paśuṃ viśāsti
7.17.6	gudaṃ mā nirvleṣīḥ / vaniṣṭhuṃ mā nirvleṣīḥ / adhyuddhiṃ klomānaṃ plīhānaṃ purītataṃ medaḥ samavadhātavā iti saṃpreṣyati
7.17.7	kumbhyāṃ paśuṃ śrapayanti

7.17.10	śṛte paśau puroḍāśena pracarati

7.18.1	śṛtaṃ havī3ḥ śamita iti
7.18.2	śṛtam iti śamitā triḥ pratyāha

7.18.4	uttarataḥ parītya pṛṣad ājyena hṛdayam abhighārayati saṃ te manasā manaḥ saṃ prāṇena juṣṭaṃ devebhyaḥ / indrāgnibhyāṃ havyaṃ ghṛtavat svāheti
7.18.5	svāhoṣmaṇo 'vyathiṣyā ity uṣmāṇam udyantam abhimantrayate
7.18.6	yadi paśuṃ vimathnīrann evam evābhimantrayet
7.18.7	ājyena paśuṃ sāṃnāyyavad abhighārya tathodvāsyāntareṇa cātvālotkarāvantareṇa yūpaṃ cāhavanīyaṃ ca paśum atyāhṛtya dakṣiṇasyāṃ vediśroṇyāṃ pañcahotrā sādayati

7.19.1	api vā trayāṇām eva mukhyānām anupūrvam avadāya yathākāmam uttareṣām avadyati

7.23.1	upaniṣkramya hṛdayaśūlena caranti

8.1.10	samānam ā vatsānām apākaraṇāt
8.1.11	āpyāyadhvam aghniyā viśvebhyo devebhyo bhāgam iti gāḥ prasthāpayati
8.1.12	samānam ā barhiṣa āharaṇāt
8.1.13	prasūmayaṃ barhir bhavati
8.1.14	tat tredhā saṃnahyaikadhā punaḥ saṃnahyati
8.1.15	evaṃ trayoviṃśatidārum idhmaṃ karoti
8.1.16	samānam ā pātrāṇāṃ prayojanāt
8.1.17	pṛṣadājyadhānīṃ dvitīyām upabhṛtaṃ prayunakti dve ājyasthālyau tisraś carusthālīḥ pālāśaṃ vājinapātram
8.1.18	samānam ā nirvapaṇāt
8.1.19	āgneyam aṣṭākapālaṃ nirvapati saumyaṃ caruṃ sāvitraṃ dvādaśakapālaṃ sārasvataṃ caruṃ pauṣṇaṃ caruṃ mārutaṃ saptakapālaṃ vaiśvadevīm āmikṣāṃ dyāvāpṛthivyam ekakapālam iti
8.1.20	samānam ā phalīkaraṇāt
8.1.21	phalīkṛtānāṃ taṇḍulānāṃ vibhāgamantreṇa caravyānapoddharati
8.1.22	sahetarān pinaṣṭi
8.1.23	saṃyutānāṃ piṣṭānāṃ pauṣṇam apoddharati
8.2.1	samānam ā prātardohāt
8.2.2	tapte prātardohe sāyaṃdoham ānīya yadā kṛtāmikṣā bhavaty athaināṃ visrāvya vivājināṃ kṛtvā dvayoḥ pātrayovyuddhṛtya vājinasyaikadeśenopasicya prajñātaṃ vājinaśeṣaṃ nidadhāti
8.2.3	ādhiśritya haviṃṣy āpyebhyo ninīya tat uttaraṃ parigrāhaṃ parigṛhṇāti
8.2.4	samānam ā saṃpraiṣāt
8.2.5	ājyena dadhnā codehīti saṃpraiṣāntaṃ namati
8.2.6	samānam ājyānāṃ grahaṇāt
8.2.7	pāśukāny ājyāni gṛhṇāti
8.2.8	etāvan nānā
8.2.9	pṛṣadājyadhānyām aupabhṛtānāṃ mantrāṇāṃ dvābhyām ājyaṃ gṛhītvā mahīnāṃ payo 'sīti dvir dadhi gṛhṇāti
8.2.10	aupabhṛtānām ekenāntata ājyam
8.2.11	iti vai khalu yadi caitryāṃ yajeta
8.2.12	atha yadi phālgunyāṃ saṃsṛṣṭam eva gṛhṇīyād yathā paśubandhe
8.2.13	amānam ā haviṣām udvāsanāt
8.2.14	ekakapālam udvāsyājyenābhipūrayati
8.2.15	āviḥpṛṣṭhaṃ karoti
8.2.16	bhūr bhuvaḥ suva iti havīṃṣy āsādayati
8.2.17	utkare vājinam
8.2.18	saṃvatsare paryāgat etābhir evāsādayet
8.2.19	āsādya havīṃṣi nirmanthyasyāvṛtā nirmanthyena carati
8.2.20	saptadaśa sāmidhenyo bhavanti
8.2.21	samānam ā prayājebhyaḥ
8.2.22	nava prayājān yajati
8.2.23	caturthecaturthe aupabhṛtaṃ samānayate sarvam antataḥ
8.2.24	upabhṛtaḥ sthāne pṛṣadājyam abhighārayati
8.2.25	samānam ā haviṣāṃ pradānāt
8.2.26	upāṃśu sāvitraikakapālābhyāṃ pracarati
8.3.1	pauṣṇaṃ hutam anumantrayate pūṣṇo 'haṃ devayajyayā puṣṭimān paśumān bhūyāsam iti
8.3.2	evam eva sarvān pauṣṇān anumantrayate
8.3.3	āmikṣayā pracaryaikakapālaṃ barhiṣadaṃ kṛtvā juhvām upastīrya sarvam ekakapālam avadyati
8.3.4	atraivāśayam anuparyāsicyābhigharya srucā pratiṣṭhitaṃ juhoti
8.3.5	yadi hutaḥ paryāvarteta pratyādāyābhighārya punar juhuyāt
8.3.6	varaṃ dattvā srucā kalpayati na pāṇinety ekeṣām
8.3.7	athainaṃ caturbhir māsanāmabhir abhijuhoti madhave svāhā // mādhavāya svāhā // śukrāya svāhā // śucaye svāheti
8.3.8	saṃvatsarīṇāṃ svastim āśāsa itīḍāyā āśīṣu yajamāno japati
8.3.9	prathamajo vatso dakṣiṇā
8.3.10	pṛṣadājyena navānūyājān yajati
8.3.11	saṃvatsarīṇāṃ svastim āśāste divyaṃ dhāmāśāsta iti sūktavāke hotāśāste
8.3.12	prahṛtya paridhīn saṃpreṣyati vājibhyo 'nubrūhīti
8.3.13	juhvām upastīrya camase vā barhiṣi niṣiñcan vājinam ānayati
8.3.14	anabhighāryātyākramyāśrāvyāha vājino yajeti
8.3.15	vaṣaṭkṛte viṣicyamānāyā juhoti
8.3.16	anuvaṣaṭkṛte dvitīyam
8.4.1	ūrdhvajñur āsīno hotā yajaty anavānam
8.4.2	vājino hutvāvaśinaṣṭi
8.4.3	vājinodrekeṇa diśaḥ pratiyajati yathā paśubandhe
8.4.4	bhakṣaṃ taṃ samupahūya bhakṣayanti hotāgre 'thādhvaryur atha brahmāthāgnīdhro 'tha yajamānaḥ
8.4.5	samaśo vā vibhajya
8.4.6	sarva eva mithaḥ karmanām abhiḥ samupahvayeran
8.4.7	asāv upahvayasvety āmantraṇaḥ / upahūta iti prativacanaḥ
8.4.8	yan me retaḥ prasidhyate yan ma ājāyate punaḥ / yad vā me pratitiṣṭhati tena mām amṛtaṃ kuru tena suprajasaṃ kuru // tasya te vājipītasyopahūtasyopahūto bhakṣyāmīti
8.4.9	samānam ā samiṣṭayajuṣaḥ
8.4.10	pāśukāni samiṣṭayajūṃṣi juhoti
8.4.11	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
8.4.12	treṇyā śalalyā vinīya lauhena kṣuraṇaudumbareṇa śmaśrūṇi vāpayitvopapakṣau ni keśān vartayata ṛtam eva parmeṣṭyṛtaṃ nātyeti kiṃ caneti
8.4.13	evam evottareṇottareṇa mantreṇottareṣu parvasu nivartayate
8.4.14	caturo māsān na māṃsam aśnāti na striyam upaiti noparyāste jugupsate 'nṛtāt prāṅ śete 'madhv aśnāti
8.4.15	madhvaśanaḥ syād ity ekam / vyañjanārtham ity aparam
8.4.16	ṛtviye tu jāyām upeyād ity ekeṣām
8.4.17	evam eva sarveṣu cāturmāsyāntarāleṣu vrataṃ carati
8.5.1	tataś caturṣu māseṣu varuṇapraghāsair yajati
8.5.2	teṣāṃ vaiśvadevena kalpo vyākhyātaḥ
8.5.3	vikārān anukramiṣyāmaḥ
8.5.4	samānam ā vatsānām apākaraṇāt
8.5.5	mārutyā āmikṣāyai pratiprasthātā vatsān apākaroti
8.5.6	vāruṇyā adhvaryuḥ
8.5.7	agreṇāhavanīyaṃ dve vedī kurutaḥ / uttarām adhvaryur dakṣiṇāṃ pratiprasthātā
8.5.8	same prācī bhavataḥ / pṛthamātreṇa prādeśamātreṇa vāsaṃbhinne
8.5.9	yad evādhvaryuḥ karoti tat pratiprasthātā karoti
8.5.10	agreṇāpareṇa vottarāṃ vediṃ pratiprasthātā stambayajur harati
8.5.11	etenaivāta ūrdhvaṃ saṃcarate
8.5.12	samāna utkaro bhavati samāna āgnīdhraḥ samāno hotā samāno brahmā
8.5.13	tatraiṣo 'tyantapradeśo yāny uttarasyāṃ karmāṇy adhvaryus tāni kuryād dakṣiṇasyāṃ pratiprasthātā
8.5.14	athaine anusaṃbhinatti
8.5.15	dakṣiṇāyai veder uttarasyāḥ śroṇer upakramya sphenollikhaty ottarasyā dakṣiṇādaṃsāt
8.5.16	yat prāg uttarasmāt parigrāhāt tat kṛtvottarasyāṃ vedyām uttaravedim upavapati na dakṣiṇasyām
8.5.17	ubhayatra saṃbhāranivapanaṃ bhavati
8.6.1	pūrvedyur agnī praṇayata ity ekam / adhiśritya havīṃṣīty aparam
8.6.2	samānam ā barhiṣa āharaṇāt
8.6.3	dve barhiṣī āharato dvāvidhmau
8.6.4	samānam ā pātrāṇāṃ prayojanāt
8.6.5	ubhau pātrāṇi prayuṅktaḥ
8.6.6	śamīmayyaḥ sruco bhavanti hiraṇyamayyo vā dakṣiṇasya vihārasya
8.6.7	samānam ā nirvapaṇāt
8.6.8	āgneyam aṣṭakapālam iti nityāni pañca saṃcarāṇi nirupyaindrāgnam ekādaśakapālaṃ nirvapati
8.6.9	tūṣṇīṃ karambhapātrebhyo yavān nirupya mantreṇa meṣapratikṛtibhyāṃ yavān nirvapataḥ
8.6.10	marudbhyaḥ pratiprasthātā varuṇāyādhvaryuḥ
8.6.11	kāyam ekakapālaṃ nirvapati
8.6.12	samānam ā phalīkaraṇāt
8.6.13	sarvāṃ stuṣānavabhṛthāya nidadhāti
8.6.14	mantreṇa meṣapratikṛtibhyāṃ yavebhyo bharjanārthe kapāle upadhattaḥ
8.6.15	tayor īṣad upataptā dhānāḥ kurutaḥ
8.6.16	āvapantāv adhiśrayaṇamantraṃ japataḥ
8.6.17	udvapantāv udvāsanamantram
8.6.18	bhṛṣṭā dhānā abhighāryodvāsayataḥ
8.6.19	kāla uvālaṃkurutaḥ
8.6.20	yatra kva ca haviṣyān bharjayed evam eva kuryāt
8.6.21	piṣṭānām āvṛtā dhānāḥ piṃṣṭaḥ
8.6.22	āmikṣāyā āvṛtāmikṣe kurutaḥ
8.6.23	vāruṇaniṣkāsaṃ prajñātaṃ nidadhāti
8.7.1	aindrāgnaparyantāni havīṃṣy adhiśrityāmapeṣāṇāṃ yavānām īṣad upataptānāṃ vā pratipūruṣaṃ patnī karambhapātrāṇi karoti yāvanto yajamānasya putrapautrā bhavanty ekam atiriktam
8.7.2	strībhyo 'pi pratikaroti
8.7.3	meṣapratikṛtī kurutaḥ
8.7.4	meṣam adhvaryur meṣīṃ pratiprasthātā
8.7.5	striyāḥ strivyañjanāni kurute puṃsaḥ puṃvyañjanāni
8.7.6	athaināv aneḍakībhir lomaśau kurutaḥ
8.7.7	yady aneḍakīrna vindeyātāṃ kuśorṇā eva niśleṣayataḥ
8.7.8	kumbhīpākyau vā bhavataḥ
8.7.9	kāyam ekakapālam adhiśritya havīṃṣy āpyebhyo ninīyāhavanīya idhmāvādīpya saṃpreṣyaty agnibhyāṃ praṇīyamānābhyām anubrūhīti
8.7.10	ye ke ca sādhāraṇāḥ saṃpraiṣā adhvaryur eva tān brūyāt
8.7.11	sahāgnī praṇayataḥ saha praṇītā harataḥ
8.7.12	uttarasminn evāgnau praṇītā āsādayataḥ
8.7.13	uttarasmin vrataṃ visṛjate
8.7.14	tata uttarau parigrāhau parigṛhṇītaḥ
8.7.15	samānam ā saṃpraiṣāt
8.7.16	yathādhikaraṇaṃ saṃpraiṣaṃ namati
8.7.17	samānam ājyānāṃ grahaṇāt
8.8.1	ubhau pāśukāny ājyāni gṛhṇītaḥ
8.8.2	etāvan nānā / pṛṣadājyadhanyor aupabhṛtānāṃ mantrāṇām ekenājyaṃ gṛhītvā mahīnāṃ payo 'sīti dvir dadhi gṛhṇītaḥ
8.8.3	aupabhṛtānāṃ dvābhyām antata ājyam
8.8.4	iti vai khalu yadi śrāvaṇyāṃ yajeta
8.8.5	atha yady āṣāḍhyāṃ saṃsṛṣṭam eva gṛhṇīyātāṃ yathā paśubandhe
8.8.6	samānam ā haviṣām udvāsanāt
8.8.7	aindrāgnaparyantāni havīṃṣy udvāsyāmikṣayor meṣapratikṛtī avadhattaḥ
8.8.8	mārutyāṃ meṣam avadadhāti vāruṇyāṃ meṣīm
8.8.9	tābhyāṃ paraḥśatāni praḥsahasrāṇi vā śamīparṇakarīrāṇy upavapataḥ
8.8.10	karambhapātreṣv āvapati
8.8.11	ekakapālasyāvṛtaikakapālam udvāsyottarasyāṃ vedyāṃ havīṃṣy āsādayati
8.8.12	dakṣiṇasyāṃ mārutīṃ karambhapātrāṇi ca
8.8.13	āmikṣayor meṣapratikṛtī vipariharataḥ
8.8.14	mārutyāṃ meṣīm avadadhāti vāruṇyāṃ meṣam
8.8.15	ubhau nirmanthyābhyāṃ carata ity ekam / adhvaryur ity aparam
8.9.1	tataḥ saṃpreṣyaty agnibhyāṃ samidhyamānābhyām anubrūhīti
8.9.2	evam eva saṃmārjane dvivat paiṣaṃ saṃnamati
8.9.3	saṃmṛṣṭa uttaro 'gnir bhavaty asaṃmṛṣṭo dakṣiṇaḥ
8.9.4	atha pratiprasthātā patnīṃ pṛcchati kati te jārā iti
8.9.5	yañ jāraṃ santaṃ na prabrūyāt priyaṃ jñātiṃ rundhyāt / asau me jāra iti nirdiśet / nirdiśyaivainaṃ varuṇapāśena grāhayatīti vijñāyate
8.9.6	yāvata ācaṣṭe tān varuṇo gṛhṇātv ity uktvā patnīm udānayati praghāyān havāmaha iti
8.9.7	eṣīke śūrpa upastīrya karambhapātrāṇy opyābhighārya śīrṣann adhinidhāya purastāt pratyaṅ tiṣṭhan dakṣiṇe 'gnau yajamānaḥ saha patnyā karambhapātrāṇi juhoti
8.9.8	yajāmanaḥ purvonuvākyām anvāha mo ṣu ṇa indreti
8.9.9	ubhau patnī ca yājyāṃ yad grāme yad araṇya iti
8.9.10	api vādhvaryur eva juhuyāt
8.9.11	anvārabheyātām itarau
8.9.12	akran karma karmakṛta iti viparāyantau japataḥ
8.9.13	tato dakṣiṇam agniṃ saṃmārṣṭi
8.9.14	adhvaryur eva pravaraṃ pravṛṇīte
8.9.15	ubhau navanava prayājān yajataḥ
8.9.16	ājyabhāgābhyāṃ pracarya
8.10.1	uparamati pratiprasthātā
8.10.2	adhvaryur havvīṃṣi prayacchati
8.10.3	aindrāgnena pracaryoparamaty adhvaryuḥ
8.10.4	mārutyā pratiprasthātā pracarati
8.10.5	pūrveṇāvadānena meṣīṃ sahāvadyaty uttareṇa saha śamīparṇakarīrāṇi
8.10.6	mārutyā pracaryoparamati pratiprasthātā
8.10.7	varuṇyādhvaryuḥ pracarati
8.10.8	pūrveṇāvadānena meṣaṃ sahāvadyaty uttareṇa saha śamīparṇakarīrāṇi
8.10.9	ekakapālasyāvṛtaikakapālaṃ hutvottaraiś caturbhir māsanāmabhir abhijuhoti nabhase svāhā // nabhasyāya svāhā // iṣāya svāhā // ūrjāya svāheti
8.10.10	pṛthak sviṣṭakṛṭe juhutaḥ / saheḍām avadyataḥ
8.10.11	parivatsarīṇāṃ svastim āśāsa itīḍāyā āśīṣu yajamāno japati
8.10.12	pravayā iva rṣabho dakṣiṇā
8.10.13	pṛṣad ājyena navānūyājān yajataḥ
8.10.14	parivatsarīṇāṃ svastim āśāste divyaṃ dhāmāśāsta iti sūktavāke hotāśāste
8.10.15	ubhau vājinena pracarataḥ
8.10.16	ā tvā viśantv indavaḥ // ā valgā dhamanīnāṃ rasena me rasaṃ pṛṇa / tasya te vājibhir bhakṣaṃ kṛtasyopahūtasyopahūto bhakṣayāmīti
8.11.1	dakṣiṇaṃ vājinaṃ bhakṣayanti
8.11.2	vājināṃ bhakṣo 'vatu vājo 'smān retaḥ siktam amṛtaṃ balāya / sa na indriyaṃ draviṇaṃ dadhātu mā riṣām vājinaṃ bhakṣayantaḥ // tasya ta upahūtasyopahūto bhakṣayāmīty uttaram
8.11.3	ubhau kastambhyāṃ srucau sādayataḥ
8.11.4	adhvaryur eva patnīḥ saṃyājayati
8.11.5	ubhau pāśukāni samiṣṭayajūṃṣi juhutaḥ
8.11.6	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
8.11.7	tuṣaiś ca vāruṇyā niṣkāsena cāvabhṛtam avayanti
8.11.8	tatra kṛtsno 'vabhṛthaḥ kriyate yad anyat sāmno 'dhvamantrād ṛjīṣabhakṣād iti
8.11.9	tuṣā ṛjīṣasya sthānaṃ pratiyanti
8.11.10	niṣkāsa ekakapālasya
8.11.11	api vā vāruṇam ekakapālaṃ nirvapet
8.11.12	tasya niṣkāsena samavadāya pracaret
8.11.13	api vā na saumiko 'vabhṛtaḥ
8.11.14	tūṣṇīm eva tuṣaniṣkāsam apsūpavapet
8.11.15	athānye vāsasī paridhāyodetaḥ
8.11.16	kāmam ete vāsasī yasmai kāmayeyātāṃ tasmai dadyātām
8.11.17	pratyetya nirvartayate
8.11.18	vyākhyātaṃ nivartanaṃ tathā vratacaryā
8.12.1	tataś caturṣu māseṣu vyahaṃ sākamedhair yajate
8.12.2	agnaye 'nīkavate puroḍāśam aṣṭākapālaṃ nirvapati sākaṃ sūryeṇodyatā
8.12.3	sākaṃ raśmibhiḥ pracarantīty ekeṣām
8.12.4	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
8.12.5	marudbhyaḥ sāṃtapanebhyo madhyaṃdine carum
8.12.6	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
8.12.7	gṛhamedhīyasya tantraṃ prakramayati
8.12.8	samānam ā vatsānām apākaraṇāt
8.12.9	ayajuṣkeṇa gṛhamedhīyāya sarvān vatsān apākaroti
8.12.10	vedaṃ kṛtvā vediṃ karoti
8.12.11	nātredhmabarhir bhavati / na praṇītāḥ praṇayati
8.12.12	agnīn paristīrya hastāv avanijya pātrāṇi prayujyolaparājīḥ stīrtvā pavitre kṛtvā saṃpreṣyati yajamāna vācaṃ yaccheti
8.12.13	vāgyataḥ pātrāṇi saṃmṛśati
8.12.14	marudbhyo gṛhamedhibhyaḥ sarvāsāṃ dugdhe sāyaṃ carum
8.12.15	pavitre sarvā gā dohayitvānutpūte payasy anutpūya taṇḍulān āvapati
8.12.16	gārhapatye vānvāhāryapacane vā prativeśam odanaṃ pacati
8.12.17	tata uttaraṃ parigrāhaṃ parigṛhṇāti
8.12.18	samānam ā saṃpraiṣāt
8.12.19	nātredhmāgarhiḥ pracodayati
8.12.20	samānam ājyānāṃ grahaṇāt
8.12.21	dhruvāyām eva gṛhṇāti
8.12.22	prokṣaṇīr abhimantrya brahmāṇam āmantrya vediṃ prokṣya prokṣaṇyavaśeṣaṃ ninīyāgnim abhimantryāntarvedi dhruvāṃ sādayitvā sruvaṃ sādayati / eṣāsadad iti mantraṃ saṃnamati
8.12.23	viṣṇv asi vaiṣṇavaṃ dhāmāsi prājāpatyam ity ājyam abhimantrayate

8.13.1	athaitaṃ carum udvāsya tasya śaraṃ prajñātaṃ nidhāya trīn odanān uddharati

8.17.1	phalīkṛtāṃs taṇḍulāṃs traidhaṃ vibhajyānvāhāryapacane bharjanārthaṃ kapālam upadhāya tasmiṃs tṛtīyaṃ taṇḍulānāṃ dhānā bharjanti
8.17.2	vyākhyātaḥ saṃskāraḥ

8.17.4	samānam ā kapālopadhānāt
8.17.5	dakṣiṇārdhe gārhapatyasya ṣaṭ kapālāny upadhāyānvāhāryapacane dhānārthaṃ kapālam upadadhāti

8.17.11	śalākāsthaṃ karoti

8.17.14	tata uttaraṃ parigrāhaṃ parigṛhṇāti
