8.24.14	vyākhyātaṃ nivartanam
8.24.15	saṃtiṣṭhante cāturmāsyāni
8.25.1	kāmyāni cāturmāsyāni vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
8.25.2	vaiśvadevena paśukāmo yajeta
8.25.3	asminn asyartau bhūyiṣṭhaṃ payaḥ syād api vā yadāsya vasante bhūyiṣṭaṃ payaḥ syād atha vaiśvadevena yajeta
8.25.4	vaiśvadevenaiva paśukāmo yajeta netaraiḥ parvabhir ā yāvat sahasraṃ paśūn prāpnūyāt
8.25.5	sahasraṃ paśūn prāpyetaraiḥ parvabhir yathākālaṃ yajeta
8.25.6	śunāsīryeṇa grāmakāmo yajeta
8.25.7	varṣyam udakam anvavasāyaitenaiva prajākāmo yajeta paśukāmo yajetānnādyakāmo yajeta pratiṣṭhākāmo yajeteti vijñāyate
8.25.8	pañcasāṃvatsarikāṇi vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
8.25.9	phālgunyāṃ prayujya trīn ṛtūn saṃvatsarān iṣṭvā māsaṃ viramet
8.25.10	caitryāṃ prayujya dvāv ṛtū saṃvatsarāv iṣṭvā viramet
8.25.11	tantraṃ vaiśvānarapārjanye bhavatas tantraṃ pañcahotā
8.25.12	cāturmāsyair iṣṭvā somena yajeta
8.25.13	somasya vā etad rūpaṃ yac cāturmāsyānīti vijñāyate
8.25.14	somāśaktau paśunā yajeta / paśunāśaktau punaḥ prayogaś cāturmāsyānām / sa triṣutriṣu saṃvatsareṣu māsam utsṛjed iti vijñāyate māsam utsṛjed iti vijñāyate
9.1.1	śrutilakṣaṇaṃ prāyaścittaṃ vidhyaparādhe vidhīyate
9.1.2	ekasmin doṣe śrūyamāṇāni prāyaścittāni samabhyuccīyerann arthāntaratvāt
9.1.3	japo homa ijyā ca
9.1.4	doṣanirghātārthāni bhavanti
9.1.5	anantaraṃ doṣāt kartavyāni
9.1.6	nirhṛte doṣe punaḥ kṛtsnaṃ karma
9.1.7	tasya nāvacanāt punaḥ prayogaḥ
9.1.8	yady anvāhitāgniḥ prayāyāt tubhyaṃ tā aṅgirastama iti gārhapatye juhuyāt
9.1.9	pṛthag araṇīṣv agnīn samāropya prayāti
9.1.10	sa yatrāvasyati tad etām iṣṭiṃ saṃsthāpayati
9.1.11	yady anvāhitāgner āhavanīya udvāyed anvagnir uṣasām agram akhyad ity anyaṃ praṇīya bhūr ity upasthāyājyasya sruvaṃ pūrṇaṃ juhoti yo agniṃ devītaye haviṣmāṃ āvivāsati / tasmai pāvaka mṛḍaya svāhā // iti
9.1.12	tat etām āhutiṃ juhotīdaṃ viṣṇur vi cakrama iti
9.1.13	manasā vratopāyanīyaṃ yajur japet
9.1.14	yaḥ kaścanānugacched etad eva praṇayanavarjam
9.1.15	manthed gārhapatyam
9.1.16	yathāprakṛty anvāhāryapacanam
9.1.17	yady āhitāgner agnir apakṣāyed ā śamyāparābhāt taṃ saṃbhared idaṃ ta ekaṃ para u ta ekaṃ tṛtīyena jyotiṣā saṃviśasva / saṃveśanas tanuvai cārur edhi priye devānāṃ parame janitre // iti
9.2.1	yadi parastarām apakṣayed anuprayāyāvasyet
9.2.2	tato 'gnaye pathikṛte puroḍāśam aṣṭākapālaṃ nirvapet
9.2.3	patho 'ntikād barhir āharet
9.2.4	anaḍvān dakṣiṇā
9.2.5	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
9.2.6	yadi haviṣe vatsā apākṛtā dhayeyur vāyavyāṃ yavāgūṃ nirvapet
9.2.7	sā dohasya sthāne syād yatarasmā apākṛtā dhayeyuḥ
9.2.8	athottarasmai haviṣe vatsān apākṛtyopavaset
9.2.9	yadi sāyaṃ dugdhaṃ havir ārtim ārcched indrāya vrīhīn nirupyopavaset
9.2.10	yat prātaḥ syāt tac chṛtaṃ kuryāt
9.2.11	athetara aindraḥ puroḍāśaḥ syāt
9.2.12	tasya prātardohena samavadāya pracaret
9.2.13	athottarasmai haviṣe vatsān apākṛtyopavaset
9.2.14	etad eva prātardoha ārtigate prāyaścittam
9.2.15	etāvan nānā / sāyaṃdohenātra samavadāya pracaret
9.2.16	yasyobhau dohāv ārtim ārcheyātām aindraṃ pañcaśarāvam odanaṃ nirvapet
9.2.17	tasyobhe devate yajetāgniṃ cendraṃ cety āśmarathyaḥ / athālekhanaḥ / indram evaitasya yajeta
9.2.18	nitya āgneyo 'ṣṭākapālaḥ
9.2.19	athottarasmai haviṣe vatsān apākṛtyopavaset
9.2.20	yasya vratye 'han patny anālambhukā syāt tām aparudhya yajeta
9.2.21	udak śulbaṃ stṛṇīyāt
9.3.1	tām iṣṭvopahvayetāmūham asmi sā tvaṃ dyaur aham pṛthivī sāmāham ṛk tvam / tāv ehi saṃbhavāvahai reto dadhāvahai puṃse putrāya vettavai rāyaspoṣāya suprajās tvāya suvīryāya // iti
9.3.2	yadi sāṃnāyyam agnihotraṃ vā viṣyandeta prājāpatyaya rcā valmīkavapāyām avanīya bhūr ity upatiṣṭhate
9.3.3	tato 'nyāṃ dugdhvā punar juhuyād yady agnihotram
9.3.4	yady u vai sāṃnāyyam uttarasmai haviṣe vatsān apākṛtyopavaset
9.3.5	yadi sāṃnāyye 'gnihotre vā kīṭo 'vapadyeta madhyamena parṇena dyāvāpṛthivyayarcāntaḥ ninayet
9.3.6	tato 'nyāṃ dugdhvā punarjuhuyād yady agnihotram
9.3.7	yady u vai sāṃnāyyam uttarasmai haviṣe vatsān apākṛtyopavaset
9.3.8	yady uddrutam agnihotram avavarṣen mitro janān kalpayati prajānan mitro dādhāra pṛthivīm uta dyām / mitraḥ kṛṣṭīr animiṣābhicaṣṭe satyāya havyaṃ ghṛtavaj juhota // iti juhuyāt
9.3.9	tato 'nyāṃ dugdhvā punar juhuyāt
9.3.10	yadi pūrvasyām āhutyāṃ hutāyām uttarāhutiḥ skandet pūrvāṃ vottarayābhijuhuyād yatra vettha vanaspate devānāṃ guhyā nāmāni / tatra havyāni gāmaya // iti vānaspatyayarcā samidham ādhāya tūṣṇīm eva punar juhuyāt
9.3.11	tato 'nyāṃ dugdhvā punar juhuyāt
9.3.12	yadi pūrvasyām āhutyāṃ hutāyām āhavanīya udvāyed antame śakale hiraṇyaṃ nidhāyābhijuhuyād agnir dārau dārāv agnir agāt svāheti
9.4.1	yadi purā prayājebhyo bahiḥparidhyaṅgāraḥ skandet taṃ sruvasya budhnenābhinidadhyān mā tamo mā yajñas taman mā yajamānas tamat / namas te astv āyate namo rudra parāyate namo yatra niṣīdasi // adhvaryuṃ mā hiṃsīir yajamānaṃ mā hīṃsīr iti yadi purastāt / bramāṇaṃ mā hiṃsīr yajamānaṃ mā hīṃsīr iti yadi dakṣiṇataḥ / hotāraṃ mā hīṃsīḥ pa
9.4.2	athainam anupraharati sahasraśṛṅgo vṛṣabho jātavedāḥ stomapṛṣṭho ghṛtavān supratīkaḥ / mā no hāsīn methito nettvā jahāma gopoṣaṃ no vīrapoṣaṃ ca yaccha // iti
9.4.3	prahṛtyābhijuhuyād ity ekeṣām
9.4.4	yena skandet tena praharet
9.4.5	yady āhitāgner agnir mathyamāno na jāyetāgniṃ naro dīdhitibhir araṇyor hastacyutī janayanta praśastam / dūredṛśaṃ gṛhapatim atharyum // ity abhimantrya yatrānyaṃ paśyet tata āhṛtya vihṛtya juhuyāt
9.4.6	tato 'tvaramāṇaḥ punarmanthet
9.4.7	yady anyaṃ na vinded ajāyai dakṣiṇe karṇe juhuyāt
9.4.8	ajasya tu tato nāśnīyāt
9.4.9	yady ajāṃ na vinded brāhmaṇasya dakṣiṇe haste juhuyāt
9.4.10	brāhmaṇaṃ tu vasatyai nāparundhyāt
9.4.11	yadi brāhmaṇaṃ na vinded darbhastambe juhuyāt
9.4.12	darbhāṃs tu nādhyāsīta
9.5.1	yadi darbhān na vinded apsu juhuyāt
9.5.2	āpas tu na paricakṣītemā bhojanīyā imā abhojanīyā ity āśmarathyaḥ / apy abhojanīyasyaitaṃ saṃvatsaraṃ parigṛhṇīyād evāpa ity ālekhanaḥ
9.5.3	adbhis tu na pādau prakṣālayītety ekeṣām
9.5.4	saṃvatsarād agnaye vratapataye puroḍāśam aṣṭākapālaṃ nirvapet
9.5.5	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
9.5.6	yady āhitāgner agnibhir agnayaḥ saṃsṛjyeran mitho vāgnaye vivicaye puroḍāśam aṣṭakapālaṃ nirvapet
9.5.7	tato vratapataye
9.5.8	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
9.5.9	yady āhitāgner agnir gṛhān dahed agnaye kṣāmavate puroḍāśam aṣṭakapālaṃ nirvapet
9.5.10	tato vratapataye
9.5.11	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
9.5.12	atha yady abhyādāhyena saṃsṛjyeran vivicaye nirupya śucaye nirvapet
9.5.13	tato vratapataye
9.5.14	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
9.5.15	atha yady vaidyutena saṃsṛjyerann agnaye 'psumate puroḍāśam aṣṭākapālaṃ nirvapet
9.5.16	tato vratapataye
9.5.17	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
9.5.18	atha yady śavāgninā sūtakāgninā vā saṃsṛjyerann agnaye saṃkusukāya puroḍāśam aṣṭākapālaṃ nirvapet
9.5.19	tato vratapataye
9.5.20	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
9.5.21	atha yady sarvāṇi saṃnipateyuḥ kṣāmavatīmante kuryāt
9.5.22	yady agnihotrasthālī sravet tām abhimantrayate garbhaṃ sravantam agadam akar agnir indras tvaṣṭā bṛhaspatiḥ / pṛthivyām avacuścotaitan nābhiprāpnoti nirṛtiṃ parācaiḥ // iti
9.5.23	skannam apo 'bhyavaharet
9.6.1	yady anadhiśritaṃ syād vaiṣṇavyānumantrayeta
9.6.2	yasya havirniruptaṃ purastāc candramā abhyudeti tredhā taṇḍulān vibhajet / ye madhyamāḥ syus tān agnaye dātre puroḍāśam aṣṭakapālaṃ kuryāt / ye sthāviṣṭhās tān indrāya pradātre dadhaṃś carum / ye 'ṇiṣṭhās tān viṣṇave śipiviṣṭāya śṛte carum
9.6.3	aniruptābhyudite katamābhyo devatābhyo nirvapet / prākṛtībhya ity āśmarathyo vaikṛtībhya ity alekhanaḥ
9.6.4	seyaṃ nāsaṃnayato vidyata ity ekam / vidyata ity aparam
9.6.5	agnaye pathikṛte puroḍāśam aṣṭākapālaṃ nirvaped yo darśapūrṇamāsayājī sannam āvāsyāṃ vā paurṇamāsīṃ vātipadayet
9.6.6	patho 'ntikād barhir āharet
9.6.7	anaḍvān dakṣiṇā
9.6.8	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
9.6.9	athaikeṣāṃ vijñāyate vi vā etasya yajñaś chidyate yasya yajñe pratata etām antareṣṭiṃ nirvapati / ya evāsāvāgneyo 'ṣṭākapālaḥ paurṇamāse yo 'māvāsyāyaṃ tam agnaye pathikṛṭe kuryāt / tenaiva punaḥ panthām avaiti na yajñaṃ vicchinatti
9.6.10	agnaye vratapataye puroḍāśam aṣṭākapālaṃ nirvaped yady āhitāgniḥ pravasan parvaṇi māṃsaṃ vāśnīyāt striyaṃ vopeyāt
9.6.11	vratabhṛta eke samāmananti
9.6.12	etām eva nirvaped yady āhitāgnir aśru kuryāt
9.6.13	yathā kathā ca kuryāt prāyaścittam eva syād ity āśmarathyaḥ / ārtijam eva kuryād ity ālekhanaḥ
9.7.1	yady agnihotry upasṛṣṭā niṣīdet tām utthāpayed udasthād devy aditir viśvarūpyāyur yajñapatāvadhāt / indrāya kṛṇvatī bhāgaṃ mitrāya varuṇāya ca // iti
9.7.2	tāṃ dugdhvā brāhmaṇāya dadyād yasyānnaṃ nādyāt
9.7.3	atha yadi spandetānyāṃ duhyāt
9.7.4	yadi duhyamānaṃ skanded yad adya dugdhaṃ pṛthivīm asakta yadoṣadhīr apy asaradyad āpaḥ / payo gṛheṣu payo aghniyāsu payo vatseṣu payo astu tan mayi // iti
9.7.5	athainad adbhir upasṛjati samudraṃ vaḥ pra hiṇomīty etayā
9.7.6	tad eva yādṛkkīdṛk ca hutvāthānyāṃ dugdhvā punar juhuyāt
9.7.7	yadi dugdhaṃ skanded yady adhiśritaṃ yadi viṣyandetābhiduhya juhuyād ity āśmarathyaḥ / tad eva yādṛkkīdṛk ca hutvāthānyāṃ dugdhvā punar juhuyād ity ālekhanaḥ
9.7.8	yady unnīyamānaṃ skanded yady unnītaṃ yadi puraḥ parāhṛtaṃ homāyābhiduhya juhuyād ity āśmarathyaḥ / tad evayādṛkkīdṛk ca hutvāthānyāṃ dugdhvā punar juhuyād ity ālekhanaḥ
9.7.9	yady uddrutasya skanded yatra skandet tan niṣadya punargṛhṇīyāt / tad eva yādṛkkīdṛk ca hutvāthānyāṃ dugdhvā punar juhuyāt
9.8.1	yadi sakṛd unnītaṃ skanded yadi dvir yadi trir na tad ādriyeteti vijñāyate
9.8.2	kṛtsānām agnihotrāṇāṃ vādam āśmarathya ūce sruvavādam ity ālekhanaḥ
9.8.3	yadi caturthaṃ skandet sthālyāṃ śeṣam ānīya tataś caturgṛhītaṃ gṛhītvā juhuyāt / api vājyasya vāruṇīm ṛcam anūcya vāruṇyarcā juhuyāt
9.8.4	athaikeṣām / yadi duhyamānav abhindyād anyāṃ nirṇijya dohyā
9.8.5	yadi dugdham anyābhidohyā / yady adhiśritam anyābhidohyā / yadi viṣyandetanyābhidohya / yady unnīyamānam anyābhidohyā / yady unnītaṃ punaḥ pratyavanīyānyābhidohyā
9.8.6	yadi prācīnaṃ hriyamāṇaṃ prajāpater viśvabhṛti tanvaṃ hutam asi svāhety abhimṛśet / ājyasya vāruṇīm ṛcam anūcya vāruṇyarcā juhuyāt
9.8.7	yadi lohitaṃ duhyetānyad vā vivarṇam anvāhāryapacanaṃ pariśrityāgnaye rudravate svāheti juhuyāt
9.8.8	yadi śiliśilībhavet samoṣāmum iti brūyād yaṃ dviṣyāt
9.8.9	yadi sāyam āhutau skanded ā prātar ahuter nāśnīyāt / yadi prātar āhutau skanded ā sāyam āhuter nāśnīyāt
9.9.1	yasyāgnihotre 'dhiśrite śvāntarāgni dhāved gārhapatyād bhasmādāyedaṃ viṣṇur vi cakrama iti vaiṣṇavyarcāhavanīyād dhvaṃsayann uddravet
9.9.2	bhasmanā śunaḥ padam apivapati
9.9.3	etad eva sūkaraikasṛke vidyāt
9.9.4	yasyāgnim anuddhṛtaṃ sūryo 'bhinimroced darbheṇa hiraṇyaṃ prabadhya pūrvaḥ pratipadyeta
9.9.5	anvaṅ brāhmaṇa ārṣeyo bahuvid agnim uddharet / anvaṅṅ agnihotreṇānūddravet
9.9.6	pratiṣṭhāpyāgnim agnihotram upasādyā tamitor aprāṇann āsitvā hutvā varaṃ datvā bhūr ity upatiṣṭhetety āśmarathyaḥ / bhūr bhuvaḥ suva ity ālekhanaḥ
9.9.7	anāśvān etāṃ rātrim upavasati
9.9.8	śvo bhūte vāruṇaṃ daśakapālaṃ nirvapati / carum ity ekeṣām
9.9.9	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
9.9.10	yadi sāyam agnihotrasya rtum atinayed doṣā vastor namaḥ svāheti juhuyāt
9.9.11	etad eva nityam agnihotram ity āśmarathyaḥ / athālekhanaḥ / kālasamāpādanīyam evaitena mantreṇa homaṃ hutvā nityam agnihotraṃ juhuyāt
9.9.12	tatra sa eva homakalpaḥ
9.9.13	etāvan nānā / bhūr bhuvaḥ suva iti purā hotor vadet
9.9.14	yadi prātar agnihotrasya rtum atinayet prātar vastor namaḥ svāhā juhuyāt
9.9.15	etad eva nityam agnihotram ity āśmarathyaḥ / athālekhanaḥ / kālasamāpādānīyam evaitena mantreṇa homaṃ hutvā nityam agnihotram upasādyā tamitor aprāṇann āsitvā varaṃ dattvā hutvā bhūr bhuvaḥ suva ity upatiṣṭheta
9.9.16	anugmamayitvāhavanīyam anyaṃ praṇayed anvagnir uṣasām agram akhyad iti
9.9.17	athainam abhimantrayata ihaiva kṣemya edhi mā prahāsīn mām amum āmuṣYāyaṇam iti
9.10.1	tatra maitraṃ caruṃ nirvapet sauryam ekakapālam
9.10.2	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
9.10.3	tasyāṃ saṃsthitāyāṃ vāgyatāv etad ahar anaśnantau jāyāpatī agnim indhānāvāsāte
9.10.4	dvayoḥ payasā sāyam agnihotraṃ juhuyāt
9.10.5	śvo 'gnaye vratapataye puroḍāśam aṣṭākapālaṃ nirvapet
9.10.6	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
9.10.7	yasyāgnim anuddhṛtaṃ sūryo 'bhyudiyāc caturgṛhītam ājyaṃ gṛhītvā pūrvaḥ pratipadyeta
9.10.8	anvaṅ brāhmaṇa ārṣeyo bahuvid agnim uddharet / anvaṅṅ agnihotreṇānūddravet
9.10.9	pratiṣṭhāpyāgnim agnihotram upasādya purastāt pratyaṅṅ upaviśyaitenājyena juhuyād uṣāḥ ketunā juṣatāṃ yajñaṃ devebhir anvitam / devebhyo madhumattamaṃ svāhā // iti
9.10.10	tato nityam agnihotraṃ juhuyāt
9.10.11	tatra sa eva homakalpaḥ
9.10.12	sa prāyaścitto yaḥ prātarṛtāv atinītaḥ
9.10.13	etāvan nānā / nātrāhavanīyam anugamayati
9.10.14	agnaye jyotiṣmate puroḍāśam aṣṭākapālaṃ nirvapet
9.10.15	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
9.11.1	athaikeṣām / yasyāgnim anuddhṛtaṃ sūryo 'bhinimroced abhyudiyād vā mano jyotir juṣatām // trayastriṃśat tantava iti dve caturgṛhīte juhuyāt
9.11.2	yady anastam ite juhuyāt punar astam ite hutvā bhavataṃ naḥ samanasāv ity upatiṣṭhate
9.11.3	yadi mahārātre juhuyāt punar evauṣasaṃ hutvā pūrvavad upatiṣṭhet
9.11.4	yasyānuditahome 'bhiprete 'gnihotram ahutaṃ sūryo 'bhyudiyād yady ante syād unnīya prāṅ udādravet
9.11.5	sa upasādyā tamitor āsīta
9.11.6	sa yadā tāmyed atha bhūḥ svāheti juhuyāt
9.11.7	yasyāhavanīye 'nudvāte gārhapatya udvāyed anugamayitvāhavanīyaṃ gārhapatyasyāvakṣāṇāni saṃnidhāya manthed itaḥ prathamaṃ agnir ity etayā
9.11.8	athainam abhimantrayata iṣe rayyai ramasva sahase dyumnāyorje 'patyāyeti
9.11.9	āhavanīyaṃ praṇīyopasaminddhe sārasvatau tvotsau samindhātām / samrāḍ asi virāḍ asīti
9.11.10	tato 'gnaye tapasvate janadvate pāvakavate 'ṣṭākapālaṃ nirvapet
9.11.11	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
9.11.12	etad eva gārhapatye dhārayaty āhavanīye 'nugate prāyaścittam
9.11.13	etāvan nānā / nātra gārhapatyam anugamayati / agnaye jyotiṣmate puroḍāśam aṣṭākapālaṃ nirvapen na tapasvate
9.11.14	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
9.12.1	yadi sāyam ahute 'gnihotre pūrvo 'gnir anugacched agnihotram adhiśrityonnīyāgninā pūrveṇoddrutyānvaṅṅ agnihotreṇānudravet
9.12.2	yo brāhmaṇo bahuvit so 'gnim uddharet
9.12.3	yat purā dhanam adāyī syāt tad dadyāt
9.12.4	etad eva prātaḥ
9.12.5	yadi prātarahute 'gnihotre 'paro 'gnir anugacched anugamayitvā pūrvaṃ mathitvāparam uddhṛtya juhuyād yadi na tvaret
9.12.6	atha yadi tvaret pūrvam agnim anvavasāya tataḥ prāñcam uddhṛtya juhuyāt
9.12.7	jāmi tu tad yo 'sya pūrvo 'gnis tam aparaṃ karoti / anyatraivāvasāyāgniṃ mathitvoddhṛtya juhuyāt / tato 'gnaye tapasvate janadvate pāvakavate 'ṣṭākapālaṃ nirvapet
9.12.8	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
9.12.9	yadi sāyam ahute 'gnihotre 'paro 'gnir anugacchet pūrvam agnim anvavasāya tata eva prāñcam uddhṛtya juhuyāt
9.12.10	athābhimantrayata ita eva prathamaṃ jajñe agnir ābhyo yonibhyo 'dhi jātavedāḥ / sa gāyatryā triṣṭubhā jagatyānuṣṭubhā ca devebhyo havyaṃ vaha naḥ prajānan // iṣe rayyau ramasva sahase dyummnāyorje patyāyeti ramayaty eva / samrāḍ asisuṣadā sīdeti suṣadā evainaṃ sādayati
9.13.1	sārasvatau tvotsau prāvatām iti / ṛksāme vai sārasvatāv utsau / tābhyām evainaṃ prāvati tābhyāṃ samardhayati
9.13.2	agnaye jyotiṣmate puroḍāśam aṣṭākapālaṃ nirvaped vāruṇaṃ yavamayaṃ carum
9.13.3	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
9.13.4	athaikeṣām / yady ahute 'gnihotre 'paro 'gnir anugacchet tebhya evāvakṣaṇebhyo manthitavyaḥ
9.13.5	atha yadi na tādṛśānīvāvakṣāṇāni syur bhasmanāraṇī saṃsparśya manthitavyaḥ / svād evainaṃ yoner janayatīti vijñāyate
9.13.6	tato 'gnaye tapasvate janadvate pāvakavate 'ṣṭākapālaṃ nirvapet
9.13.7	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
9.13.8	athaikeṣām / yataro 'gnir anugacchet tebhya eva dārubhyo 'dhimanthitavyaḥ
9.13.9	atha yadi tṛṇaidhaḥ śakaidho vā syād bhasmanāraṇī saṃsparśya manthitavyaḥ / svād evainaṃ yoner janayatītivijñāyate
9.13.10	tato 'gnaye tapasvate janadvate pāvakavate 'ṣṭākapālaṃ nirvapet
9.13.11	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
9.13.12	na vānugateṣṭiṃ kuryāt
9.13.13	etā evāhutīr juhuyān mitrāya svāhā // varuṇāya svāhā // sūryāya svāhā // agnaye svāhā // agnaye vratapataye svāhā // agnaye tapasvate janadvate pāvakavate svāhā // agnaye śucaye svāhā // agnaye jyotiṣmate svāhā // iti
9.13.14	vyāhṛtībhir juhoty ekaikaśaḥ samastābhiś ca
9.14.1	agnaye tantumate puroḍāśam aṣṭākapālaṃ nirvaped yasyāgnihotraṃ vilupyeta
9.14.2	āgnavaiṣṇavam ekādaśakapālaṃ nirvaped yam anyasyāgniṣu yājayeyur yo vānyasyāgniṣu yajeta
9.14.3	agnaye 'gnivate puroḍāśam aṣṭākapālaṃ nirvaped yasyāgnāv agnim abhyuddhareyuḥ
9.14.4	trayastriṃśat tantava ity etayā juhuyād yasyāgnihotre 'dhiśrite haviṣi vā nirupte puruṣo vā śvā vāno vāratho vāntarāgnī vīyād iti vijñāyate
9.14.5	yasyāno vā ratho vāntarāgnī vīyād ity ekeṣām
9.14.6	na kālam avadhārayati
9.14.7	tato 'trāpo 'nvatiṣicya gamanvaty āvartayet
9.14.8	idaṃ viṣṇur vi cakrama iti padaṃ saṃlopayet
9.14.9	anugamayitvāhavanīyam anyaṃ praṇayed yad agne pūrvaṃ prabhṛtaṃ padaṃ hi te sūryasya raśmīn anvātatān / tatra rayiṣṭhām anusaṃbharaitaṃ saṃ naḥ sṛja sumatyā vajavatyā // tvam agne saprathā asi juṣṭo hotā vareṇyaḥ / tvayā yajñaṃ vitanvate // iti
9.14.10	tato 'gnaye pathikṛte puroḍāśam aṣṭākapālaṃ nirvapet
9.14.11	patho 'ntikād barhir āharet
9.14.12	anaḍvān dakṣiṇā
9.14.13	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
9.14.14	etām eva nirvapet stotre mūḍhe / etāṃ śastre
9.14.15	etāṃ yasyāgnināgnīn vyaveyuḥ
9.14.16	etāṃ jane pramītasya
9.14.17	janayatu khalu pramītasyeti vijñāyate
9.14.18	abhivānyavatsāyā asya payasāgnihotraṃ juhuyur ā yāvad asyāgnibhiḥ śarīrāṇi saṃsparśayeyuḥ
9.15.1	dakṣiṇāprāgagrair darbhair agnīn paristṛṇāti
9.15.2	adhastāt samidhaṃ dhārayann uddravati
9.15.3	somaṃ pitṛmantaṃ pūrvasyām āhutyām upalakṣayaty agniṃ kavyavāhanam uttarasyām
9.15.4	pātranirṇejanam udakaṃ dakṣiṇā prasiñceyuḥ
9.15.5	brāhmaṇāya yajñāyadhāni dadyuḥ
9.15.6	apo 'bhyavahareyuḥ
9.15.7	amaiva putrasya dṛṣat syād āyasaṃ ca
9.15.8	yasyājyam anutpūtaṃ skandec chindata prāṇi dadyāt
9.15.9	yady utpūtaṃ yad asya gṛheṣu citraṃ dhanaṃ tad dadyāt
9.15.10	etad vaikeṣāṃ viparītavat / anutpūte citram utpūte chindat
9.15.11	atha yadi sruggataṃ skandet yatra skandet tat prāñcaṃ prādeśaṃ nidadhyād bhūtapataye svāheti / bhuvanapataye svāheti dakṣiṇāprāñcam / bhūtānāṃ pataye svāheti pratyañcam / bhūtāya svāhety udañcam
9.15.12	athainat saṃsiñced ity āśmarathyaḥ / saṃ tvā siñcāmīty etayānumantrayetety ālekhanaḥ
9.15.13	bhūtapataye svāhā bhuvanapataye svāhā bhūtānāṃ pataye svāheti skannam anumantrayetety ekeṣām
9.15.14	na kiṃ cana havir adhikṛtya vadati
9.15.15	devāñjanam agan yajñas tasya māśīr avatv ity enad abhimantrayetety ekeṣām ājyādanantaraṃ vadati
9.15.16	yadi praṇītāḥ skandeyur āpo hi ṣṭhā mayobhuva iti tisṛbhir gṛhītvā tataṃ ma āpa ity āhutiṃ juhuyāt
9.16.1	yadi kapālaṃ bhidyeta tat saṃdadhyād gāyatryā tvā śatākṣarayā saṃdadhāmīti
9.16.2	athainad apo 'bhyavahared abhinno gharmo jīradānur iti
9.16.3	tata etām āhutiṃ juhoti trayastriṃśat tantava ity etayā
9.16.4	tato 'nyat kapālaṃ saṃskṛtya kapāleṣv apisṛjed gharmo devāṃ apyetv iti
9.16.5	iti vai khalu yadi prāg upadhānād bhidyeta
9.16.6	atha yady upahitānām etenaiva mantreṇopadadhyāt
9.16.7	yadi kapālaṃ naśyed āśvinaṃ dvikapālaṃ nirvaped dyāvāpṛthivyam ekakapālam
9.16.8	bhārgavo hotā bhavati / ekahāyano dakṣiṇā dadātīti vijñāyate
9.16.9	yathā kathā ca naśyet prāyaścittam eva syād ity āśmarathyaḥ / upayuktānāṃ prāg vimokād ity ālekhanaḥ
9.16.10	yadi patnīḥ saṃyājayan kapālam abhijuhuyāt vaiśvānaraṃ dvādaśakapālaṃ nirvapet
9.16.11	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
9.16.12	etām eva nirvaped amāvāsyāṃ paurṇamāsīṃ vātipādya
9.16.13	etāṃ yad aniṣṭvāgrayaṇena navam aśnīyāt
9.16.14	yasya yamau jāyeyātāṃ gāvau vā puruṣau vā vaiśvānaraṃ dvādaśakapālaṃ nirvapet
9.16.15	yasya triṣṭubhau yājyānuvākye bhavato jagatyai vā
9.16.16	raudraṃ vāstumayaṃ caruṃ nirvaped yasya rudraḥ paśūn śamāyeta
9.16.17	tayā niṣādasthapatiṃ yājayet
9.16.18	kṛṣṇājinaṃ vā kūṭaṃ vākarṇo vā gardabho hariṇo vā hariṇapṛṇākā vā śaphakaśyāmākapātrau vā dve vā kambuśūrpe dakṣiṇeti vijñāyate
9.17.1	yo brahmacārī striyam upeyāt sa raudraṃ gardabham ālabheta
9.17.2	tasyāvadānair apsu pracaranti
9.17.3	nāsya vapayā caranti na paśupuroḍāśo bhavati
9.17.4	iḍānto bhavati śaṃyuvanto vā
9.17.5	nairṛtaḥ prājāpatyo vā
9.17.6	yasya haviḥ kṣāyati taṃ yajñaṃ nirṛtir gṛhṇāti
9.17.7	yad ucchiṣṭaṃ syāt tena śeṣaṃ saṃsthāpayet
9.17.8	yajño hi yajñasya prāyaścittiḥ
9.17.9	yaṃ dviṣyāt tasmai tāṃ dakṣiṇāṃ dadyāt
9.17.10	yathā kathā ca kṣāyet prāyaścittam eva syād ity āśmarathyaḥ / yady avadānebhyo na prabhaved ity ālekhanaḥ
9.17.11	apo duṣṭaṃ havir abhyavaharantīti vijñāyate
9.17.12	yady aprattadaivataṃ havir vyāpadyetāpas tad abhyavahṛtyānyat tad daivataṃ havir nirvapet
9.17.13	tatra srug ādānaprabhṛtayo mantrā abhyāvarteran
9.17.14	atha yadi prattadaivatam ājyena śeṣaṃ saṃsthāpayed ity ekam / tūṣṇīkaṃ havir abhyudāhared ity aparam
9.18.1	atha yadi sarvāṇy eva havīṃṣi naśyeyur vā duṣyeyur vājyenaināni prati saṃkhyāya tayājyahaviṣeṣṭyā yajeta
9.18.2	ato 'nyām iṣṭim anulbaṇāṃ tanvīta
9.18.3	yajñena hi yajñasya prāyaścittiṃ kurvantīti vijñāyate
9.18.4	kathaṃ duṣṭaṃ havir vidyāt / yad āryāṇāṃ dharmajñānāṃ dharmakāmānām abhojanīyaṃ na tena devān yajeta
9.18.5	yadd havir duḥśṛtaṃ tad yamadevatyam / yamam eva tad gacchatīti vijñāyate
9.18.6	saṃsthāpya tadd havir anvāhāryapacane catuḥśarāvam odanaṃ paktvā caturbhyo brāhmaṇebhyo jīvataṇḍulam ivopaharet
9.18.7	tatrāpi bhārgavo ekaḥ prāśitṝṇāṃ syāt
9.18.8	yady ādiṣṭāṃ dakṣiṇām antariyād urvarāṃ pratiṣṭhitāṃ dadyāt
9.18.9	yo 'dakṣiṇena yajñena yajeta sa yajñaḥ prakṣāmaḥ / anāyur yajamānaḥ syāt
9.18.10	urvarāṃ sasyavatīṃ dadyāt
9.18.11	yady abhāgāṃ devatām āvāhayed ājyenaināṃ yathoḍhāṃ yajeta
9.18.12	bhāginīm antaritāṃ yatra smaret tad upotthāyāvāhayet
9.18.13	yad vo devā atipādayānīty atrāhutiṃ juhuyāt
9.19.1	yadi daivate vāvadāne vā yājyānuvākye vā parihareyur yad asya gṛheṣu citraṃ dhanaṃ tad dadyāt
9.19.2	yady āhutiḥ skanded āgnīdhraṃ brūyāj juhudhīti
9.19.3	tāṃ so 'ñjalinā juhoty agnes tvāsye juhomi mā yajamāno riṣan mā yajñapatnī mā yajñanīr iti / amuṣmai tvāsye juhomīti vā
9.19.4	yasyai devatāyai hutaṃ bhavati tasyai pūrṇapātraṃ dadyāt
9.19.5	yasyai devatāyai gṛhītam ahutaṃ skanded yasya vā devatām antariyur yad asya gṛheṣu puṣkalaṃ dhanaṃ tad dadyāt
9.19.6	yad āhutī viparihared athaitāṃ prāyaścittiṃ juhuyāt tvaṃ no agne // sa tvaṃ no agna iti
9.19.7	ete evāntaraye sarvatra viparyaye ca juhuyāt
9.19.8	yadi puroḍāśaḥ saṃ vā vijetod vā patet tam udvāsya barhiṣy āsādyaitenābhi ca ghārayed abhi ca mantrayeta kim utpatasi kim utproṣṭhāḥ śāntaḥ śānter ihāgahi / aghoro yajñiyo bhūtvāsīda sadanaṃ svam // mā hiṃsīr devapreṣita ājyena tejasājyasya mā naḥ kiṃcana rīriṣaḥ / yogakṣemasya śāntyā asminn āsīda barhiṣīti
9.19.9	bhūtvā prabhavati yajamāno yasyaitāṃ yajñe prāyaścittiṃ kurvantīti vijñāyate prāyaścittiṃ kurvantīti vijñāyate
10.1.1	vasante jyotiṣṭomena yakṣyamāṇo brāhmaṇān ārṣeyān ṛtvijo vṛṇīte yūnaḥ sthavirān vānūcānān anaṅgahīnān ūrdhvavācaś caturaḥ
10.1.2	sarvān vā
10.1.3	caturo vṛṇāno mahartvijo vṛṇīte 'dhvaryuṃ brahmāṇaṃ hotāram udgātaram iti
10.1.4	ādityo devo daivyo 'dhvaryuḥ sa me 'dhvaryur astv ity upāṃśu daivyam adhvaryuṃ vṛtvāsau mānuṣa ity uccair mānuṣaṃ vṛṇīte
10.1.5	candramā devo daivyo brahmā sa me brahmāstv ity upāṃśu daivyaṃ brahmāṇaṃ vṛtvāsau mānuṣa ity uccair mānuṣaṃ vṛṇīte
10.1.6	agnir devo daivyo hotā sa me hotāstv ity upāṃśu daivyaṃ hotāraṃ vṛtvāsau mānuṣa ity uccair mānuṣaṃ vṛṇīte
10.1.7	parjanyo devo daivya udgātā sa ma udgātāstv ity upāṃśu daivyaṃ udgātāraṃ vṛtvāsau mānuṣa ity uccair mānuṣaṃ vṛṇīte
10.1.8	sadasyaṃ mahartvijaṃ pañcamaṃ kauṣītakinaḥ samāmananti
10.1.9	sa kṛtākṛtakarmaṇām upadraṣṭā bhavati
10.1.10	taṃ vṛṇīte
10.1.11	ākāśo devo daivyaḥ sadasyaḥ sa me sadasyo 'stv ity upāṃśu daivyaṃ sadasyaṃ vṛtvāsau mānuṣa ity uccair mānuṣaṃ vṛṇīte
10.1.12	āpo devīr daivyā hotrāśaṃsinas te me hotrāśaṃsinaḥ santv ity upāṃśu daivyān hotrāśaṃsino vṛtvāsau cāsau mānuṣa ity uccair mānuṣān vṛṇīte
10.2.1	raśmayo devā daivyāś camasādhvaryavas te me camasādhvaryavaḥ santv ity upāṃśu daivyāṃś camasādhvaryūn vṛtvāsau cāsau mānuṣa ity uccair mānuṣān vṛṇīte
10.2.2	yajñopavītaṃ kṛtvāpa ācamya prāṅ vodaṅ vā tiṣṭhan japaty āsīno vā bhūr bhuvaḥ suvaḥ // āyur me prāvoco varco me prāvoco yaśo me prāvocaḥ śriyaṃ me prāvocaḥ // āyuṣmān ahaṃ varcasvī yaśasvī śrīmān apacitimān bhūyāsam // bhūr bhuvaḥ suvaḥ // sarvaṃ bhūyāsam ity uktvā prati vā caṣṭe prati vā jānīte
10.2.3	sa pratijñāya devo devam etu somaḥ somam etv ṛtasya pathā // emi vihāya dauṣkṛtyam ity abhipravrajati
10.2.4	padvā nāmāsi srutiḥ somasaraṇī somaṃ gameyam iti panthānam ātiṣṭhate
10.2.5	pitaro bhūr iti pitṝn dakṣiṇāmukha upatiṣṭhate
10.2.6	athainaṃ gṛhān ohyāhvayati
10.2.7	ācchādya cainaṃ kuṇḍalinaṃ karoti
10.2.8	ekadhanaṃ cāsmai dadāti
10.2.9	amāvāsyāyāṃ dīkṣate paurṇamāsyāṃ vā
10.2.10	tasyāparimitā dīkṣāḥ saṃvatsaraparārdhyāḥ
10.2.11	na darśapūrṇamāsābhyām aniṣṭvā somena yajeta
10.2.12	nāgniṣṭomenāniṣṭvetaraiḥ kratubhir iti
10.2.13	atirātram eke prathamaṃ yajñaṃ samāmananti
10.2.14	na rathantarapṛṣṭham akṛtvā bṛhatpṛṣṭhaṃ kurvīta
10.2.15	amāvāsyāyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ vā sutyam ahar bhavati
10.3.1	prācīnavaṃśaṃ vimitaṃ minvanti purastād unnatam
10.3.2	tasya pratidiśaṃ dvārāṇi bhavanti / uttarapūrvam avāntaradeśaṃ prati pañcamaṃ dvāram
10.3.3	sraktiṣv ārokān kurvantīty ekeṣām
10.3.4	tasmin saptahotāraṃ manasānudrutyāhavanīye sagrahaṃ juhoti
10.3.5	dīkṣaṇīyām iṣṭiṃ nirvapati
10.3.6	āgnāvaiṣṇavam ekādaśakapālam āgnāvaiṣṇavaṃ vā ghṛte carum
10.3.7	patnīsaṃyājāntā dīkṣaṇīyā saṃtiṣṭhate
10.3.8	yat prāg agnīṣomīyāt sarvaṃ tad upāṃśu kriyate
10.3.9	nātrānvāhāryo bhavati
10.3.10	uttareṇa prāgvaṃśaṃ pariśrite yajamānaḥ keśaśmaśru vāpayate
10.3.11	tasya dakṣiṇaṃ godānam unatty āpa udantu jīvasa iti
10.3.12	treṇyā śalalyā vinīya trīṇi darbhapuñjīlāny ūrdhvāgrāṇy upaniyacchaty oṣadhe trāyasvainam iti
10.3.13	svadhite mainaṃ hiṃsīr iti svadhitinādhinidadhāti
10.3.14	devaśrūr etāni pra vapa iti pravapati
10.3.15	svasty uttarāṇy aśīyety etaṃ mantraṃ yajamāno japati
10.3.16	śmaśrūṇy agre vāpayate 'thopapakṣāv atha keśān iti vijñāyate
10.3.17	audumbareṇa dantadhāvanena dato dhāvate lohitam anāgamayan
10.3.18	dantān prakṣālyābhyantaraṃ nakhāni kārayate
10.3.19	savyasyāgre kaniṣṭhikātaḥ / atha dakṣiṇasya
10.3.20	hastyāny agre 'tha padyāni
10.3.21	yal lomaśam avakāvalaṃ tīrthaṃ tasmin snāti
10.3.22	sthāvarāḥ saṃtatā bhavanti
10.4.1	kuṇḍe snātīty ekeṣām
10.4.2	śaṅkhini hrade hiraṇyam avadhāyāpo asmān mātaraḥ śundhantv iti snāta udgāhata ud ābhyaḥ śucir ā pūta emīti
10.4.3	apa ācamya kṣaumaṃ vāso 'hatam antaraṃ paridhatte somasya tanūr asi tanuvaṃ me pāhīti
10.4.4	somasya nīvīr asīti nīvīm anuparikalpayate
10.4.5	yad asya pratipriyam annaṃ tad aśnāty ūrg asīti
10.4.6	sarpirmiśraṃ dadhi madhu cābhyupasekam āśito bhavati
10.4.7	kanīyaḥkanīyo 'ta ūrdhvaṃ vratayati
10.4.8	mahīnāṃ payo 'sīti darbhapuñjīlābhyāṃ navanītaṃ saṃyutya triḥ parācīnam abhyaṅkte varcodhā asi varco mayi dhehīti
10.4.9	mukham agre 'nulomam aṅgāni
10.4.10	svabhyakto bhavati
10.4.11	traikakudenāñjanenāṅkte
10.4.12	yadi traikakudaṃ nādhigacched yenaiva kena cāñjanenāñjīta
10.4.13	satūlayā śareṣīkayā darbheṣīkayā darbhapuñjīlena vā dakṣiṇaṃ pūrvam anidhāvamāno vṛtrasya kanīnikāsi cakṣuṣpā asi cakṣur me pāhīti / trir dakṣiṇaṃ dvir uttaram
10.5.1	athainam ekaviṃśatyā darbhapuñjīlaiḥ saptabhiḥ saptabhis triḥ pavayati citpatis tvā punātu // vākpatis tvā punātu // devas tvā savitā punātv ity etair mantraiḥ
10.5.2	acchidreṇa pavitreṇety etaṃ mantraṃ sarvatrānuṣajati
10.5.3	dvir ūrdhvaṃ nābher unmārṣṭi sakṛd avāṅ
10.5.4	pavamānaḥ suvarjana ity etam anuvākaṃ pāvyamāno japati
10.5.5	yad devā devaheḍanam iti ca / tasya te pavitrapate pavitreṇa yasmai kaṃ pune tac chakeyam iti caitaṃ mantram
10.5.6	ā vo devāsa īmaha iti pūrvayā dvārā prāgvaṃśaṃ praviśyāpareṇāhavanīyam atikramya dakṣiṇatas tiṣṭhann āhavanīyam abhimantrayata indrāgnī dyāvāpṛthivīty anuvākaśeṣeṇa
10.5.7	tasyaiṣa eva saṃcaro bhavaty ā sutyāyāḥ
10.5.8	atraike dīkṣaṇīyām iṣṭiṃ samāmananti
10.5.9	yad dīkṣaṇīyāyāṃ dhrauvam ājyaṃ tataḥ sruveṇa catasro dīkṣāhutīr juhoty ākūtyai prayuje 'gnaye svāhety etair mantraiḥ
10.5.10	srucā pañcamīm āpo devīr bṛhatīr viśvaśaṃbhuva iti
10.5.11	caturgṛhītena srucaṃ pūrayitvā dvādaśagṛhītena vā pūrṇāhutiṃ juhoti viśve devasya netur ity etayā
10.5.12	bilāvakāśaṃ kṛtvā juhotīty ekeṣām
10.5.13	kṛṣṇājinasya dakṣiṇaṃ pūrvapādaṃ pariṣīvyati
10.5.14	dve vā samīcī māṃsasaṃhite kṛtvā
10.5.15	antarvedi kṛṣṇājinaṃ prācīnagrīvam uttaralomāstīrya śuklāṃ ca kṛṣṇāṃ ca rājiṃ yajamānaḥ saṃmṛśaty ṛksāmayoḥ śilpe stha iti
10.5.16	bhasatto jānvakna ārohatīmāṃ dhiyaṃ śikṣamāṇasya // sutrāmāṇam iti dvābhyām
10.6.1	ārūḍho japatīmāṃ su nāvam āruham ity etām
10.6.2	viṣṇoḥ śarmāsi śarma yajamānasya śarma me yacchety aṃsaṃ prorṇute
10.6.3	nakṣatrāṇāṃ mātīkāśāt pāhīty uṣṇīṣeṇa śiro veṣṭayate
10.6.4	saśiro vā prorṇute yathāsuṣṭhu
10.6.5	patnyāḥ śirasi kumbakurīraṃ kalpayati
10.6.6	jālaṃ kurīram ity ācakṣate
10.6.7	kṛṣṇānāṃ jīvorṇānāṃ bhavatīti vijñāyate
10.6.8	athaināṃ kṣaumeṇa vāsasā prācīnamātrā paridhāpayati
10.6.9	ūrdhvavāsyaṃ bruvate
10.6.10	yajamānam anyatarataḥpāśayā mauñjyā mekhalayā trivṛtā pṛthvyā madhyataḥ saṃnahyaty ūrg asy āṅgirasīti
10.6.11	uttareṇa nābhiṃ niṣṭarkyaṃ granthiṃ kṛtvā dakṣiṇato nābheḥ paryūhate
10.6.12	yoktreṇa patnīṃ saṃnahyati yathā darśapūrṇamāsayoḥ saṃ tvā nahyāmīty etayā
10.6.13	athāsmai trivaliṃ pañcavaliṃ vā kṛṣṇaviṣāṇāṃ pradakṣiṇāvartāṃ prayacchatīndrasya yonir asi mā mā hiṃsīr iti
10.6.14	tām etenaiva mantreṇābadhnāti
10.6.15	tayā veder loṣṭam uddhanti kṛṣyai tvā susasyāyā iti
10.6.16	supippalābhyas tvauṣadhībhya iti śirasi kaṇḍūyate yadāsya kaṇḍūyati
10.6.17	viṣāṇe viṣyaitaṃ granthiṃ yad asya gulphitaṃ hṛdi mano yad asya gulphitam ity aṅgeṣu
10.6.18	athāsmā audumbaraṃ dīkṣitadaṇḍaṃ prayacchati mukhena saṃmitam ūrdhvasad asi vānaspatyaḥ sudyumno dyumnaṃ yajamānāya dhehīti
10.6.19	yaḥ kaś ca yajñiyo vṛkṣaḥ phalagrahis tasya kārya ity ekeṣām
10.6.20	taṃ pratigṛhṇāti sūpasthā adya devo vanaspatir iti
10.7.1	camasaṃ vratapradānam abhimantrayata uruvyacā asi janadhāḥ sapatno mā pāhyasya yajñasyodṛcaḥ
10.7.2	athāṅgulīr nyañcati / svāhā yajñaṃ manaseti dve / svāhā dyāvāpṛthivībhyām iti dve / svāhoror antarikṣād iti dve
10.7.3	svāhā yajñaṃ vātādārabha iti muṣṭī karoti
10.7.4	athainaṃ saṃbhārayajūṃṣi vācayaty agnir yajurbhir iti
10.7.5	tato vācaṃ yacchaty ā nakṣatrāṇām udayāt
10.7.6	yadi purā nakṣatrebhyo vācaṃ visṛjed vaiṣṇavīm āgnāvaiṣṇavīṃ sārasvatīṃ bārhaspatyām ity anūcya punar eva vācaṃ yacchet
10.7.7	tvam agne vratapā asīti brūyād yadi muṣṭī vācaṃ vā visṛjet
10.7.8	athainam āvedayaty adīkṣiṣṭāyaṃ brāhmaṇo 'sāv āmuṣyāyaṇo 'muṣya putro 'muṣya pautro 'muṣya naptāmuṣyāḥ putro 'muṣyāḥ pautro 'muṣyā napteti / trir upāṃśu trir uccaiḥ
10.7.9	yaḥ kaścana dīkṣeta brāhmaṇa ity evainam āvedayet
10.7.10	aparāhṇe dīkṣate
10.7.11	yaṃ kāmayeta tapasvī syād iti taṃ prātardīkṣayet
10.7.12	utthāya kṛṣṇājinaṃ pratimuñcati
10.7.13	sa etad vrataṃ carati / na māṃsam aśnāti na striyam upaiti noparyāste jugupsetānṛtāt
10.7.14	parihvālaṃ mānuṣīṃ vācaṃ vadati canasitaṃ vicakṣaṇaṃ vānuṣajan
10.7.15	canasiteti brāhmaṇam āmantrayīta / vicakṣaṇeti rājanyavaiśyāv iti vijñāyate
10.7.16	brāhmaṇena caiva kṣatriyeṇa vā vaiśyena vā saṃbhāṣeta
10.7.17	tata evainam anuprayujyeran
10.7.18	yady enaṃ śūdreṇa saṃvāda upapadyetaiteṣām evaikaṃ brūyād imaṃ nu vicakṣveti
10.8.1	na purā somasya krayād aporṇvīta
10.8.2	na purā dakṣiṇābhyo netoḥ kṛṣṇaviṣāṇām avacṛtet
10.8.3	kṛṣṇaviṣāṇayā kaṇḍūyate
10.8.4	apigṛhya smayate
10.8.5	amedhyaṃ dṛṣṭvā japaty abaddhaṃ mano daridraṃ cakṣuḥ sūryo jyotiṣāṃ śreṣṭho dīkṣe mā mā hāsīr iti
10.8.6	abhivṛṣyamāṇo japaty undatīr balaṃ dhattaujo dhatta balaṃ dhatta mā me dīkṣāṃ mā tapo nirvadhiṣṭeti
10.8.7	na dīkṣitavimitāt pravaset
10.8.8	nainam anyatra dīkṣitavimitāt sūryo 'bhyudiyān nābhyastamiyāt
10.8.9	dakṣiṇata āhavanīyam abhyāvṛtya śayīta
10.8.10	na nyaṅ śayīta nottānaḥ / nāgner apaparyāvarteta
10.8.11	yathartu smayet / yathartu niṣkrāmatīti vijñāyate
10.8.12	yathākālaṃ bruvate
10.8.13	na niṣṭhīven na dato dhāven na divā vicāraṃ kuryān na mūtram
10.8.14	yadi kuryāc chāyāyāṃ kuryāt
10.8.15	apo muñcāmi na prajāmaṃhomucaḥ svāhākṛtāḥ pṛthivīm āviśateti mūtraṃ visṛjati
10.8.16	na pacati na dadāti na kāṃcanāhutiṃ juhoty anyatra somāṅgebhyaḥ
10.8.17	karśed ātmānaṃ yāvad asya kṛṣṇam akṣyor naśyati
10.8.18	kṛṣṇājinān na chidyeta / evaṃ daṇḍāt
10.9.1	yad anyatra kṛṣṇājinād āsīta devāñjanam agan yajñasya māśīr avatv ity etad abhimantrayeta
10.9.2	nāsya nāma gṛhṇīyāt / na pāpaṃ kīrtayet / nainam abhivadet / dīkṣita evābhivadet
10.9.3	nāsyānnam adyād āgnīṣomīyāt
10.9.4	kāmaṃ saṃsthite 'gnīṣomīye hutāyāṃ vā vapāyāṃ krīte vā rājani
10.9.5	api vādita eva yajñārtham utkalpya dīkṣeta
10.9.6	athetarato bhuñjīran
10.9.7	tāny etāni vratāny ūrdhvaṃ dīkṣaṇīyāyāḥ prakrāmanti
10.9.8	athemāni dravyopayogāni yathaitat kṛṣṇaviṣāṇayā kaṇḍūyanaṃ kṛṣṇājina āsanaṃ daṇḍadhāraṇam iti
10.9.9	payovratā patnī brahmacāriṇī bhavati
10.9.10	eṣṭrī stha iti catasro 'ṅgulīr utsṛjati
10.9.11	dugdhe vrate nakṣatraṃ dṛṣṭvā vrataṃ kṛṇuteti vācaṃ visṛjati
10.9.12	jāgarti etāṃ rātrim
10.9.13	yavāgū rājanyasya vratam āmikṣā vaiśyasya payo brāhmaṇasya
10.9.14	tāny etāni daikṣāṇi vratāni
10.9.15	sarveṣāṃ tv evopasatsu stanavibhāgaḥ
10.10.1	gārhapatye yajamānasya vrataṃ śrapayati / dakṣiṇāgnau patnyāḥ
10.10.2	yāgnihotrasya skannasya prāyaścittiḥ sā vratasya
10.10.3	tad u haike paya eva vratayanti
10.10.4	tad u tathā na kuryāt / payasy eva yavāguṃ śrapayitvā vratayet
10.10.5	yadi alpaṃ syād anyāṃ dugdhvā śrapayitvā vratayet
10.10.6	yadi payo na vidyetāpsv eva śrapayitvā vratayet
10.10.7	yadi dadhīyād etad evāsmai dadhi kuryuḥ
10.10.8	yady annīyād dhānā asmā anvāvapeyuḥ saktūn asmā anvāvapeyur ghṛtam asmā anvānayeyuḥ / apy antataḥ phalāny eva vratayed agnihotrasyāvicchedāyeti vijñāyate
10.10.9	apareṇāhavanīyaṃ vratam atyāhṛtya prayacchati
10.10.10	athainam āha vratya vrataya vratam upehīti
10.10.11	nādīkṣitā dīkṣitam vratayantaṃ paśyanti
10.10.12	daivīṃ dhiyaṃ manāmaha iti hastāv avanenikte
10.10.13	ye devā manojātā manoyuja iti madhyarātre vratayati
10.10.14	vratayitvāpa ācāmati śivāḥ pītā bhavatha yūyam āpo 'smākaṃ yonā udare suśevāḥ / irāvatīr anamīvā anāgasaḥ śivā no bhavatha jīvase // iti
10.10.15	upodayaṃ vrataprado vācaṃ yamayaty agnīñ jyotiṣmataḥ kuruta dīkṣita vācaṃ yaccha patni vācaṃ yaccheti
10.11.1	udyantam ādityam upatiṣṭhate yāḥ paśūnām ṛṣabhe vāco agne tā agne sūryaḥ śukro agre / tā vaḥ prahiṇomi yathābhāgam atra śivā nas tāḥ punar āyantu vāca iti
10.11.2	udita āditye dugdhe vrate vrataṃ kṛṇuteti vācaṃ visṛjati
10.11.3	evaṃ madhyaṃdine vratayati
10.11.4	adhivṛkṣasūrye vrataprado vācaṃ yamayaty agnīñ jyotiṣmataḥ kuruta dīkṣita vācaṃ yaccha patni vācaṃ yaccheti
10.11.5	evam evāta ūrdhvam
10.11.6	madhyarātre madhyaṃdine vratayati
10.11.7	evam upodayam
10.11.8	adhivṛkṣasūrye vrataprado vācaṃ yamayati
10.11.9	na sūtye 'hani vrataṃ vidyata ity ekam / vidyata ity aparam
10.11.10	svapsyann āhavanīyam abhimantrayate 'gne tvaṃ su jāgṛhi vayaṃ su mandiṣīmahīti
10.11.11	prabudhya japati tvam agne vratapā asīti pratipadya viśve devā abhi mām avavṛtrann ity antena
10.11.12	tvam agne vratapeti brūyāt svapsyan suptvā vā pratibudhya yadi vādīkṣitavāco 'vāvadet
10.11.13	eṣa evāta ūrdhvaṃ saṃveśanapratibodhanānāṃ kalpo bhavati
10.11.14	pūṣā sanyā somo rādhaseti
10.12.1	sanīhārān saṃśāsti
10.12.2	te yal labhante tat pratigṛhṇāti devaḥ savitā vasor vasudāvā rāsveyat somā bhūyo bhara / mā pṛṇan pūrtyā virādhi māhamāyuṣā // candramasi mama bhogāya bhavety etair mantrair yathārūpam
10.12.3	sāvitreṇānyat pratigṛhṇāti
10.12.4	dvādaśāhaṃ dakṣiṇārthaṃ bhikṣate
10.12.5	vāyave tveti naṣṭām anudiśati
10.12.6	varuṇāya tvety apsu magnām
10.12.7	nirṛtyai tvety avasannām
10.12.8	rudrāya tveti mahādevahatām
10.12.9	indrāya tveti meṣkahatāṃ yā vā saṃśīryeta
10.12.10	marudbhyas tveti hrādunihatām
10.12.11	indrāya tvā prasahvana iti yāṃ senā abhītvarī vindeta
10.12.12	yamāya tvety avijñāte
10.12.13	yady anupradiṣṭām adhigacchen na goṣu cārayet
10.12.14	atha yadi prayiyāset pṛthag araṇīṣv agnīn samāropya rathena prayāyāt
10.12.15	yadi ratho na vidyeta rathāṅgam ādāya prayāyāt
10.12.16	bhadrād abhi preyaḥ prehīty āhavanīyam abhimantrayate
10.12.17	devīr āpo 'pāṃ napād ity apo 'tigāhate
10.12.18	acchinnaṃ tantuṃ pṛthivyā anu geṣam iti loṣṭaṃ vimṛdnaṃs tarati
10.12.19	sikatā loṣṭaṃ vā madhye pāre ca nyasyati pṛthivyā saṃ bhaveti
10.12.20	atha yadi nāvyās tared araṇīś ca rathaṃ cādāya taret
10.12.21	yadi ratho na vidyeta rathāṅgam ādāya taret
10.13.1	kṣatriyaṃ yācitvodakānte devayajanam adhyavasyati yad udīcīnaprācīnapravaṇam edam aganma devayajanaṃ pṛthivyā iti
10.13.2	na vā devayajanaṃ yācet
10.13.3	ādityam evaitena mantreṇopatiṣṭheta sakṣedaṃ paśya / vidhartar idaṃ paśya / nākedaṃ paśya / ramatiḥ paniṣṭhā / ṛtaṃ varṣiṣṭham / amṛtā yānyāhuḥ / sūryo variṣṭho akṣabhir vibhāti / anu dyāvāpṛthivī devaputra iti
10.13.4	na purastād devayajanamātram atiricyeta
10.13.5	ādita evaike devayajanasyādhyavasānaṃ samāmananti
10.13.6	purohaviṣi devayajane yājayed iti kāmyāni devayajanāni brāhmaṇavyākhyātāni bhavanti
10.13.7	kautsāt somaṃ krīṇīteti vijñāyate
10.13.8	śūdrād ity ekeṣām
10.13.9	uttaravedyāṃ voparavāṇāṃ kāla ānaḍuhaṃ rohitaṃ carma prācīnagrīvam uttaralomāstīrya tasmin rājānaṃ nyupyottarata udakumbhaṃ nidhāya saṃpreṣyati somavikrayin somaṃ śodhayeti
10.13.10	pariśrite somavikrayī rājānaṃ vicinoti
10.13.11	na vicīyamānasyopadraṣṭāro bhavanti
10.14.1	prāyaṇīyāyās tantraṃ prakramayati
10.14.2	tatraitāni na kriyante 'gnyanvādhānaṃ vratopāyanaṃ patnīsaṃnahanam anvāhārya iti
10.14.3	ye ke ca soma iṣṭipaśubandhāḥ sarveṣv evaitāni na kriyante
10.14.4	udayanīyāyām anūbandhyāyāṃ vratopāyanaṃ patnīsaṃnahanam iti kriyante
10.14.5	sarvāṇy udavasānīyāyāṃ kriyante 'nyatrānvāhāryāt
10.14.6	tatraiṣo 'tyantapradeśaḥ / yat kiṃ ca pratate tantre havir āgacchati yāni kṛtāni na tāni punaḥ kriyante / yathā paśupuroḍāśe prayājānūyājā yāni cānyāny evaṃrūpāṇi bhavanti
10.14.7	adityai prāyaṇīyaṃ caruṃ nirvapati
10.14.8	payasi śṛto bhavati
10.14.9	samānam ā sadanāt
10.14.10	uddhṛtya caruṃ ṣaḍḍhotrā sādayati
10.14.11	etasyām eva sthālyāṃ mekṣaṇe niṣkāsam iti prajñātaṃ nidadhāti
10.14.12	saptadaśa sāmidhenyo bhavanti
10.14.13	samānam ājyabhāgābhyām
10.14.14	catura ājyabhāgān yajati pathyāṃ svastiṃ purastād agniṃ dakṣiṇataḥ somaṃ paścāt savitāram uttarataḥ
10.14.15	haviṣāditiṃ madhye
10.14.16	śaṃyuvantā prāyaṇīyā saṃtiṣṭhate
10.14.17	atraike rājño nivapanaṃ samāmananti
10.14.18	yat prāyaṇīyāyā dhrauvam ājyaṃ tato juhvāṃ catur gṛhītvā darbheṇa hiraṇyaṃ niṣṭarkyaṃ baddhvāvadadhātīyaṃ te śukra tanūr idaṃ varca iti
10.14.19	eṣā somakrayaṇī bhavati / akūṭā ced akarṇākāṇāśroṇāsaptaśaphāruṇā piṅgākṣy ekahāyanī dvihāyanī vā / yā śuṇṭhādhīlodhakarṇī tayā ṣoḍaśinaḥ somaṃ krīṇātīti vijñāyate
10.15.1	tam īkṣamāṇo juhoti jūr asi dhṛtā manaseti
10.15.2	aparaṃ caturgṛhītaṃ gṛhītvā śukram asy amṛtam asīti hiraṇyaṃ ghṛtād uddharati
10.15.3	vaiśvadevaṃ havir ity ājyam abhimantrayate
10.15.4	pramucya hiraṇyam ādityam upatiṣṭhate sūryasya cakṣur āruham iti
10.15.5	somakrayaṇīm abhimantrayate cid asi manāsīti pratipadyendrāya somam ity antena
10.15.6	athāsyā dakṣiṇena padā dakṣiṇāni ṣaṭ padāny anukrāmati vasvy asi // rudrāsīty etair mantraiḥ
10.15.7	saptamaṃ padam abhinigṛhṇāti bṛhaspatis tvā sumne raṇvatv iti

11.1.1	pravargyaṃ saṃbhariṣyann udagayan āpūryamāṇapakṣe puṇye nakṣatre paurṇamāsyām amāvāsyāyāṃ vā tūṣṇīṃ kāṇṭakīṃ samidham ādhāya yujñate mana iti caturgṛhītaṃ juhoti yady adīkṣito bhavati

11.4.2	pacyamānān upacaraty abhīmaṃ mahinā divam ity etayottarayā vā
11.4.3	sarvāṇy upacāraṇāni mantravanti bhavanti
11.4.4	pakveṣu siddhyai tveti dhṛṣṭī ādāyādhvaryuḥ prathamakṛtaṃ mahāvīram udvāsayati devas tvā savitodvapatv iti
11.4.5	uttarataḥ sikatāsu pratiṣṭhāpayaty upadyamānaḥ pṛthivyām āśā diśa āpṛṇeti
11.4.6	athainam anvīkṣate sūryasya tvā cakṣuṣānvīkṣa iti
11.4.7	evam eva dvitīyam udvāsayaty evaṃ tṛtīyam
11.4.8	tuṣṇīm itarāṇi
11.4.9	athainān sikatābhiḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ paryūhatīdam aham amum āmuṣyāyaṇaṃ viśā paśubhir brahmavarcasena paryūhāmīti
11.4.10	viśeti rājanyasya / paśubhir iti vaiśyasya
11.4.11	athainān prabhūtenājāpayasā chṛṇatti gāyatreṇa tvā chandasā chṛṇadmīty etair mantraiḥ / tribhis tribhir ekaikam
11.4.12	api vā sarvair ekaikam
11.4.13	athainān kṛṣṇājina upanahyāsajati deva puraścara saghyāsaṃ tveti
11.4.14	upariṣṭāt kāla eṣa mantro bhavatīty aparam
11.5.1	pravargyeṇa pracariṣyantaḥ saṃvṛṇvanti dvārāṇi
11.5.2	pariśrayanti patnyāḥ
11.5.3	paścādd hotopaviśati / purastād adhvaryuḥ / dakṣiṇato brahmā yajamānaḥ prastotā ca / uttarata āgnīdhraḥ pratiprasthātā ca
11.5.4	madantīr upaspṛśya prathamenānuvākena śāntiṃ kṛtvottareṇa vihāraṃ darbhān saṃstīrya tatraitān mahāvīrān upāvaharati deva puraścara savyāsaṃ tveti
11.5.5	upariṣṭāt kāla eṣa mantro bhavatīty aparam
11.5.6	atraiva sarvaṃ parigharmyam upāvaharati
11.5.7	audumbarīṃ samrāḍāsandīṃ nitarām
11.5.8	rājāsandyā varṣīyasīm eke samāmananti
11.5.9	mauñjībhī rajjubhir ekasarābhir vyutām
11.5.10	catasra audumbarīḥ srucaḥ
11.5.11	tāsāṃ dve aniṣṭubdhe
11.5.12	niṣṭubdhayor varṣīyasy upayamanī hrasīyasī prokṣaṇīdhānī
11.5.13	audumbarau sruvau / audumbarau śaphau mahāvīrasaṃmitāv raskyau / audumbarī dhṛṣṭī / audumbarī methī / trīn audumbarān mayukhān / ṣaḍ audumbarān śakalān
11.5.14	trayodaśa vaikaṅkatān paridhīn kāṇṭakīṃ ca samidham
11.5.15	prabhūtāni gharmendhanāni khādirāṇy audumbarāṇi vaikaṅkatāni kārṣmaryamayāṇi vā
11.5.16	trīṇi kārṣṇājināni dhavitrāṇi yeṣāṃ śuklakṛṣṇalomāni syuḥ
11.5.17	vaiṇavā daṇḍā bāhumātrā bhavantīti vijñāyate
11.5.18	audumbaradaṇḍānīty aparam
11.5.19	dvau rukmau rajatasuvarṇau
11.5.20	śatamānau bhavataḥ
11.5.21	mauñjau vedau / tayor anyataraḥ parivāsitaḥ
11.5.22	mauñjīm abhidhānīm / mauñje nidāne / trīṇi mauñjāni viśākhadāmāni
11.5.23	dvayān muñjapralavānapratiśīrṇāgrān
11.5.24	rauhiṇyoḥ piṣṭāny aphalīkṛtānām
11.5.25	kharebhyaḥ sikatāḥ
11.5.26	mauñje pavitre ity ekam / darbhamaye ity aparam
11.6.1	tūṣṇīṃ prokṣaṇīdhānyāṃ prokṣaṇīḥ saṃskṛtya brahmāṇam āmantrayate brahman pravargyeṇa pracariṣyāmaḥ / hotar gharmam abhiṣṭuhi / agnīd rauhiṇau puroḍāśāv adhiśraya / pratiprasthātar vihara / prastotaḥ sāmāni gāyeti
11.6.2	brahmā prasauti yajur yuktaṃ sāmabhirāktavam ity upāṃśūktvom indravantaḥ pracaratety uccaiḥ
11.6.3	api vā pracaratety uccaiḥ sarvam anyad upāṃśu
11.6.4	prasūto brahmaṇā sarvaṃ parigharmyaṃ prokṣati
11.6.5	yamāya tvā // makhāya tvety etair mantrais triḥ prokṣati
11.6.6	abhipūrvaṃ prokṣati
11.6.7	prokṣitāni vyāyātayatīti vijñāyate
11.6.8	athaitāṃ samrāḍāsandīm agreṇāhavanīyaṃ paryāhṛtya purastād rājāsandyāḥ pratiṣṭhāpya tāsyāṃ kṛṣṇājinaṃ prācīnagrīvam uttaralomāstīrya tasminn apracaraṇīyau sahāvīrāv upāvaharati deva puraś cara sadhyāsaṃ tveti
11.6.9	upariṣṭāt kāla eṣa mantro bhavatīty aparam
11.6.10	athaitāṃ methīṃ mayūkhān viśakhadāmānīty ādāyāgreṇa hotāraṃ jaghanena gārhapatyaṃ dakṣiṇayā dvāropaniṣkramya dakṣiṇena dakṣiṇaṃ dvāraṃ methīṃ nihanti hotuḥ samīkṣāyai
11.6.11	etasyaiva dvārasya pūrvasya dvāryāyā dakṣiṇato vatsāya śaṅkuṃ nihanti
11.6.12	etasyaivāparasyai dvāryāyai dakṣiṇato 'jāyai / uttarato 'bhyantaraṃ barkarāya
11.6.13	teṣu trīṇi viśākhadāmāni vyāyātayati
11.6.14	tair etān kāle badhnanti
11.6.15	tataḥ kharān upavapati
11.6.16	uttareṇa gārhapatyam ekam / uttareṇāhavanīyam ekam / uttarapūrvam avāntaradeśaṃ pratyucchiṣṭakharaṃ bāhyato niḥṣecanavantam
11.6.17	evaṃ vyāyātitāny eva bhavanty odvāsanāt
11.7.1	etasmin kāle pratiprasthātā darvihomasaṃskāreṇājyasthālyām ājyaṃ saṃskaroti
11.7.2	naitasya saṃskāro vidyata ity aparam
11.7.3	adhiśrityāgnīdhro rauhiṇau puroḍāśau tūṣṇīm upacaratau
11.7.4	śaphābhyāṃ mahāvīraṃ parigṛhya vedenāparivāsitena bhasma saṃmārṣṭi deva puraś cara sadhyāsaṃ tveti
11.7.5	sruveṇāhavanīye saptaikadāśa vā prāṇāhutīr juhoti prāṇāya svāhā // vyānāya svāheti
11.7.6	athainam ājyenānakti devas tvā savitā madhvānaktv iti
11.7.7	aparasmin khare rājataṃ rukmaṃ nidhāya pṛthivīṃ tapasas trāyasveti pratiṣṭhāpya mahāvīram anyasmai vā pradāya dvayān muñjapralavān ādāya dakṣiṇeṣām agrāṇi gārhapatye pradīpayaty arciṣe tveti
11.7.8	teṣām agrair uttareṣāṃ mulāni śociṣe tveti
11.7.9	teṣāṃ mūlair dakṣiṇeṣāṃ mūlāni jyotiṣe tveti
11.7.10	teṣāṃ mūlair uttareṣām agrāṇi tapase tveti
11.7.11	tān vyatyastān upari rukme nidadhāty arcir asi śocir asīti
11.7.12	dakṣiṇān uttarān karotīti vijñāyate
11.7.13	teṣūpariṣṭān mahāvīraṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati saṃsīdasva mahāṃ asīti
11.7.14	athainam ājyenābhipūrayaty añjanti yaṃ prathayanta iti
11.7.15	adhyadhi mahāvīram asaṃspṛśan yajamānaḥ prājcaṃ prādeśaṃ dhārayamāṇo japaty anādhṛṣyā purastād ity etair mantrair yathārūpam
11.7.16	manor aśvāsi bhūriputrety uttarataḥ pṛthīvim abhimṛśati
11.8.1	siddhyai tveti dhṛṣṭī ādāyādhvaryuḥ pratiprasthātā ca gārhapatyād udīco 'ṅgārān nirūhatas tapo ṣvagne antarāṃ amitrān iti
11.8.2	tair enaṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ paryūhataś citaḥ stha paricita iti
11.8.3	athainaṃ trayodaśabhir vaikaṅkataiḥ paridhibhiḥ paridhattaḥ / mā asīti prāñcāv adhvaryur nidadhāti / pramā asīty udañcau pratiprasthātā
11.8.4	evam evottarairuttarair mantraiḥ paridhattaḥ / pūrveṇapūrveṇādhvaryur uttareṇottareṇa pratiprasthātā
11.8.5	adhvaryur eva dakṣiṇatas trayodaśaṃ nidadhāty antarikṣasyāntardhir asīti
11.8.6	athainaṃ sauvarṇena rukmeṇāpidadhāti divaṃ tapasas trāyasveti
11.8.7	athainam abhimantrayata ābhir gīrbhir iti tisṛbhiḥ
11.8.8	tato dhavitrāṇy ādatte / gāyatram asīti prathamam / traiṣṭubham asīti dvitīyam / jāgatam asīti tṛtīyam
11.8.9	tair trir ūrdhvam upavājayati madhu madhv iti
11.8.10	teṣām ekaṃ pratiprasthātre prayacchaty ekam āgnīdhrāya
11.8.11	agnīdhraprathamās triḥ pradakṣiṇam ūrdhvaṃ dhūnvantaḥ pariyanti
11.8.12	athainaṃ paryupaviśānti purastād adhvaryur dakṣiṇataḥ pratiprasthātottarata āgnīdhraḥ
11.8.13	avyatiṣaṅgaṃ dhūnvantaḥ praṇavaiḥ saṃrādhayanta indhānāḥ samañjanta āsate
11.8.14	prajvalite rukmam apādatta iti vijñāyate
11.8.15	yatrābhijanati yābhir vartikāṃ grasitām amuñjatam iti tad adhvaryur mahāvīram āmantrayate daśa prācīrdaśa bhāsi dakṣiṇā ity anuvākena
11.8.16	yatrābhijānāty apnasvatīm aśvinā vācam asma iti tad upottiṣṭhann adhvaryur āha rucito gharma iti
11.8.17	tato 'dhvaryuprathamās trir anabhidhūnvantaḥ pratipariyanti
11.8.18	dhavitrāṇy ādāya pratiprasthātre prayacchati
11.8.19	tat pratiprasthātāgreṇāhavanīyaṃ paryāhṛtya samrāḍāsandyāṃ nidadhāti
11.8.20	athālokam avasthāya sarva ṛtvijo yajamānaś cādhīyanto mahāvīram avekṣante 'paśyaṃ gopām iti
11.8.21	anuvākaśeṣaṃ tu pratiprasthātā pariśrite patnīṃ vācayati tvaṣṭīmatī te sapeyeti
11.9.1	tataḥ saṃpreṣyaty agnīd rauhiṇau puroḍāśāv āsādayeti
11.9.2	aniṣṭubdhayoḥ srucor upastīrṇābhighāritau puroḍāśāv āsādayati
11.9.3	dakṣiṇaṃ paridhisaṃdhim anv ekam / uttaraṃ paridhisaṃdhim anv itaram
11.9.4	sāvitreṇa raśanām ādāya pūrvasyā dvāropaniṣkramya trir upāṃśu gharmadughmāhvāyatīḍa ehy adita ehi sarasvaty ehīti
11.9.5	pratyetya dogdhre nidāne ity ādāya dakṣiṇayā dvāropaniṣkramya trir uccair asāv ehy asāv ehīti yathānamā bhavati
11.9.6	adityā uṣṇīṣam asīti raśanayā gharmadugham abhidadhāti / vāyur asy aiḍa iti vatsam
11.9.7	puṣā tvopāvasṛjatv ity upāvasṛjati
11.9.8	yas te stanaḥ śaśaya iti gharmadugham abhimantrayate
11.9.9	usra gharmaṃ śiṃṣeti nidāya vatsam upasīdati bṛhaspatis tvopasīdatv iti
11.9.10	dānavaḥ stha perava iti stanān saṃmṛśati
11.9.11	varṣīyasi dogdhre dogdhāśvibhyāṃ pinvasva sarasvatyai pinvasveti
11.9.12	tūṣṇīṃ pratiprasthātā hrasīyasyājām
11.9.13	agnīdhe payasī pradāya pūrvāv atidrutya śaphopayamān ādadāte / gāyatro 'sīti prathamam / traiṣṭubho 'sīti dvitīyam / jāgatam asīty upayamanaṃ pratiprasthātā
11.9.14	yatrābhijānāty uttiṣṭha brahmaṇaspata iti tad āgnīdhra upottiṣṭhati
11.9.15	yatrābhijānāty upadrava payasā godhugoṣam iti tat paya āharati
11.9.16	āhriyamāṇam abhimantrayate sahorjo bhāgenopa meha iti
11.9.17	indrāśvinā madhunaḥ sāradhasyeti mahāvīre gopaya ānayati
11.9.18	svāhā tvā sūryasya raśmaye vṛṣṭavinaye juhomīty uṣmāṇam udyantam abhimantrayate
11.9.19	madhu havir asīty ajāpayaḥ
11.10.1	ajāpayasa eke pūrvam ānayanaṃ samāmananti
11.10.2	dyāvāpṛthivībhyāṃ tvā parigṛhṇāmīti śaphābhyāṃ mahāvīraṃ parigṛhya vedena parivāsitena bhasma pramṛjya pratiprasthātopayamenopayacchaty antarikṣeṇa tvopayacchāmīti
11.10.3	devānāṃ tvā pitṝṇām anumato bhartuṃ śakeyam ity udyamya harati tejo 'si tejo 'nu prehīti
11.10.4	gacchann evānavānaṃ pañca vātanāmāni vyācaṣṭe samudrasya tvā vātāya svāheti
11.10.5	apānya pañcottarāṇy agnaye tvā vasumate svāheti
11.10.6	etasmin kāle pratiprasthātā dakṣiṇaṃ rauhiṇaṃ srucā pratiṣṭhitaṃ juhoty ahar jyotiḥ ketunā juṣatāṃ sujyotir jyotiṣāṃ svāheti
11.10.7	dakṣiṇātikrāmann adhvaryur brāhmaṇam īkṣate viśvā āśā dakṣiṇasad iti
11.10.8	viśvān devān ayāḍ iheti hotāram
11.10.9	svāhākṛtasya gharmasyeti gharmam abhimantryāśrāvya pratyāśrāvite saṃpreṣyati gharmasya yajeti
11.10.10	vaṣaṭkṛte juhoty aśvinā gharmaṃ pātam iti
11.10.11	anuvaṣaṭkṛte dvitīyaṃ svāhendrā vaḍ iti
11.10.12	hutaṃ yajamāno 'numantrayate gharmapātam aśvinety anuvākaśeṣeṇa
11.10.13	athainam upary āhavanīye dhārayan śṛtadadhnābhipūrayati
11.10.14	vikṣarantam abhimantrayata iṣe pīpihy ūrje pīpihīti
11.10.15	athainaṃ diśo 'nuprahāvayati / tviṣyai tveti purastāt / dyumnāya tveti dakṣiṇataḥ / indrāya tveti paścāt / bhūtyai tvety uttarataḥ
11.10.16	pratyākramyopayamane śeṣam ānīyāntarvedy upayamanaṃ nidhāya pūrvasmin khare rājataṃ rukmaṃ nidhāya mahāvīraṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati
11.11.1	dharmāsi sudharmā me nyasme brahmāṇi dhārayeti
11.11.2	kṣatrāṇi dhārayeti rājanasya / viśaṃ dhārayeti vaiśyasya
11.11.3	net tvā vātaḥ skandayād iti
11.11.4	yady abhicared amuṣya tvā prāṇe sādayāmy amunā saha nirarthaṃ gaccheti brūyād yaṃ dviṣyat
11.11.5	atra pratiprasthātā pūrvavad uttaraṃ rauhiṇaṃ juhoti
11.11.6	upayamane 'ñjan śakalān ādadhāti pūṣṇe śarase svāhety etaiḥ pratimantram
11.11.7	ṣaṣṭhaṃ śakalaṃ sarveṣu lepeṣv aktvānanvīkṣamāṇa udañcaṃ nirasyati rudrāya rudrahotre svāheti
11.11.8	apa upaspṛśati
11.11.9	purastād rauhiṇahomāc chakalān eke samāmananti
11.11.10	tūṣṇīṃ kāṇṭakīṃ samidham ādhāya tūṣṇīm agnihotraṃ juhoti
11.11.11	bhūḥ svāheti vā
11.11.12	upayamane śeṣaṃ samupahūya bhakṣayanti / hotāgre 'thādhvaryur atha brahmātha pratiprasthātāthāgnīdhro 'tha yajamānaḥ
11.11.13	sarve pratyakṣam / api vā yajamāna eva pratyakṣam avaghreṇetare
11.11.14	hutaṃ havir madhu havir iti bhakṣayitvopayamanaṃ pratiprasthātre prayacchati
11.11.15	tat pratiprasthātocchiṣṭakhare mārjayitvāntarvedy upayamanaṃ nidhāya tasmin rājatasuvarṇau rukmāv avadhāya madantīr ānīyottamenānuvākena śāntiṃ kṛtvā ninīyāpa upayamane sarvaṃ parigharmyaṃ samavadhāya saṃpreṣyati
11.12.1	gharmāya saṃsādyamānāyānubrūhīti
11.12.2	ā yasmin sapta vāsavā ity abhijñāyāgreṇāhavanīyaṃ prayāhṛtya samrāḍāsandyāṃ sādayati / svāhā tvā sūryasya raśmibhya iti prātaḥ / svāha tvā nakṣatrebhya iti sāyam
11.12.3	yatrābhijānāty adbhi tṛṇam aghniye viśvadānīm iti tad gām avasṛjati
11.12.4	evam eva sāyaṃprātaḥ pravargyeṇa pracarati
11.12.5	tryupasatke ṣaṭkṛtvaḥ ṣaḍupasatke dvādaśakṛtvo dvādaśopasatke caturviṃśatikṛtvaḥ
11.12.6	etāvan nānā
11.12.7	uttareṇa mantreṇa sāyaṃ rauhiṇaṃ juhoti
11.12.8	apīparo māhno rātriyai mā pāhīti sāyaṃ kāṇṭakīṃ samidham ādadhāti / apīparo mā rātriyā ahno mā pāhīti prātaḥ
11.12.9	agnir jyotir jyotir agniḥ svāheti sāyam agnihotraṃ juhoti / sūryo jyotir jyotiḥ sūryaḥ svāheti prātaḥ
11.12.10	saṃsṛṣṭhomaṃ vā
11.12.11	agniṣṭome pravṛṇakti
11.12.12	nokthye pravṛñjyāt
11.12.13	viśvajiti sarvapṛṣṭhe pravṛṇakti
11.12.14	na prathamayajñe pravṛñjyāt
11.12.15	pravṛñjyād vā
11.12.16	yo 'nūcānaḥ śrotriyas tasya pravṛñjyāt
11.12.17	pravṛñjyād durbrāhmaṇasya
11.12.18	brahmavarcasakāmasyety ekeṣām
11.12.19	taṃ pravṛjya saṃvatsaraṃ na māṃsam aśnīyān na rāmām upeyān na mṛnmayena piben nāsya rāma ucchiṣṭaṃ pibet
11.12.20	teja eva tat saṃśyatīti vijñāyate
11.13.1	pravargyam udvāsayiṣyann ajām agnīdhe dadāti paṣṭhauhīṃ brahmaṇe dhenuṃ hotre rukmāv adhvaryave
11.13.2	samopyāparaṃ kharaṃ pūrvasmin khare nivapati
11.13.3	athaitāṃ samrāḍāsandīm uttareṇāhavanīyaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya tasyāṃ sarvaṃ parigharmyaṃ samavadadhāti
11.13.4	audumbaryāṃ sruci caturgṛhītaṃ gṛhītvāhavanīye tisra āhutīr juhoti gharma yā te divi śug ity etair mantraiḥ
11.13.5	api vā pratiprasthātā trīn saṃnakhān śalākām uṣṭīnādāya teṣām ekam āhavanīye pradīpyāsyadaghne dharayati / tam adhvaryur abhijuhoti gharma yā te divi śug iti
11.13.6	tasminn aparaṃ pradīpyāhavanīye pūrvaṃ prahṛtya nābhidaghne dhārayati / tam adhvaryur abhijuhoti gharma yā te antarikṣe śug iti
11.13.7	tasminn aparaṃ pradīpyāhavanīye pūrvaṃ prahṛtya jānudaghne dhārayati / tam adhvaryur abhijuhoti gharma yā te pṛthivyāṃ śug iti
11.13.8	āhavanīya evainam anupraharati
11.13.9	etasmin kāle pratiprasthātā pariśrite patnīm udānayaty anu no 'dyām anumatir iti
11.13.10	anv id anumate tvam ity upaniṣkrāmanti
11.13.11	āharanti methīm / anuharanti mayūkhān / ādadate kharau
11.13.12	dakṣiṇata ucchiṣṭakharaṃ pariharati
11.13.13	athaitasyāḥ samrāḍāsandyā dvāv antarvedi pādau dvau bahirvedi pratiṣṭhāpya saṃpreṣyati prastotaḥ sāmānigāyeti
11.13.14	saha patnyā triḥ sāmno nidhanam upayanti
11.13.15	ardhādhve dvitīyam / apareṇottarvediṃ tṛtīyam
11.13.16	divas tvā paraspāyā iti prathame 'bhipravrajanti / brahmaṇas tvā paraspāyā iti dvitīye / prāpaṇasya tvā paraspāyā iti tṛtīye
11.14.1	athaitāṃ samrāḍāsandīm uttareṇottaravediṃ pratiṣṭhāpya saṃpreṣyati prastotar vārṣāharaṃ sāma gaya / iṣṭāhotrīyaṃ sāma gāyeti
11.14.2	iṣṭāhotrīyasya sāmno nidhanam upayanti na vārṣāharasya
11.14.3	yady upariṣṭāt pariṣiñcet tatra vārṣāharaṃ codayet
11.14.4	udakumbham ādāya pradakṣiṇam uttaravediṃ triḥ pariṣiñcan paryeti valgur asi śaṃyudhāyā iti
11.14.5	trir apariṣiñcan pratiparyeti śaṃ ca vakṣi pari ca vakṣīti
11.14.6	catuḥsraktir nābhir ṛtasyety uttaravedim abhimṛśyottareṇottaranābhiṃ kharau nyupyānuvyūhati sado viśvāyur iti
11.14.7	mārjalīyadeśe ucchiṣṭakharaṃ nivapaty apa dveṣo apa hvara iti
11.14.8	apa upaspṛśyottareṇottaranābhiṃ khare hiraṇyaṃ nidhāya tasmin pracaraṇīyaṃ mahāvīram upāvahṛtyetarāv upāvaharati pūrvāparau dakṣiṇottarau vā
11.14.9	athaitasmin pracaraṇīye gopaya ānayati mahīnāṃ payo 'si vihitaṃ devatreti
11.14.10	jyotirbhā asi vanaspatīnām oṣadhīnāṃ rasa iti madhu
11.14.11	vājinaṃ tvā vājino 'vanayāma iti dadhi
11.14.12	evam eva dvitīyaṃ pūrayaty evaṃ tṛtīyam
11.14.13	api vājyam eva prathama ānayen madhu dvitīye dadhi tṛtīye
11.14.14	gharmaitat te 'nnam etat purīṣam iti dadhnā madhumiśreṇa yāny āsecanavanti tāni pūrayati
11.14.15	abhyukṣatītarāṇy ariktatāyai
11.14.16	ādityākṛtiṃ karoti
11.15.1	atha yadi puruṣākṛtiṃ cikīrṣed atraivetarāv upāvahṛtya śiraso rūpaṃ karoti
11.15.2	upariṣṭān mauñjavedam pracchinnāgraṃ śikhāyai rūpam
11.15.3	hiraṇyaśakalāv ājyasruvau vākṣyo rūpam
11.15.4	sruvau nāsikayo rūpam
11.15.5	dogdhre karṇayo rūpam
11.15.6	prokṣaṇīdhānīṃ mukhasya rūpam
11.15.7	ājyasthālīṃ grīvāṇāṃ rūpam
11.15.8	dhṛṣṭī jatrūṇāṃ rūpam
11.15.9	śaphāv aṃsayo rūpam
11.15.10	rauhiṇahavanyau bāhvo rūpam
11.15.11	daśaudumbarīḥ samidho 'ṅgulīnāṃ rūpam
11.15.12	prācīṃ methīṃ pṛṣṭīnāṃ rūpam
11.15.13	abhito dhavitre pārśvayo rūpam
11.15.14	madhye tṛtīyam uraso rūpam
11.15.15	madhya upayamanam udarasya rūpam
11.15.16	tasmin sarvaṃ rajjumayaṃ samavadadhāty āntrāṇāṃ rūpam
11.15.17	paścād abhriṃ tiraścīṃ śroṇyo rūpam
11.15.18	abhitaḥ śaṅkū sakthyo rūpam
11.15.19	madhye tṛtīyaṃ meḍhrasya rūpam
11.15.20	rauhiṇakapāle pārṣṇyo rūpam
11.15.21	daśaudumbarīḥ samidho 'ṅgulīnāṃ rūpam
11.15.22	rauhiṇapiṣṭaśeṣam abhidhvaṃsayati majjānāṃ rūpam
11.15.23	upariṣṭān mauñjavedaṃ visrasya nidadhāti snāvnāṃ rūpam
11.15.24	avakābhir dhūpatṛṇair iti pracchādayati māṃsasya rūpam
11.15.25	dadhnā madhumiśreṇāvokṣati lohitasya rūpam
11.15.26	kṛṣṇājinena prācīnagrīveṇottaralomnā pracchādayati tvaco lomnāṃ rūpam
11.15.27	upariṣṭāt samrāḍāsandīṃ visrasya nidadhāti / sāmrājyasya rūpaṃ karoti
11.16.1	uttaravedyām udvāsayet tejaskāmasya / uttaravedyām annādyakāmasya
11.16.2	puro vā paścād vodavasayet
11.16.3	nadīdvīpa udvāsayet
11.16.4	yadi nadīdvīpa udvāsayen na pariṣiñcet
11.16.5	yaṃ dviṣyād yatra sa syāt tasyāṃ diśyaudumbaryāṃ śākhāyām udvāsayed idam aham amuṣyāmuṣyāyaṇasya śucā prāṇam apidahāmīti
11.16.6	śucaivāsya prāṇam apidahati / tājag ārtim ārchatīti vijñāyate
11.16.7	yatra darbhā upadīkasaṃtatāḥ syus tad udvāsayed vṛṣṭikāmasya
11.16.8	uttaravedyāṃ nityaṃ kalpaṃ bruvate
11.16.9	nainam udvāsitaṃ vayāṃsi paryāsīrann āgneḥ praṇayanāt
11.16.10	atraike pariṣecanaṃ samāmananti
11.16.11	athainam upatiṣṭhante rantir nāmāsi divyo gandharva iti pratipadya saha prajayā saha rāyaspoṣeṇety antena
11.16.12	mārjālīyadeśa ucchiṣṭakhare mārjayante sumitrā na āpa oṣadhayaḥ santv iti
11.16.13	ud vayaṃ tamasas parīty ādityam upasthāyod u tyam // citram iti dvābhyāṃ gārhapatye hutvopatiṣṭhanta imam ū ṣu tyam asmabhyam iti
11.17.1	yadi gharmaḥ skanded askān dyauḥ pṛthivīm iti dvābhyām enam abhimantrayeta
11.17.2	yadi gharmaḥ caratsu vidyud āpated yā purastād vidyud āpatad ity etair yathāliṅgaṃ juhuyāt
11.17.3	atha yadi sarvataḥ sarvā juhuyāt
11.17.4	athaitāni gharmaprayaścittāni juhoti prāṇāya svāhā // pūṣṇe svāhety anuvākābhyām
11.17.5	gharmeṣṭakām upadadhāty ud asya śuṣmād bhānur ity anuvākena
11.17.6	kulāyinīṃ yās te agne ārdrā yonaya ity anuvākena
11.17.7	saṃcitam agnim aiḍikyābhimṛśaty agnir asi vaiśvānaro 'sīty anuvākena
11.17.8	bhūr bhuvaḥ suva iti sarvaprāyaścittāni
11.17.9	yadi mahāvīraḥ padyetordhva ū ṣu ṇa ūtaya iti dvābhyām enam ucchrayet
11.17.10	yadi bhidyeta vidhuṃ dadrāṇam iti saṃdhāya yāni dṛḍhārthe saṃśleṣaṇāni tair enam abhidihyed yad anyan māṣebhyo māṃsāc ca yad ṛte cid abhiśriṣa iti
11.17.11	yady apracaraṇīyaḥ saṃpadyetānyasmai sthānam apidadhyāt
11.17.12	yadi gharmam atiparīyuḥ na vā pratiparīyuḥ punar ūrjā // saha rayyety etābhyām enaṃ pratiparīyuḥ
11.18.1	athaitāni gharme vyathite prāyaścittāni juhoti mā no gharma vyathito vivyatho na ity aṣṭau
11.18.2	yadi gharmeṇa caratsv ādityo 'stamiyād aparasyāṃ dvāri darbheṇa hiraṇyaṃ prabadhyod vayaṃ tamasas parīty upasthāyod u tyam // citram iti dvābhyāṃ gārhapatye hutvā pravṛjya śvo bhūta ādityam upatiṣṭhate vayaḥ suparṇā ity etayā
11.18.3	dadhigharmaṃ bhakṣayanti bhūr bhuvaḥ suva ity anuvākena
11.18.4	yadi gharmadhug dohanakāle nāgacched anyāṃ dugdhvā pravṛjya tāṃ sutyāyāṃ brāhmaṇāya dadyāt
11.18.5	yadi gharmadudhi payo na syād dṛteś caturthaṃ pādaṃ stanaṃ kṛtvā pinvayet
11.18.6	yadi dadhi duhīta bārhaspatyaṃ śaṃset / yadi paya āśvinaṃ sodarkam
11.18.7	yadi lohitaṃ duhyetānyad vā vivarṇam anvāhāryapacanaṃ pariśrityāgnaye rudravate svāheti juhuyāt
11.18.8	yadi niṣīded dhātur ṛgbhyāṃ juhuyāt
11.18.9	yady amedhyam ayajñiyaṃ vābhyupaviśed āgnivāruṇyarcā juhuyāt / āgneyya vā
11.18.10	yady enāṃ vayo 'bhivikṣiped vāyavyarcā juhuyāt
11.18.11	yady ud vā patet pra vā mīyeta saṃ vā śīryeta śārdūlo vā hanyād arkakṣīram ajākṣīra āścotya pracaret
11.19.1	athātaḥ sutyāyāṃ pravṛñjanam
11.19.2	yadi purastād aruṇā syād atha pravṛjyaḥ
11.19.3	upakāśa upavyuṣaṃ samayāviṣita uditānudita udite vā
11.19.4	prātaḥ saṃgave vā
11.19.5	mādhyaṃdine vā pavamāne stute
11.19.6	sakṛd evāgnīdhre pravṛjya iti vijñāyate
11.19.7	tāny etāni pravṛñjanāny aupasadaiḥ pravṛñjanair vikaplperan
11.19.8	vyākhyātā ghorās tanvaḥ / araṇye 'nuvākyaś ca gaṇa uttarau cānuvākau
11.19.9	yadi gharmeṇa caratsv ekasṛka uttiṣṭhed vi gā vicaran spāśayasvety enam abhimantrayate
11.19.10	ubhayata ādīpyolmukam asmai pratyasyed agne agninā saṃvadasveti
11.19.11	athainam abhimantrayate sakṛt te agne nama ity anuvākaśeṣeṇa
11.19.12	yadi gṛdhraḥ sālāvṛkī bhayeḍako dīrghamukhyulūko bhūtopasṛṣṭaḥ śakunir vā vaded asṛṅmukhaḥ // yad etat // yad īṣitaḥ // dīrghamukhi // itthāk ulūkaḥ // yad etad bhūtāny anvāviśya // prasārya sakthyāv ity etair yathāliṅgam abhimantryolmukapratyasanādi samānam
11.20.1	yadi gharmadhuk krimīṇā syād atriṇā tvā krime hanmīty anuvākenāsyāḥ krimīn hanyāt
11.20.2	api vā sārvatrikam evaitat prāyaścittaṃ kriyeta
11.20.3	yam abhicaret tasya lohitam avadānaṃ juhuyād āharāvadya śṛtasyety anuvākena
11.20.4	yam abhivyāhariṣyan syāt trirātrāvaraṃ brahmacaryaṃ caritvā gatvainam abhiyāhared brahmaṇā tvā śapāmīty anuvākena
11.20.5	yaṃ dviṣyāt tasya goṣṭhaṃ gatvā svajam oṣadhīṃ nikhaned uttuda śimijāvarīty anuvākena
11.20.6	api vā goṣṭhasyaiva dakṣiṇāṃ dvārasthūṇāṃ vicālayet
11.20.7	yadi udgātā puruṣasāma na gāyet svayam evādhvaryur udgāyed bhūr bhuvaḥ suva ity anuvākena
11.21.1	athāto 'nvāntaradīkṣāṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
11.21.2	parvaṇy udgayan āpūryamāṇapakṣe puṇye nakṣatre 'parāhṇe keśaśmaśru vāpayitvā prācīṃ vodīcīṃ vā diśam upaniṣkramya khile 'chadir deśe 'gnim upasamādhāya saṃparistīrya pūrvavad upākṛtya madantīr upaspṛśya prathamenānuvākenaśāntiṃ kṛtvā catasra audumbarīḥ samidho ghṛtānvaktā ādadhāti pṛthivī samid ity etair mantraiḥ
11.21.3	atha devatā upatiṣṭhate 'gne vratapate vrataṃ cariṣyāmīti
11.21.4	athainaṃ sarveṣām anuvākānāṃ prabhṛtīr abhivyāhārayati / prathamottamayor vā
11.21.5	uttamenānuvākena śāntiṃ kṛtvā saṃmīlati vācaṃ ca yacchati
11.21.6	athāsyāhatena vāsasā śiraḥ saṃmukhaṃ veṣṭayitvāstam ite grāmaṃ prapādayati
11.21.7	vāgyata etāṃ rātriṃ tiṣṭhaty āste vā
11.21.8	śvo bhūte khile 'chadirdarśe 'gnim upasamādhāya saṃparistīryāthāsya ṣaṭtayam abhividarśayati / saptatayam ity eke / agnim ādityam udakumbham aśmanaṃ vatsaṃ mahānagnāṃ hiraṇyaṃ saptamam
11.21.9	api vāditas trīṇy abhividarśayati / yathopapātam itarāṇy abhividarśayati
11.21.10	tata ādityam upatiṣṭhate vayaḥ suparṇā ity etayā
11.21.11	atraitad vāso gurave dattvā
11.21.12	athāsya brahmacaryam adhi
11.21.13	nitye
11.21.14	na naktaṃ bhuñjīta
11.21.15	yadi bhuñjītāpajvalitaṃ bhuñjīta
11.21.16	na mṛnmayaṃ pratidhayīta
11.21.17	na striyā na śūdreṇa vā saṃbhāṣeta
11.21.18	na cakrīvad ārohet
11.21.19	nopānahau na chatraṃ dhārayīta
11.21.20	na samājam īkṣeta na harmyāṇi na śarīrāṇi na śavaṃ nāntāvasāyinam
11.22.1	aṣṭamyāṃ parvaṇi copavasati vāgyataḥ
11.22.2	na ca saṃviśet
11.22.3	saṃvatsaram etad vrataṃ caret
11.22.4	etasminn eva saṃvatsare 'dhīyīta
11.22.5	yady etasmin saṃvatsare nādhīyīta yāvad adhyayanam etad vrataṃ caret
11.22.6	saṃvatsarasya parastāt khile 'chadirdarśe 'gnim upasamādhāya saṃparistīrya pūrvavad visṛjyāvṛttair mantraiḥ samidha ādhāyāvṛtair devatā upasthāyātra gurave varaṃ dattvā keśaśmaśru vāpayate
11.22.7	athāsya svādhyāyam adhi
11.22.8	nitye
11.22.9	nānutsṛṣṭādhyāyo 'dhīyīta na naktaṃ nābhidoṣam abrahmacaryam āpadya na māṃsaṃ khāditvā na keśaśmaśru vāpayitvā na lomāni kārayitvā na nakhāni na dataḥ prakṣālya
11.22.10	nākto nābhyakto nārdro nārdre nānavavṛṣṭe na haritayavān prekṣamāṇaḥ
11.22.11	na grāmyasya paśor ante nāraṇyasya nāpāṃ nābhre na chāyāyāṃ na paryāvṛtta āditye
11.22.12	nāśṛṭam utpatitaṃ na lohitaṃ dṛṣṭvā na harmyāṇi na śarīrāṇi na śavaṃ nāntāvasāyinam
11.22.13	khile 'chadirdarśe 'gnim upasamādhāya saṃparistīryāpareṇāgniṃ darbheṣv āsīno darbhān dūrvā vā dhārayamāṇaḥ parācīnam adhīyīta
11.22.14	varaṃ vā dattvaupāsane
11.22.15	adhyeṣyamāṇaḥ prathamenānuvākena śāntiṃ kṛtvādhīyīta
11.22.16	adhītya cottamena
11.22.17	adhīyāno nānyā vāco vadet
11.22.18	yatra kva cāśāntiṃ kṛtaṃ paśyet punar eva śāntiṃ kṛtvādhīyīta
11.22.19	pravargyāyopaniṣkramya nāpratipraviśyānyad adhīyītānyad adhīyīta
12.1.1	yadātithyāyā dhrauvam ājyaṃ tat kaṃse camase vā pañcagṛhītaṃ tānūnaptraṃ samavadyaty āpataye tvā gṛhṇāmīty etair mantraiḥ
12.1.2	tad yajamānasaptadaśā ṛtvijaḥ saṃmṛśanti yajamānapañcamā vā mahartvijo 'nādhṛṣṭam asy anādhṛṣyaṃ devānām ojo 'bhiśastipā anabhiśastenyam iti
12.1.3	anu me dīkṣāṃ dīkṣāpatir manyatām iti yajamāno 'vamṛśati
12.1.4	tad yajamānas trir avajighret prajāpatau tvā manasi juhomīti
12.1.5	api vānvaham ekaikasmin vrate pratinayet
12.1.6	tataḥ saṃpreṣyaty agnīn madanty āpā3 iti
12.1.7	madanti devīr amṛtā ṛtāvṛdha ity āgnīdhraḥ
12.1.8	tābhir ādravety adhvaryuḥ
12.1.9	madantībhir mārjayitvā visrasya rājānaṃ sahiraṇyaiḥ pāṇibhir āpyāyayanti ye tānūnaptraṃ samavamṛśanty aṃśur aṃśus te deva somāpyāyatām iti pratipadya svasti te deva soma sutyām aśīyety antena
12.1.10	dakṣiṇe vedyante prastare nihnavante dakṣiṇān uttānān pāṇīn kṛtvā savyān nīca eṣṭā rāyaḥ preṣe bhagāyeti
12.1.11	tataḥ saṃpreṣyati subrahmaṇya subrahmaṇyām āhvayeti
12.1.12	evam eva sarvāsu subrahmaṇyāsu saṃpreṣyati
12.1.13	subrahmaṇyāyāṃ yajamānaṃ vācayati sāsi subrahmaṇye tasyās te dyauḥ pādaḥ / sāsi subrahmaṇye tasyās te diśaḥ pādaḥ / parorajās te pañcamaḥ pādaḥ / sā na iṣam ūrjaṃ dhukṣva teja indriyaṃ brahmavarcasam annādyam iti
12.1.14	evam eva sarvāsu subrahmaṇyāsu yajamānaṃ vācayati
12.2.1	tato 'vāntaradīkṣām upaiti
12.2.2	dakṣiṇatas tiṣṭhann āhavanīyam abhimantrayate 'gne vratapate tvaṃ vratānāṃ vratapatir asīti
12.2.3	saṃtarāṃ mekhalāṃ samāyacchate
12.2.4	saṃtarāṃ muṣṭiṃ karṣate
12.2.5	taptavrato bhavati
12.2.6	madantībhir mārjayate
12.2.7	yā te agne rudriyā tanūr iti vratayati
12.2.8	yad ātithyāyā barhis tad upasadāṃ tad agnīṣomīyasya / tad eva prastaraparidhīti vijñāyate
12.2.9	pravargyeṇa pracaryopasadas tantraṃ prakramayati / upasadā vā pūrvam
12.2.10	tat stīrṇam eva barhir bhavati / tat parihitāḥ paridhayaḥ
12.2.11	daśadārum idhmaṃ karoti
12.2.12	vedaṃ kṛtvāgnīn paristīrya hastāv avanijya pātrāṇi prayujyolaparājīṃ stīrtvā pavitre kṛtvā saṃpreṣyati yajamāna vācaṃ yaccheti
12.2.13	vāgyataḥ pātrāṇi saṃmṛśati
12.2.14	prokṣaṇīḥ saṃskṛtya brahmāṇam āmantrya pātrāṇi prokṣya haviṣkṛtā vācaṃ visṛjya barhiṣo darbhān eva stambayajur harati
12.2.15	sphyaṃ stabdhvā saṃpreṣyati prokṣaṇīr āsādayedhmam upasādaya sruvaṃ ca srucaś ca saṃmṛḍḍhy ājyenodehīti
12.2.16	samānam ājyānāṃ grahaṇāt
12.2.17	dhruvāyām eva gṛhṇāti
12.2.18	prokṣaṇīr abhimantrya brahmāṇam āmantryedhmaṃ vediṃ ca prokṣya prokṣaṇyavaśeṣaṃ ninīyāgnim abhimantrya pūrvām āghārasamidham ādhāyāntarvedi dhruvāṃ sādayitvā sruvaṃ sādayati / eṣāsadad iti mantraṃ saṃnamati
12.2.19	viṣṇv asi vaiṣṇavaṃ dhāma prājāpatyam ity ājyam abhimantrayate
12.3.1	agreṇa dhruvāṃ vedaṃ sādayitvā sāmidhenībhyaḥ saṃpreṣyati
12.3.2	nava sāmidhenyo bhavanti
12.3.3	srauvam āghāram āghārya saṃpreṣyaty agnīt paridhīṃś cāgniṃ ca tris triḥ saṃmṛḍḍhīti
12.3.4	samānam ā pravarāt
12.3.5	āśrāvyāha sīda hotar iti
12.3.6	etāvān pravaraḥ
12.3.7	yatrābhijānāti ghṛtavatīm adhvaryo srucam āsyasveti tad dhruvāyā gṛhṇāty aṣṭagṛhītaṃ juhvāṃ caturgṛhītam upabhṛti
12.3.8	gṛhṇan saṃpreṣyaty agnaye 'nubrūhīti
12.3.9	atyākramyāśrāvyāhāgniṃ yajeti
12.3.10	vaṣaṭkṛte 'rdhaṃ juhvā juhoti
12.3.11	apunaratikrāman saṃpreṣyati somāyānubrūhīti
12.3.12	āśrāvyāha somaṃ yajeti
12.3.13	vaṣaṭkṛte sarvaṃ juhoti
12.3.14	atraiva tiṣṭhan saṃpreṣyati viṣṇave 'nubrūhīti
12.3.15	juhvām aupabhṛtaṃ paryāsicyāśrāvyāha viṣṇuṃ yajeti
12.3.16	vaṣaṭkṛte juhoti
12.3.17	pratyākramya sruveṇopasadaṃ juhoti yā te agne 'yāśayā tanūr ity etām
12.3.18	yadi puro yudhyeyur ayaḥ prathamāyām avadhāya juhuyād rajataṃ madhyamāyāṃ haritam uttamāyām iti vijñāyate
12.3.19	yadi saṃgrāmaṃ yudhyeyur ity ekeṣām
12.3.20	upasadaṃ hutvā tathaiva rājānam āpyāyayanti tathā nihnavante
12.3.21	athopasadā caranti
12.3.22	tataḥ saṃpreṣyaty agnīd devapatnīr vyācakṣva subrahmaṇya subrahmaṇyām āhvayeti
12.3.23	apareṇa gārhapatyam upaviśyāgnīdhro devapatnīr vyācaṣṭe senendrasyety etam anuvākam
12.3.24	āhvayati subrahmaṇyaḥ subrahmaṇyām
12.3.25	saṃtiṣṭhata upasat
12.4.1	svaparāhṇa āparāhṇikībhyāṃ pravargyopasadbhyāṃ pracaranti
12.4.2	ayāśayām eva juhoti
12.4.3	etāvan nānā / yāḥ prātaryājyāḥ syus tāḥ sāyaṃ puronuvākyāḥ kuryāt / yāḥ puronuvākyās tā yājyāḥ
12.4.4	savyān uttānān pāṇīn kṛtvā nihnavante dakṣiṇān nīcaḥ
12.4.5	catuḥstanaṃ madhyarātre vratayati
12.4.6	jāgarty etāṃ rātrim
12.4.7	supūrvāhṇe paurvāhṇikībhyāṃ pravargyopasadbhyāṃ pracaranti
12.4.8	rajāśayām atropasadaṃ juhoti
12.4.9	saṃsthitāyām upasadi mahāvediṃ vimimīte vimime tvā payasvatīṃ devānāṃ dhenuṃ sudughām anapasphurantīm / indraḥ somaṃ pibatu kṣemo astu na iti
12.4.10	agreṇa prāgvaṃśaṃ trīn prācaḥ prakramān prakramya śaṅkuṃ nihanti
12.4.11	sa vedeḥ paścārdhyaḥ śaṅkuḥ
12.4.12	tataḥ ṣaṭtriṃśataṃ prācaḥ prakramān prakramya śaṅkuṃ nihanti
12.4.13	sa yūpāvaṭyaḥ śaṅkuḥ
12.4.14	paścārdhyāc chaṅkoḥ pañcadaśa dakṣiṇā prakramān prakramya pañcadaśottaratas tac chaṅkuṃ nihanti
12.4.15	te śroṇī bhavataḥ
12.4.16	yūpāvaṭyāc chaṅkor dvādaśa dakṣiṇā prakramān prakramya dvādaśottaratas tac chaṅkuṃ nihanti
12.4.17	tāv aṃsau bhavataḥ
12.4.18	athainam akṣṇayā pramāṇena pramāya spandyayā paryātanoti
12.4.19	anvātanoti pṛṣṭhyām
12.4.20	athaināṃ sphyena vighanena parśvā paraśuneti kurvanti
12.5.1	athaināṃ darśapaurṇamāsikena saṃskāreṇa saṃskaroti yad anyat saṃnamanāt
12.5.2	yat prāg uttarasmāt parigrahāt tat kṛtvāpareṇa yūpāvaṭadeśaṃ śamyayottaravediṃ parimimīte śamyāmātrīṃ yugamātrīṃ vā / sarvato vā daśapadām
12.5.3	etām uttarasmād vedyaṃsād udañcaṃ prakramaṃ prakramya śaṅkuṃ nihanti
12.5.4	sa cātvālo bhavati
12.5.5	apareṇa cātvālaṃ dvādaśasu prakrameṣu tāvaty udag utkaraḥ
12.5.6	apareṇotkaraṃ ca ṣaṭsv āgnīdhraḥ
12.5.7	antareṇa cātvālotkarau saṃcaro bhavati / antareṇa cātvālaṃ cāgnīdhraṃ cety ekeṣām
12.5.8	yat kiṃ ca vedim anvavahariṣyan syād etenaivānvavaharet
12.5.9	uttaravedyā āvṛtottaravedim upopya prokṣāntāṃ kṛtvaudumbaraśākhābhiś channāṃ parivāsayati
12.5.10	tristanaṃ madhyaṃdine vratayati
12.5.11	svaparāhṇa āparāhṇikībhyāṃ pracaranti
12.5.12	rajāśayām eva juhoti
12.5.13	dvistanaṃ madhyarātre vratayati
12.5.14	supūrvāhṇe paurvāhṇikībhyāṃ pravargyopasadbhyāṃ pracaranti
12.5.15	harāśayām atropasadaṃ juhoti
12.5.16	tadānīm evāparāhṇikībhyāṃ pravargyopasadbhyāṃ pracaranti
12.5.17	harāśayām eva juhoti
12.5.18	ekastanaṃ madhyaṃdine vratayati
12.5.19	saṃtiṣṭhanta upasadaḥ
12.6.1	pravargyam udvāsyāgner āvṛtāgniṃ praṇīyāmikṣāyai dadhigharmāyeti vatsān apākaroti
12.6.2	mitrāvaruṇābhyām ity āmikṣāyām upalakṣayed indraṃ dadhigharme
12.6.3	athādhvaryavo mahāvedikaṃ barhiḥ prabhūtam āharanti yathā darśapūrṇamāsayoḥ
12.6.4	tata uttaraṃ parigrāhaṃ parigṛhṇāti yathā darśapūrṇamāsayoḥ
12.6.5	na parigṛhītām abhicaranty ā prokṣaṇāt
12.6.6	prokṣaṇīnām āvṛtā prokṣaṇīḥ saṃskṛtya brahmāṇam āmantrya vediṃ barhir iti triḥ prokṣati yathā darśapūrṇamāsayoḥ
12.6.7	athaitad barhiḥ sarvasyāṃ mahāvedyāṃ stṛṇanti yathā darśapūrṇamāsayoḥ
12.6.8	ā dhā ye agnim indhate stṛṇanti barhir ānuṣak / yeṣām indro yuvā sakhā // ity etām eke staraṇīṃ samāmananti
12.6.9	apareṇa vedim abhitaḥ prāgvaṃśaṃ havirdhāne samāvartayanti prakṣālite viṣitagranthinī naddhayuge avahitaśamye chadiṣmatī
12.6.10	tata auttaravedika āhutiṃ juhoti yuñjate mana iti
12.6.11	etasminn evāta ūrdhvam āhavanīyakarmāṇi kriyante
12.6.12	patnī padatṛtīyena dakṣiṇasya havirdhānasya dakṣiṇām akṣadhuraṃ prācā hastena triḥ parācīnam upānakty ā no vīro jāyatāṃ karmaṇya iti / nottarām / ubhayata upānaktīty ekeṣām
12.6.13	evam evottarasyopānakti
12.6.14	tataḥ saṃpreṣyati
12.7.1	havirdhānābhyāṃ prohyamāṇābhyām anubrūhīti
12.7.2	trir anūktāyāṃ prathamāyām udgṛhṇantaḥ pravartayanti prācī pretam adhvaraṃ kalpayantīti
12.7.3	yady akṣa utsarjet suvāg deva duryāṃ āvadety etad abhimantrayeta
12.7.4	adhvaryur dakṣiṇasya havirdhānasya dakṣiṇe vartmani hiraṇyam upāsya juhotīdaṃ viṣṇur vi cakrama iti
12.7.5	evaṃ pratiprasthātottarasyottare vartmani hiraṇyam upāsya juhotīrāvatī dhenumatī hi bhūtam iti
12.7.6	tatraiṣo 'tyantapradeśaḥ / yāni dakṣiṇasya karmāṇy adhvaryus tāni kuryād uttarasya pratiprasthātā
12.7.7	vitṛtīyadeśe hotā manasā padā janyaṃ bhayaṃ pratinudaty apa janyaṃ bhayaṃ cakrāṇi vartaya / gṛhaṃ somasya gacchatam // iti / adhvaryur ity ekeṣāṃ brahmety ekeṣāṃ yajamāna ity ekeṣāṃ
12.7.8	apareṇottaravediṃ triṣu prakrameṣv aparimite vābhitaḥ pṛṣṭhyāṃ nabhyasthe sthāpayato 'tra ramethāṃ varṣman pṛthivyā iti
12.7.9	yathārthaṃ havirdhānayor antarālaṃ bhavati
12.7.10	vaiṣṇavam asi viṣṇus tvottabhnātv ity upastabhnītaḥ
12.7.11	purastād unnate bhavataḥ
12.7.12	adhvaryur dakṣiṇasya havirdhānasya dakṣiṇaṃ karṇātardaṃ prati methīṃ nihanti divo vā viṣṇav uta vā pṛthivyā iti
12.7.13	evaṃ pratiprasthātā
12.8.1	uttarasyottaraṃ karṇātardaṃ prati methīṃ nihanti viṣṇor nu kaṃ vīryāṇi pravocam iti
12.8.2	tayor havirdhāne nibadhnīto viṣṇo syūr asīti
12.8.3	viṣṇor dhruvam asīti granthiṃ karoti
12.8.4	yaṃ prathamaṃ granthiṃ grathnīyāt sa prajñātaḥ pariśayīta
12.8.5	paścād upaminvanti
12.8.6	ūrdhvāḥ śamyā udvṛhyopariṣṭāt pariveṣṭayanti
12.8.7	agreṇa havirdhāne sthūṇe nihatya tayor udagagraṃ vaṃśaṃ nidhāya tasmin rarāṭīṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati viṣṇo rarāṭam asīti
12.8.8	rarāṭyāṃ tiryañcaṃ vaṃśaṃ niṣīvyati viṣṇo syūr asīti
12.8.9	viṣṇor dhruvam asīti granthiṃ karoti
12.8.10	yaṃ prathamaṃ granthiṃ grathnīyāt sa prajñātaḥ pariśayīta
12.8.11	viṣṇoḥ pṛṣṭham asīti madhyamaṃ chadir adhinidadhāti
12.8.12	viṣṇo śnaptre stha iti rarāṭyā antau vyavāsyati
12.8.13	kaṭāṃs tejanīr iti pravartam antarāleṣūpāsyati
12.8.14	tān antarvartā ity ācakṣate
12.8.15	pari tvā girvaṇo gira iti pariśrayati
12.8.16	dve dvāre utsṛjanti / pūrvaṃ cāparaṃ ca
12.8.17	śālāmukhīyo hotrīya auttaravedika iti samānaṃ sāṃkāśinaṃ bhavati
12.8.18	dakṣiṇe dvāryāv adhvaryuḥ pariṣīvyaty uttare pratiprasthātā viṣṇo syūr asīti
12.8.19	viṣṇor dhruvam asīti granthiṃ karoti
12.8.20	yaṃ prathamaṃ granthiṃ grathnīyāt sa prajñātaḥ pariśayīta
12.9.1	saṃmitam abhimṛśati vaiṣṇavam asi viṣṇave tveti
12.9.2	saṃmitād yajamānaṃ prāñcam upaniṣkrāmati pra tad viṣṇuḥ stavate vīryāya mṛgo na bhīmaḥ kucaro giriṣṭhāḥ / yasyoruṣu triṣu vikramaṇeṣv adhikṣiyanti bhuvanāni viśvā // iti / triḥ prakrāmayatīti vijñāyate
12.9.3	upaniṣkrāmatīty ekeṣām
12.9.4	prācīnavaṃśaṃ havirdhānaṃ minvanti
12.9.5	prācīnavaṃśam āgnīdhraṃ dakṣiṇādvāram ardham antarvedy ardhaṃ bahirvedi
12.9.6	tiraścīnam udagāyataṃ sadaḥ
12.9.7	tatraiṣo 'tyantapradeśaḥ / na prāṅ havirdhāne atīyād adhvaryuḥ
12.9.8	yady atīyād vaiṣṇavyarcā saṃcaret kṣaitrapatyā vā
12.9.9	na pratyak sado 'tīyāt
12.9.10	yady atīyād aindryarcā saṃcared iti vijñāyate
12.9.11	paścārdhyāc chaṅkos trīn prācaḥ prakramān prakramya audumbarīṃ sarvasya sadaso madhyato minoti
12.9.12	dakṣiṇena pṛṣṭhyāṃ prakrama audumbarīṃ sarvasya sadaso madhyato minoti
12.9.13	navāratni tiryak saptaviṃśatir udagāyatam iti sadaso vijñāyate / aṣṭādaśety ekeṣām
12.9.14	yāvad ṛtvigbhyo dhiṣṇiyebhyaḥ prasarpakebhya āptaṃ manyate tāvat sadaḥ karotīty ekeṣām
12.9.15	sāvitreṇābhrim ādāyaudumbaryā avaṭaṃ parilikhati parilikhitaṃ rakṣaḥ parilikhitā arātaya iti
12.9.16	khātvā yavamatībhiḥ prokṣaṇībhir audumbarīṃ prokṣati / dive tvety agram / antarikṣāya tveti madhyam / pṛthivyai tveti mūlam
12.9.17	apām avanayanaṃ yavasya prāsanaṃ barhiṣo 'vastaraṇam iti yūpo vyākhyātam
12.10.1	prācīnakarṇāṃ sahodgātrocchrayaty ud divaṃ stabhānāntarikṣaṃ pṛṇeti
12.10.2	prācīnakarṇāṃ sahodgātrā minoti dyutānas tvā māruto minotv iti
12.10.3	paryūhaṇaṃ paridṛṃhaṇaṃ pariṣecanam iti yūpe vyākhyātam
12.10.4	athāsyā antareṇa karṇau hiraṇyaṃ nidhāyābhijuhoti ghṛtena dyāvāpṛthivī āpṛṇethāṃ svāheti / āntam anvavasrāvayati
12.10.5	yajamānamātry audumbarī barṣiṣṭhā sthūṇānāṃ bhavati / yathāsuṣṭhuparyantāṃ minvanti
12.10.6	yajamānamātraṃ hrasīyo vā sadaḥ saṃminoti
12.10.7	yadi kāmayeta varṣukaḥ parjanyaḥ syād iti nīcaistarāṃ minuyāt / yadi kāmayetāvarṣukaḥ syād ity uccaistarām / nābhidaghnaparyantāṃ minvantīti vijñāyate
12.10.8	aindram asīty ekaikaṃ madhyamāni chadīṃṣy adhinidadhāti
12.10.9	indrasya sado 'sīti dakṣiṇāni
12.10.10	viśvajanasya chāyety uttarāṇi
12.10.11	dakṣiṇāny uttarāṇi karoti
12.10.12	audumbarīm abhi saṃmukhāni bhavanti
12.10.13	navachady agniṣṭomasya minuyāt / pañcadaśachady ukthyasya / saptadaśachady atirātrasya / navachadi pañcadaśachadi vā ṣoḍaśinaḥ
12.10.14	navachadi tejaskāmasya minuyād iti kāmyāś chadiḥkalpā brāhmaṇavyākhyātāḥ
12.10.15	antarvartān pariśrayaṇaṃ sāṃkāśinaṃ pariṣīvaṇaṃ granthikaraṇam abhimarśanam iti / etāvan nānā / aindrā ete mantrā bhavanti
12.11.1	uparavān vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
12.11.2	dakṣiṇasya havirdhānasyādhastāt paro 'kṣaṃ catvāro 'vāntaradeśeṣu prādeśamukhāḥ prādeśāntarālā bhavanti / asaṃbhinnā upariṣṭāt saṃtṛṇṇā adhastāt
12.11.3	sāvitreṇābhrim ādāya parilikhati parilikhitaṃ rakṣaḥ parilikhitā arātaya iti
12.11.4	dakṣiṇayoḥ pūrvaṃ tato 'paraṃ tata uttaratas tataḥ pūrvam
12.11.5	evam anupūrvāṇy evaiṣv ata ūrdhvaṃ karmāṇi kriyante
12.11.6	bāhumātrān khātvābhryā praharati rakṣohaṇo valagahano vaiṣṇavān khanāmīti / sakṛd eva mantraṃ japati
12.11.7	virāḍ asi sapatnaheti bāhum upāvahṛtya purīṣam udvapatīdam ahaṃ taṃ valagam udvapāmi yaṃ naḥ samānoyam asamāno nicakhāneti
12.11.8	uparavabile nyupyāvabādhata idam enam adharaṃ karomi yo naḥ samāno yo 'samāno 'rātīyati gāyatreṇa chandaseti
12.11.9	evam evottareṇottareṇa mantreṇottareṣu bāhum upāvahṛtya purīṣam udvapaty uttareṇottareṇa chandasāvabādhate / traiṣṭubhaṃ jāgatam ānuṣṭubhaṃ pāṅktam ity etāny āmnātāni bhavanti
12.11.10	nirasto valaga iti purīṣaṃ harati
12.11.11	avabāḍho durasyur iti khare nyupyāvabādhate
12.12.1	atha saṃmṛśāte 'dhvaryur yajamānaś ca
12.12.2	yaḥ pūrvayor dakṣiṇas taṃ yajamāno 'vamṛśati yo 'parayor uttaras tam adhvaryuḥ
12.12.3	adhastāddhastau saṃsparśayataḥ
12.12.4	sa yajamānaḥ pṛcchaty adhvaryo kim atreti
12.12.5	bhadram ity adhvaryuḥ
12.12.6	tan nau saheti yajamānaḥ
12.12.7	atha viparisarpataḥ
12.12.8	yaḥ pūrvayor uttaras taṃ yajamāno 'vamṛśati yo 'parayor dakṣiṇas tam adhvaryuḥ
12.12.9	adhastāddhastau saṃsparśayataḥ
12.12.10	sa yajamānaḥ pṛcchaty adhvaryo kim atreti
12.12.11	bhadram ity adhvaryuḥ
12.12.12	tan mayīti yajamānaḥ
12.12.13	athainān saṃmṛśati virāḍ asi sapatnahety etair mantraiḥ
12.12.14	athainān yavamatībhiḥ prokṣaṇībhiḥ prokṣati rakṣohaṇo valagahanaḥ prokṣāmi vaiṣṇavān iti
12.12.15	avasiñcati rakṣohaṇo valagahano 'vanayāmi vaiṣṇavān iti
12.12.16	yavo 'si yavayāsmad dveṣa iti yavaṃ prāsyati
12.12.17	barhir avastṛṇāti rakṣohaṇo valagahano 'vastṛṇāmi vaiṣṇavān iti
12.12.18	ājyena vyāghārayati rakṣohaṇo valagahano 'bhijuhomi vaiṣṇavān iti
12.12.19	evam uparavamantrān eke samāmananti
12.12.20	rakṣohaṇau valagahanau vaiṣṇavī prokṣāmīty adhiṣavaṇaphalake prokṣati / audumbare pālāśe kārṣmaryamaye vā / asaṃtṛṇṇe bhavataḥ saṃtṛṇṇe vā
12.13.1	pradhimukhe purastāt saṃhite samāvakṛtte paścād dvyaṅgula uttarādhiṣavaṇaphalake bhavati caturaṅgulaṃ vā
12.13.2	purastād aṃhīyasī bhavataḥ paścāt prathīyasī
12.13.3	dvau dakṣiṇenāpidadhāti dvāv uttareṇa rakṣohaṇau valagahanāv upadadhāmi vaiṣṇavī iti
12.13.4	paryūhati rakṣohaṇau valagahanau paryūhāmi vaiṣṇavī iti
12.13.5	paristṛṇāti rakṣohaṇau valagahanau paristṛṇāmi vaiṣṇavī iti
12.13.6	abhimantrayate rakṣohaṇau valagahanau vaiṣṇavī iti
12.13.7	rakṣohaṇaṃ tvā valagahanaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ prokṣāmīty adhiṣavaṇacarma prokṣaty ānaḍuhaṃ rohitam
12.13.8	adhiṣavaṇaphalakayor adhiṣavaṇacarmāstṛṇāty uttaralomāsecanavad rakṣohā tvā valagahā vaiṣṇavam āstṛṇāmīti
12.13.9	tasmiṃś caturo grāvṇaḥ sādayaty ūrdhvasānūn āhananaprakārān uparaṃ pratiṣṭhaṃ madhye pañcamaṃ bṛhann asi bṛhadgrāvā bṛhatīm indrāya vācaṃ vadety ekaikam
12.13.10	auparavāt purīṣād dakṣiṇasya havirdhānasyāgreṇopastambhanaṃ catuḥsraktiṃ kharaṃ karoti yāvantaṃ pātrebhya āptaṃ manyate
12.14.1	cātvālād dhiṣṇiyān upavapati
12.14.2	āgnīdhrāgāre 'ntarvedy āgnīdhrīyaṃ vibhūr asi pravāhaṇa iti
12.14.3	raudreṇānīkenety enaṃ mantraṃ sarvatrānuṣajati
12.14.4	apareṇa sadobilaṃ pṛṣṭhyāyāṃ hotrīyaṃ vahnir asi havyavāhana iti
12.14.5	dakṣiṇena hotrīyaṃ praśāstrīyaṃ śvātro 'si pracetā iti
12.14.6	uttareṇa hotrīyam udīca itarān
12.14.7	tutho 'si viśvavedā iti brāhmaṇācchaṃsinaḥ
12.14.8	uśig asi kavir iti potuḥ
12.14.9	aṅghārir asi bambhārir iti neṣṭuḥ
12.14.10	avasyur asi duvasvān ity acchāvākasya
12.14.11	dakṣiṇārdhe veder mārjālīyaṃ praṣṭim āgnīdhrīyeṇa śundhyūr asi mārjālīya iti
12.15.1	tata itarān upatiṣṭhate
12.15.2	samrāḍ asi kṛśānur ity āhavanīyam
12.15.3	pariṣadyo 'si pavamāna iti yatra bahiṣpavamānaṃ stuvate
12.15.4	pratakvā 'si nabhasvān iti cātvālam
12.15.5	asaṃmṛṣṭo 'si havyasūda iti śāmitradeśam
12.15.6	ṛtadhāmāsi suvarjotir ity audumbarīm
12.15.7	brahmajyotir asi suvardhāmeti brahmasadanam
12.15.8	samudro 'si viśvavyacā iti sadaḥ
12.15.9	ajo 'sy ekapād iti śālāmukhīyam
12.15.10	ahir asi budhniya iti prājahitam
12.15.11	kavyo 'si kavyavāhana ity anvāhāryapacanam
12.15.12	atraike barhiṣaḥ staraṇaṃ samāmananti
12.15.13	tataḥ saṃpreṣyati stṛṇīta barhiḥ pra vrataṃ yacchata sam apivratān hvayadhvam
12.15.14	na kharam adhistṛṇanti / na dhiṣṇiyān
12.15.15	atrāsmā ekastanavrataṃ prayacchati
12.16.1	agnīṣomīyasya paśos tantraṃ prakramayati
12.16.2	plakṣaśākhām ātithyābarhiṣy upasaṃnahyati / ātithyāparidhīn idhme
12.16.3	trayoviṃśatidārum idhmaṃ karoti
12.16.4	samānam ājyānāṃ grahaṇāt
12.16.5	śālāmukhīye pāśukāny ājyāni gṛhṇāti
12.16.6	etasminn evāta ūrdhvaṃ gārhapatyakarmāṇi kriyante
12.16.7	ā somaṃ dadata ā grāvṇa ā vāyavyāny ā droṇakalaśam ut patnīm ānayanty anv anāṃsi pravartayanti
12.16.8	śālāmukhīyaṃ gārhapatyakarmabhyo 'nvavasyanti
12.16.9	prācī patnī pūrvam agnim abhyudaiti praitu brahmaṇas patnīti
12.16.10	agne gṛhapata upa mā hvayasvety etadādi śālāmukhīye kuruta ā gārhapatyābhimantraṇāt
12.16.11	upasthe brahmā rājānaṃ kurute
12.16.12	saṃhvayanti yajamānasyāmātyān
12.16.13	adhvaryuṃ yajamāno 'nvārabhate yajamānaṃ patnī patnīm itare putrabhrātaraḥ
12.16.14	ahatena vāsasāmātyān saṃpracchādya vāsaso 'ntaṃ srugdaṇḍa upaniyamya juhoti vaisarjanāni tvaṃ soma tanūkṛdbhya iti
12.16.15	juṣāṇo aptur ājyasya vetu svāheti dvitīyām āhutiṃ hutvā
12.17.1	śālāmukhīya idhmam ādīpya saṃpreṣyaty agnīṣomābhyāṃ praṇīyamānābhyām anubrūhīti
