12.17.2	trir anūktāyāṃ prathamāyām agniprathamāḥ prāñco 'bhipravrajanti
12.17.3	athainam anuharanty ājyāny anuharantīdhmābarhir anuharanti prokṣaṇīr anunayanty agnīṣomīyam
12.17.4	āgnīdhra etam idhmaṃ sādayitvā nayavatyarcā abhijuhoty ayaṃ no agnir varivaḥ kṛṇotv iti
12.17.5	atraiva grāvṇo vāyavyāni droṇakalaśam āgnīdhra upavāsayati
12.17.6	somaprathamāḥ prāñco 'bhipravrajanti
12.17.7	uru viṣṇo vi kramasvety āhavanīye hutvāparayā dvārā havirdhāne rājānaṃ prapādayati somo jigāti gātuvid iti / pūrvayā vā
12.17.8	pūrvayā tu yajamānaḥ prapadyate
12.17.9	yadi gataśrīḥ syāt pūrvayaiva dvārā rājānaṃ prapādayet
12.17.10	dakṣiṇasya havirdhānasya nīḍe kṛṣṇājinaṃ prācīnagrīvam uttaralomāstṛṇāty adityāḥ sado 'sīti
12.17.11	tasmin rājānam āsādayaty adityāḥ sada āsīdeti
12.18.1	āsannaṃ rājānaṃ yajamāno 'bhimantrayata eṣa vo deva savitaḥ somas taṃ rakṣadhvaṃ mā vo dabhad etat tvaṃ soma devo devān upāgā iti
12.18.2	pradakṣiṇam āvartata idam ahaṃ manuṣyo manuṣyān saha prajayā saha rāyaspoṣeṇeti
12.18.3	namo devebhya iti prācīnam añjaliṃ karoti
12.18.4	svadhā pitṛbhya iti dakṣiṇataḥ
12.18.5	upaniṣkrāmatīdam ahaṃ nir varuṇasya pāśād iti
12.18.6	vihāram abhivīkṣate suvar abhi vi khyeṣaṃ vaiśvānaraṃ jyotir iti
12.18.7	tato 'vāntaradīkṣāṃ visṛjate
12.18.8	dakṣiṇatas tiṣṭhann āhavanīyam abhimantrayate 'gne vratapate tvaṃ vratānāṃ vratapatir asīti
12.18.9	nitarāṃ mekhalāṃ mṛdhnīte
12.18.10	tato muṣṭī visṛjate / svāhā yajñaṃ manaseti dve / svāhā dyāvāpṛthivībhyām iti dve / svāhoror antarikṣād iti dve / svāhā yajñaṃ vātād ārabha iti dve
12.18.11	svāhā vāci vāto visṛja iti vācaṃ visṛjate
12.18.12	nivartate vratam
12.18.13	somān haviḥśeṣān iti sutye 'hani bhakṣayati
12.18.14	tata idhmaṃ barhir iti prokṣati darśapūrṇamāsayoḥ
12.18.15	athaitad barhiḥ sarvasyāṃ mahāvedyāṃ stṛṇīyād ity ekam / apareṇottaravedim ity aparam
12.18.16	yat kiṃ cāta ūrdhvaṃ barhir āgacched evam evainaṃ stṛṇīyāt
12.18.17	samānam ā srucāṃ sādanāt
12.18.18	srucaḥ sādayitvā
12.19.1	yūpaṃ chinatti
12.19.2	dīkṣāsu yūpaṃ chinatty upasatsu vā
12.19.3	vijñāyate yadi dīkṣitasyāvṛkṇo yūpaḥ syād araṇī cājyaṃ cādāya yūpasyānte 'gniṃ mathitvā juhuyād iti
12.19.4	atha yadi krītaḥ somaḥ syād āhavanīya eva juhuyāt
12.19.5	samānam ā paśūpākaraṇāt
12.19.6	agnīṣomīyaṃ paśum upākaroti
12.19.7	samānam ā pravarāt
12.19.8	prākṛtena pravareṇa hotāraṃ vṛtvā punar āśrāvyopāṃśunāmadheyagrāham asphya uttarān ṛtvijo vṛṇīte
12.19.9	indraṃ hotrād asau mānuṣa iti hotāram
12.19.10	agnim āgnīdhrād asau mānuṣa ity āgnīdhram
12.19.11	aśvinādhvaryū ādhvaryavād ahaṃ cāsau mānuṣāv ity ātmānaṃ pratiprasthātāraṃ ca
12.19.12	mitrāvaruṇau praśāstārau praśāstrād asau manuṣa iti maitrāvaruṇam
12.19.13	indro brahmā brāhmaṇād asau mānuṣa iti brāhmaṇācchaṃsinam
12.19.14	marutaḥ potrād asau mānuṣa iti potāram
12.19.15	gnāvo neṣṭrād asau mānuṣa iti neṣṭāram
12.19.16	tato yajamānaṃ vṛnīte 'gnir daivīnāṃ viśāṃ puraetāyaṃ sunvan yajamāno manuṣyāṇāṃ tayor nāv asthūri gārhapatyāni santu śataṃ himā dvā yū rādhāṃsīt saṃpṛñcānāv asaṃpṛñcānau tanva iti
12.19.17	savanīya eke vṛṇate / tatra sunvann iti brūyāt
12.19.18	ayaṃ yajamāno manuṣyāṇām ity agnīṣomīye vṛṇānaḥ
12.20.1	pravṛtaḥ pravṛtaḥ pravṛtahomau juhoti juṣṭo vāco bhūyāsam // ṛcā stomaṃ samardhayety etābhyām
12.20.2	pravṛtaḥ pravṛto juhuyād ity ekam / adhvaryur eva juhuyād ity aparam
12.20.3	samānam ā vapāyā homāt
12.20.4	hutāyāṃ vapāyām āhvayati subrahmaṇyaḥ subrahmaṇyāṃ pitāputrīyām
12.20.5	aparāhṇe vasatīvarīr gṛhṇāti vahantīnāṃ pratīpaṃ tiṣṭhan
12.20.6	kumbham upamārayati haviṣmatīr imā āpa iti
12.20.7	nāntamā vahantīr atīyāt
12.20.8	chāyāyai cātapataś ca sandhau gṛhṇāti / vṛkṣasya vātmano vā chāyāyām
12.20.9	yasyāgṛhītā abhinimrocej jyotiṣā vā gṛhṇīyāddhiraṇyaṃ vāvadhāya
12.20.10	yo vā brāhmaṇo bahuyājī tasya kumbhyānāṃ gṛhṇīyāt
12.20.11	varaṃ dattvā gṛhṇīyād ity ekeṣām
12.20.12	athainā apareṇa gārhapatyam upasādayaty agner vo 'pannagṛhasya sadasi sādayāmīti
12.20.13	samānam eḍāyāḥ
12.20.14	dakṣiṇena havirdhāne samavattaṃ haraty uttareṇa vā
12.20.15	tataḥ saṃpreṣyaty agnīd aupayajān aṅgārān āhareti
12.20.16	śāmitrād āgnīdhrād vāṅgārān āhṛtyāgnīdhro hotrīye nivapati
12.20.17	pratiprasthātopayajati
12.20.18	nātrānūyājānte svaruṃ juhoti / na savanīye / anūbandhyāyām eva juhoti
12.20.19	taṃ divopākṛtya naktaṃ saṃsthāpayati
12.20.20	patnīsaṃyājāntaḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
12.20.21	hṛdayaśūlena caritvā na yūpam upatiṣṭhate
12.20.22	nāgnīṣomīye na savanīye hṛdayaśūlena caranti / anūbandhyāyām eva carantīty ekeṣām
12.21.1	niśāyām antarvedy āsīnau yajamānaṃ patnīṃ ca vasatīvarībhir abhipariharanti
12.21.2	nādīkṣitaṃ vasatīvarībhir abhiparihareyuḥ
12.21.3	ādāya kumbhaṃ savye 'ṃse nidhāya dakṣiṇayā dvāropaniṣkramya dakṣiṇaṃ vedyantam anuparītya dakṣiṇasyām uttaravediśroṇyāṃ sādayatīndrāgniyor bhāgadheyī stheti
12.21.4	ādāya kumbhaṃ dakṣiṇe 'ṃse nidhāya yathetaṃ pratiparītyottarayā dvāropaniṣkramyottaraṃ vedyantam anuparītyottarasyām uttaravediśroṇyāṃ sādayati mitrāvaruṇayor bhāgadheyī stheti
12.21.5	ādāya kumbhaṃ savye 'ṃse nidhāya yathetaṃ pratiparītya pūrvayā dvāropaniṣkramyāgnīdhre sādayati viśveṣāṃ devānāṃ bhāgadheyī stha yajñe jāgṛteti
12.21.6	atra etā upavāsayati
12.21.7	āhvayati subrahmaṇyaḥ subrahmaṇyaṃ pitāputrīyām
12.21.8	tataḥ payāṃsi viśāsti / yā yajamānasya vratadhuk tasyā āśiraṃ kuruta yā patniyai tasyai dadhigrahāya yā gharmadhuk tasyai dadhigharmāya taptam anātaktaṃ maitrāvaruṇāya śṛtātaṅkyaṃ kurutādityagrahāyeti
12.21.9	yathācoditaṃ kurvanti
12.21.10	atrāmikṣāyāḥ sāyaṃdohaṃ dohayati
12.21.11	havirdhāne yajamānaṃ jāgarayanti / prāgvaṃśe patnīm
12.21.12	āgnīdhra ṛtvijo vasanti / na sadasi kaścana vasati
12.21.13	yajamāna evaitāṃ rātriṃ rājānaṃ gopāyatīti vijñāyate
13.1.1	mahārātre budhyante
13.1.2	āgneyyarcāgnīdhram abhimṛśet / vaiṣṇavyā havirdhānam / āgneyyā srucaḥ / vāyavyayā vāyavyāni / aindryā sadaḥ
13.1.3	atraivābhimṛśed ity ekam / karmāgame karmāṅgam ity aparam
13.1.4	āgnīdhre yajñatanūr juhoti prajāpatir manasāndho 'ccheta ity etās trayastriṃśatam / yajñārtiṃ ca pratijuhoti / pūrvām anudrutyottarayā juhotīti vijñāyate
13.1.5	ekayā tu prathamam
13.1.6	khare pātrāṇi prayunakty agnir devatā gāyatrī chanda upāṃśoḥ pātram asīty etair mantrair yathārūpam
13.1.7	dakṣiṇe 'ṃsa upāṃśvantaryāmayoḥ pātre prayunakti / pūrvam upāṃśor aparam antaryāmasya
13.1.8	api vā dakṣiṇam upāṃśor uttaram antaryāmasya
13.1.9	te antareṇopāṃśusavanaṃ saṃspṛṣṭaṃ sādayati
13.1.10	pratyañci dvidevatyapātrāṇi / parisrug aindravāyavasyājagāvaṃ maitrāvaruṇasya dvisraktyāśvinasya
13.1.11	tato 'pare śukrāmanthinoḥ pātre / dakṣiṇaṃ bailvaṃ śukrapātram uttaraṃ vaikaṅkataṃ manthipātram
13.1.12	tato 'pare āśvatthe aśvaśaphabudhne ubhayatomukhe ṛtupātre / dakṣiṇam adhvaryor uttaraṃ pratiprasthātuḥ
13.1.13	dakṣiṇasyāṃ śroṇyām āgrayaṇasthālīṃ prayunakti / uttarasyām ukthyasthālīṃ cokthyapātraṃ cāśvaśaphabudhnam
13.1.14	te antareṇa
13.2.1	trīṇy atigrāhyapātrāṇi prayunakti
13.2.2	dakṣiṇasya havirdhānasyāgreṇopastambhanam ādityasthālīṃ cādityapātraṃ ca / uttarasyāgreṇopastambhanam anupopte dhruvasthālīm
13.2.3	uttare 'ṃse audumbaraṃ catuḥsrakti dadhigrahapātram
13.2.4	madhye pariplavāṃ yathā srug adaṇḍā
13.2.5	yathāvakāśaṃ khādiraṃ catuḥsrakti ṣoḍaśipātraṃ yadi ṣoḍaśī bhavati
13.2.6	prādeśamātrāṇy ūrdhvasānūni madhye saṃnatāni vāyavyāny āsecanavanti bhavanti
13.2.7	yāny anādiṣṭavṛkṣāṇi yaḥ kaśca yajñiyo vṛkṣas tasya syur ity āśmarathyaḥ / vaikaṅkatānīty ālekhanaḥ
13.2.8	etena camasānāṃ vṛkṣaniyogo vyākhyātaḥ / naiyagrodhā eva syur ity aparam
13.2.9	tsarumanto 'tsarukā vā daśa camasā bhavanti
13.2.10	daśa camasādhvaryavaḥ
13.2.11	hotur brahmaṇa udgātur yajamānasya maitrāvaruṇasya brāhmaṇācchaṃsinaḥ potur neṣṭur acchāvākasyāgnīdhrasyety eteṣām ete camasāḥ / tān khare yathāvakāśaṃ prayunakti
13.2.12	dakṣiṇasya havirdhānasyādhastāt paścād akṣaṃ droṇakalaśaṃ sadaśāpavitraṃ prayunakti yunajmi te pṛthivīṃ jyotiṣā saheti
13.2.13	uttarasya nīḍa ādhavanīyaṃ yunajmi vāyum antarikṣeṇa te saheti
13.2.14	prauge pūtabhṛtaṃ yunajmi vācaṃ saha sūryeṇa ta iti
13.2.15	atraike 'dhiṣavaṇacarmaṇo grāvṇām iti prayojanaṃ samāmananti
13.2.16	uparam abhi saṃmukhā bhavanti
13.3.1	athainān saṃmṛśaty apāṃ kṣayā ṛtasya garbhāḥ / bhuvanasya gopāḥ śyenā atithayaḥ / parvatānāṃ kakubhaḥ na pātāraḥ / vagnunendraṃ hvayata / ghoṣeṇāmīvāṃś cātayata / yuktāḥ stha vahata / svargaṃ lokam abhivahata yajamānam iti
13.3.2	savanīyasya tantraṃ prakramayati
13.3.3	samānam ājyānāṃ grahaṇāt
13.3.4	laukikād ājyāt pracaraṇyām agre gṛhṇāti
13.3.5	sahedhmenaidhān prokṣati yān etad ahar abhyādhāsyan bhavati
13.3.6	yat kiṃcābhi tayor āghārasamidhor ādadhyāt prokṣitam evādadhyāt
13.3.7	samānam ā srucāṃ sādanāt
13.3.8	srucaḥ sannā abhimṛśati yunajmi tisro vipṛcaḥ sūryasya ta iti
13.3.9	atraike pātraprayojanaṃ samāmananti
13.3.10	āsanyān mā mantrāt pāhi kasyāścid abhiśastyā ity āgnīdhre hutvāntareṣe rājānaṃ grāvasūpāvaharati hṛde tvā // soma rājann ehy avaroheti dvābhyām
13.3.11	athāgnīdhre pañcahotāraṃ hutvā hotre prātaranuvākāya saṃpreṣyati devebhyaḥ prātaryāvabhyo 'nubrūhi brahman vācaṃ yaccha subrahmaṇya subrahmaṇyām āhvaya pratiprasthātaḥ savanīyān nirvapāmikṣāṃ dohayeti
13.3.12	yaṃ dviṣyāt tasya pravaditāsu vāksūpākuryāt
13.3.13	āhvayati subrahmaṇyaḥ subrahmaṇyāṃ pitāputrīyām
13.3.14	atra savanīyān nirvaped āmikṣāṃ dohayed ity ekam / uparitarām ity aparam
13.4.1	yatrābhijānāty abhūd uṣā ruśatpaśur iti tat pracaraṇyā juhoti śṛṇotv agniḥ samidhā havaṃ ma iti
13.4.2	aparaṃ caturgṛhītaṃ gṛhītvā darbhān ādāyopaniṣkramya saṃpreṣyaty apa iṣya hotar maitrāvaruṇasya camasādhvaryav ādravaikadhanina ādravata neṣṭaḥ patnīm udānayonnetar hotṛcamasena vasatīvarībhiś cātvālaṃ pratyupāsveti
13.4.3	tryavarārdhyā ayuja ekadhanā bhavanti
13.4.4	yathācoditaṃ kurvanti
13.4.5	prehy udehīti neṣṭā patnīm udānayati
13.4.6	yatra hotuḥ prātaranuvākam anubruvata upaśṛṇuyāt tad apo 'dhvaryur gṛhṇīyāt / yadi na śṛṇuyād badhiraḥ syāt / vācopachidyeta
13.4.7	yadi dūre syuḥ pratyudūhya gṛhṇīyāt
13.4.8	vahantīṣu tṛṇaṃ prāsyaitac caturgṛhītaṃ juhoti devīr āpo apāṃ napād iti
13.4.9	yadi vā purā tṛṇaṃ bhavati tasminn eva juhoti
13.4.10	kārṣir asīti darbhair āhutim apaplāvya ghṛtaliptānāṃ maitrāvaruṇacamasenonnayati samudrasya vo 'kṣityā unnaya iti
13.4.11	evam evaikadhanā unnayati / somasya vo mūjavato rasaṃ gṛhṇāmīti vā
13.4.12	patnī pannejanīr gṛhṇāti vasubhyo rudrebhya ādityebhyo viśvebhyo vo devebhyaḥ pannejanīr gṛhṇāmi yajñāya vaḥ pannejanīr gṛhṇāmīti
13.4.13	āharanty apaḥ
13.4.14	prehy udehīty eva neṣṭā patnīm udānayati
13.5.1	apareṇa neṣṭur dhiṣṇiyaṃ patnī pannejanīḥ sādayati vasubhyo rudrebhya ādityebhyo viśvebhyo vo devebhyaḥ pannejanīḥ sādayāmi yajñāya vaḥ pannejanīḥ sādayāmīti
13.5.2	upari cātvāle 'dhvaryur hotṛcamasaṃ ca maitrāvaruṇacamasaṃ ca saṃspṛśya vasatīvarīr vyānayati sam āpo adbhir agmata sam oṣadhībhir oṣadhayaḥ saṃ vratair vratacāriṇa iti
13.5.3	hotṛcamasa ānīya maitrāvaruṇacamasaṃ pūrayati / maitrāvaruṇacamasāddhotṛcamasam / hotṛcamasān maitrāvaruṇacamasam
13.5.4	athaināḥ pracaraṇyā samanakti saṃ vo 'naktu varuṇaḥ sam indraḥ saṃ bṛhaspatiḥ / tvaṣṭā viṣṇuḥ prajayā saṃrarāṇo yajamānāya draviṇaṃ dadhātu // iti / yathāyathaṃ dhuro dhūrbhiḥ kalpantām iti ca
13.5.5	pṛcchati hotādhvaryum adhvaryo 'ver apa iti
13.5.6	utem anannamur iti pratyāha
13.5.7	tataḥ kratukaraṇaṃ juhoti yam agne pṛtsu martyam ity etayā yady agniṣṭomaḥ
13.5.8	yady ukthyo hutvā paridhau lepaṃ nimārṣṭi
13.5.9	yadi ṣoḍaśī hutvā paridhau lepaṃ nimṛjya droṇakalaśam upaspṛśati rarāṭīṃ vā
13.5.10	na juhoti na nimārṣṭi nopaspṛśati vājapeye 'tirātre vā / etad yajur vadan prapadyate
13.5.11	dakṣiṇasya havirdhānasya pradhure pracaraṇīṃ sādayati
13.5.12	yaṃ dviṣyāt tam upaspṛśet
13.6.1	aparayā dvārā havirdhāne 'paḥ prapādayati pūrvayā vā / pūrvayā tu yajamānaḥ prapadyate
13.6.2	uttarasya havirdhānasyādhastād vasatīvarīr ekadhanā maitrāvaruṇacamasīyā iti sādayati
13.6.3	dakṣiṇasya havirdhānasyādhastāt puro 'kṣaṃ hotṛcamasaṃ sādayitvā dadhigrahaṇe carati
13.6.4	audumbareṇa pātreṇa catuḥsraktinā dadhi gṛhṇāty upayāmagṛhīto 'si prajāpate tvā jyotiṣmate jyotiṣmantaṃ gṛhṇāmīti
13.6.5	haraty upendra dviṣato mana iti
13.6.6	juhoti prāṇāya tvety anuvākaśeṣeṇa
13.6.7	ājyagrahaṃ gṛhṇīyāt tejaskāmasya / somagrahaṃ gṛhṇīyād brahmavarcasakāmasya / dadhigrahaṃ gṛhṇīyāt paśukāmasya
13.6.8	ājyagrahasyaiṣa eva kalpaḥ
13.6.9	somagrahaṃ grahīṣyann adhiṣavaṇacarmaṇi rājānaṃ nivapati yāvantam ekagrahāyāptaṃ manyate
13.6.10	pratyupanahyetaraṃ vasatīvarībhir hotṛcamasaṃ pūrayitvā nigrābhyāsu yajamānaṃ vācayati nigrābhyā stha devaśruta iti pratipadya gaṇā me mā vi tṛṣann ity antena
13.6.11	vasatīvarībhir upasṛjyābhiṣoṣyann abhimantrayate 'vīvṛdhaṃ vo manasā sujātā iti
13.6.12	yatra kva cābhiṣuṇuyād evam evābhimantrayate
13.6.13	athainam upare grāvṇābhiṣunoti
13.7.1	tisro yahvasya samidhaḥ parijmano devā akṛṇvann uśijo amartyave / tāsām enām adadhur martye bhujaṃ lokam id dve upa jāmī īyatur iti
13.7.2	yatra kva cābhiṣuṇuyād upara eva grāvṇābhiṣuṇuyāt
13.7.3	etasyaivaiṣo 'bhiṣavamantraḥ
13.7.4	yo 'bhiṣūyamāṇasya prathamo 'ṃśuḥ skandati tam abhimantrayetā mā skān saha prajayā saha rāyaspoṣeṇeti
13.7.5	abhiṣave 'bhiṣave 'bhimantrayetety ekam / ya eva sarvaprathama ity aparam
13.7.6	drapsaś caskandeti vipruṣo 'bhimantrayeta
13.7.7	abhiṣave 'bhiṣave 'bhimantrayetety ekam / ya eva sarvāntata ity aparam
13.7.8	atra yajamāno daśāpavitrasya nābhiṃ kurute
13.7.9	athainaṃ sahiraṇyena pāṇinā tiraḥ pavitram acchinnāṃ dhārāṃ srāvayan dadhigrahapātreṇa gṛhṇāti / vāyavyenaiva gṛhṇīyād ity aparam
13.7.10	athainaṃ khare sādayaty eṣa te yonir iti
13.7.11	athainaṃ sahiraṇyena pāṇinā prāṅmukho juhoti / tasya dadhigraheṇa mantrā vyākhyātāḥ
13.7.12	anadhikṛto vā somadharmair dadhigrahavikāratvāt
13.7.13	tatrārthagrahaṇo 'bhiṣavaḥ paratrasaṃyogāt / somakaraṇī cāsyābhiṣavamantraḥ
13.7.14	tatraiṣo 'tyantapradeśaḥ
13.8.1	sarvān somān sahiraṇyena pāṇinā gṛhṇāti ca juhoti ca
13.8.2	sarvāḥ somāhutīḥ prāṅmukho juhoti
13.8.3	hutvā sadasi śeṣaṃ bhakṣayati
13.8.4	mārjālīye pātraṃ prakṣālayati
13.8.5	sadasy evāta ūrdhvaṃ somabhakṣān bhakṣayanti / āgnīdhre havirbhakṣān
13.8.6	mārjālīya ucchiṣṭapātrāṇi prakṣālayati
13.8.7	tato 'dābhyaṃ gṛhṇāti
13.8.8	upanaddhasya rājñas trīn aṃśūn pravṛhati vasavas tvā pra vṛhantu gāyatreṇa chandasety etair mantraiḥ
13.8.9	nigrābhyāṇāṃ dadhnaḥ payaso vā camase niḥṣicyāṃśūn ādhūnoti māndāsu te śukra śukram ā dhūnomītyetair mantraiḥ
13.8.10	tribhir ādhūnotīty ekeṣām / pañcabhir ity ekeṣām / saptabhir ity ekeṣām
13.8.11	athainaṃ dadhigrahapātreṇa gṛhṇāti śukraṃ te śukreṇa gṛhṇāmi // agniḥ prātaḥsavane pātv asmān iti caitābhis tisṛbhiḥ
13.8.12	haraty āsminn ugrā acucyavur iti
13.8.13	juhoti somaḥ somasya purogā iti
13.8.14	tato 'ṃśuṣv aṃśūn apisṛjaty uśik tvaṃ deva soma gāyatreṇa chandasety etaiḥ pratimantram
13.8.15	anusavanam apisṛjed ity ekam / tadānīm ekaikam apisṛjed ity aparam
13.8.16	dvādaśa paṣṭhauhīr dakṣiṇā dadāti kṛttyadhīvāsaṃ ca
13.8.17	tato 'ṃśuṃ gṛhṇāti
13.8.18	adhiṣavaṇacarmaṇi rājānaṃ nivapati yāvantam ekagrahāyāptaṃ manyate
13.9.1	athainam anavānaṃ sakṛdabhiṣutya tiraḥ pavitram acchinnāṃ dhārāṃ srāvayann adābhyapātreṇānavānaṃ sakṛd gṛhṇāti
13.9.2	vāmadevyaṃ manasā gāyamāno gṛhṇātīti vijñāyate
13.9.3	vāmadevyasyarcā gṛhṇīyād ity ekeṣāṃ kayā naś citra ā bhuvad ity etayā
13.9.4	prāṇatā grāhyo 'pānatā grāhyaḥ prāṇyāpānya vyanatā gṛhītavya iti vijñāyate
13.9.5	gṛhītvā śatamānaṃ hiraṇyam abhivyanity ā naḥ prāṇa etu parāvata iti
13.9.6	hiraṇyena graham apidhāyāpa upaspṛśatīndrāgnī me varcaḥ kṛṇutām iti
13.9.7	athainam anavānaṃ sakṛj juhoti dadhanve vā yadīm iti
13.9.8	yady anavānaṃ na śaknuyāddhotuṃ gṛhītuṃ vā vare datte juhuyāt
13.9.9	hutvā sadasi śeṣaṃ bhakṣayati yathā purastāt
13.9.10	dvādaśa paṣṭhauhīr dakṣiṇā dadāti kṛttyadhīvāsaṃ ca
13.9.11	tata upāṃśusavanaṃ grāvāṇam ādatte devasya tvā savituḥ prasava iti pratipadya vṛṣṭivanim ity antena
13.9.12	tam ādāya vācaṃ yacchaty āgrayaṇāt
13.9.13	athainad ūrdhvasānuṃ sahiraṇyena pāṇinā rājño 'bhimimīta indrāya tvā vṛtraghna ity etair mantraiḥ
13.9.14	tatra sa eva mānakalpo yaḥ kraye 'nyatropasamūhanāt
13.9.15	tata upāṃśuṃ gṛhṇāti
13.9.16	adhiṣavaṇacarmaṇi rājānaṃ nivapati yāvantam ekagrahāyāptaṃ manyate
13.10.1	śvātrā stha vṛtratura ity āpyāyyābhimantrayate yat te soma divi jyotir iti
13.10.2	adhiṣavaṇaphalake abhimantrayate dhiṣaṇe vīḍū satī vīḍayethām iti
13.10.3	upariṣṭād grāvā bhavaty adhastād aṃśavaḥ
13.10.4	atha hotṛcamase pradakṣiṇaṃ pariplāvayan nigrābham upaiti prāg apāg udag adharāktās tvā diśa ādhāvantv amba ni ṣvareti
13.10.5	ṣaḍ aṃśūn upayacchati / ārdrāḥ santo 'ṃsaśliṣṭā bhavanti
13.10.6	mā bher mā saṃ vikthā iti grāvāṇam udyamya vadanti
13.10.7	yatra tṛṇaṃ mūlaṃ vā paśyati tat pratyabhiṣunoty anāgasas tvā vayam indreṇa preṣitā upa vāyuṣ ṭe astv aṃśabhūr mitras te astv aṃśabhūr varuṇas te astv aṃśabhūr ahataḥ somo rājā mayeti
13.10.8	etayaivāta ūrdhvam abhiṣuṇuyāt
13.10.9	aṣṭau kṛtvo 'gre 'bhiṣutya punar eva nigrābham upaiti
13.10.10	dvir ādito 'ntato vā / catur nigrābham upaiti
13.10.11	trir udacanena saṃbhṛtyodañcatīti vijñāyate
13.10.12	apāttānām aṃśūnāṃ dvābhyāṃ pratiprasthātopāṃśupātram apidhāyottarata upayacchati
13.10.13	añjalinā rājānam ādāyādhvaryur upāṃśupātraṃ nayati vācaspataye pavasva vājinn iti
13.10.14	evaṃvihitāv aparau dvāv abhiṣavau bhavataḥ
13.10.15	api vaikādaśakṛtvo dvitīyam abhiṣuṇuyād dvādaśakṛtvas tṛtīyam
13.11.1	anyābhyām anyābhyām aṃśubhyāṃ pratiprasthātā pātram apidadhāti
13.11.2	asādayitvā graham ādāyādhvaryur uttiṣṭhati svāṅkṛto 'si madhumatīr na iṣas kṛdhīti
13.11.3	uttareṇa hotāraṃ haraty urv antarikṣam anvihīti
13.11.4	manas tvāṣṭv ity uttaraṃ paridhisaṃdhim anvavatiṣṭhataḥ
13.11.5	ṛjus tiṣṭhan dakṣiṇāprāñcaṃ saṃtataṃ juhoti svāhā tvā subhavaḥ sūryāyeti
13.11.6	devebhyas tvā marīcipebhya iti hutvā paridhau lepaṃ nimārṣṭi
13.11.7	yadi kāmayeta varṣukaḥ parjanyaḥ syād iti nīcā hastena nimṛjyāt
13.11.8	yadi kāmayetāvarṣukaḥ syād ity uttānena nimṛjyāt
13.11.9	āgrayaṇasthālyāṃ saṃpātam avanīyāyatane pātraṃ sādayaty eṣa te yoniḥ prāṇāya tveti
13.11.10	anabhiṣutānām aṃśūnām ekam ādāyādhvaryur upāṃśupātre 'pāsyati / sa ā tṛtīyasavanāt pariśere
13.11.11	tato 'ṃśuṣvaṃśūn apisṛjati yat te somādābhyaṃ nāma jāgṛvīti / dvaudvāv anusavanaṃ vā
13.11.12	yady abhicared amuṣya tvā prāṇe sādayāmīty upāṃśuṃ gṛhītvā sādayet
13.11.13	athainaṃ sāvitreṇādāya harati
13.11.14	samānam ā homāt
13.11.15	hoṣyann abhimantrayate 'muṃ jahy atha tvā hoṣyāmīti
13.11.16	yadi dūre syād ā tamitos tiṣṭhet
13.11.17	samanya juhoti praharṣiṇo madirasya made mṛṣāsāv astu svāheti
13.11.18	samānam itarat
13.12.1	tato grāvṇa ādāyādhvaryavo mahābhiṣavāyopaviśanti / purastād adhvaryur dakṣiṇataḥ pratiprasthātā paścān neṣṭottarata unnetā
13.12.2	adhiṣavaṇacarmaṇi bhūyiṣṭhaṃ rājānaṃ nivapati / alpīyāṃsaṃ mādhyaṃdināya savanāyāvaśinaṣṭi
13.12.3	vasatīvarībhir upasṛjya nigrābham upetyāparimitam abhiṣuṇvanti
13.12.4	nigrābham upayanti / abhiṣuṇvanti / nigrābham upayanti / abhiṣuṇvanti
13.12.5	trir abhiṣutaṃ rājānaṃ camase saṃsicyādhavanīya ānayati
13.12.6	evaṃvihitāv aparau bhavataḥ
13.12.7	uttame 'bhiṣave prapīḍyarjīṣam
13.12.8	susaṃbhṛtaṃ rājānaṃ kurvanti
13.12.9	pavitreṇa nirmṛjya prapīḍayati
13.12.10	adhiṣavaṇacarmaṇi saṃmukhān grāvṇaḥ kṛtvā grāvabhya ṛjīṣaṃ vyapohati / ṛjīṣamukhān karoti
13.12.11	prāñcam udgātāro droṇakalaśaṃ grāvasv adhyūhanti
13.12.12	samayākṣaṃ prakarṣanti
13.12.13	droṇakalaśa udīcīnadaśaṃ pavitraṃ vitanvanti
13.12.14	pavitraṃ te vitataṃ brahmaṇaspate prabhur gātrāṇi paryeṣi viśvataḥ / ataptatanūr na tad āmo aśnute śṛtāsa id vahantas tat samāśateti rājānam abhimantrya hotṛcamasād yajamānaḥ pavitre saṃtatāṃ dhārāṃ srāvayati / yaṃ dviṣyāt tasya vicchindyāt
13.13.1	udacanenonnetādhavanīyāddhotṛcamasa ānayati
13.13.2	tiraḥ pavitraṃ sravantyā dhārāyā antaryāmaṃ gṛhṇāti upayāmagṛhīto 'sy antar yaccha maghavann iti
13.13.3	tasyopāṃśunā kalpo vyākhyātaḥ
13.13.4	etāvan nānā / dakṣiṇena hotāraṃ haraty uttareṇa vā
13.13.5	manas tvāṣṭv iti dakṣiṇaṃ paridhisaṃdhim anvavatiṣṭhataḥ
13.13.6	ṛjus tiṣṭhan prāñcam udañcaṃ saṃtataṃ juhoti svāhā tvā subhavaḥ sūryāyeti
13.13.7	vyākhyātaṃ lepanimārjanaṃ saṃpātāvanayanam iti
13.13.8	sūdavad antaryāmapātram āyatane sādayaty eṣa te yonir apānāya tveti
13.13.9	yady abhicaret amuṣya tvāpāne sādayāmīty antaryāmapātraṃ gṛhītvā sādayet
13.13.10	samānam itarat
13.13.11	te antareṇopāṃśusavanaṃ saṃspṛṣṭaṃ sādayati vyānāya tveti
13.13.12	yady abhicaret amuṣya tvā vyāne sādayāmīty upāṃśusavanaṃ sādayet
13.13.13	evaṃ sannāny eva bhavanty ā tṛtīyasavanāt
13.13.14	tāv ubhāv udite juhuyād yadi na tvareta
13.13.15	atha yadi tvaretānudita upāṃśuṃ juhuyāt / udite'ntaryāmam
13.13.16	viparītam eka upāṃśvantaryāmayor homaṃ samāmananti / ubhāv anudita ity eke
13.14.1	tiraḥ pavitraṃ sravantyā dhārāyā grahān gṛhṇāti
13.14.2	yadi rathantarasāmā somaḥ syād aindravāyavāgrān gṛhṇīyāt / yadi bṛhatsāmā śukrāgrān / yadi jagatsāmāgrayaṇāgrān / ubhayasāmaindravāyavāgrān gṛhṇīyāt
13.14.3	aindravāyavāgrān gṛhṇīyād āmayāvina iti kāmyāni grahāgrāṇi brāhmaṇavyākhyātāni bhavanti / aindravāyavāgrān ity eva bhavanti
13.14.4	yady anyam aindravāyavāt kāmyaṃ pūrvaṃ grahaṃ gṛhṇīyāddhārayed evam aindravāyavasya sādanāt
13.14.5	athainam aindravāyavaṃ sādayitvā sādayet
13.14.6	yān prācīnam āgrayaṇād grahān gṛhṇīyāt tān upāṃśu gṛhṇīyāt / yān ūrdhvāṃs tān upabdimata iti
13.14.7	āgrayaṇāgrān gṛhṇan manthinam eva gṛhītvā vācaṃ visṛjeta / ukthyāgrān gṛhṇann upāṃśūkthyaṃ gṛhṇīyāt
13.14.8	aindravāyavaṃ gṛhṇāti ā vāyo bhūṣa śucipā iti pratipadya upayāmagṛhīto 'si vāyave tvety antena
13.14.9	apayamya pātraṃ punar eva gṛhṇātīndravāyū ime sutā iti pratipadya upayāmagṛhīto 'sīndravāyubhyāṃ tvety antena
13.14.10	athainaṃ pavitreṇa parimṛjyāyatane sādayaty eṣa te yoniḥ sajoṣābhyāṃ tveti
13.14.11	evam evetarān grahān yathādevataṃ gṛhītvā yathāyatanaṃ svena svena sādanena sādayati
13.14.12	yarhy anāmnātaṃ sādanaṃ syād eṣa te yonir ity evainaṃ sādayet
13.15.1	maitrāvaruṇaṃ gṛhṇāty ayaṃ vāṃ mitrāvaruṇā iti
13.15.2	athainaṃ śṛtaśītena payasā śrīṇāti / rāyā vayaṃ sasṛvāṃso madema havyena devā yavasena gāvaḥ / tāṃ dhenuṃ mitrāvaruṇā yuvaṃ no viśvāhā dhattam anapasphurantīm / iti
13.15.3	atītyāśvinaṃ śukraṃ gṛhṇāty ayaṃ venaś codayat pṛśnigarbhā iti
13.15.4	athainaṃ hiraṇyena śrīṇāti śukraṃ te śukreṇa śrīṇāmīti
13.15.5	tato manthinaṃ taṃ pratnathā pūrvatheti
13.15.6	athainaṃ saktubhiḥ śrīṇāti / mano na yeṣu havaneṣu tigmaṃ vipaḥ śacyā vanutho dravantā / ā yaḥ śaryābhis tuvinṛmṇo asyāḥ śrīṇītād imaṃ gabhastāt / ity anabhidhvaṃsayann ātmānaṃ cetarāṃś ca grahān
13.15.7	tata āgrayaṇaṃ dvayor dhārayor gṛhṇāti
13.15.8	ya eṣa āgrayaṇasthālyāṃ rājā tam anyasmin pātre paryāsicya dvitīyāṃ dhārāṃ kurute ye devā divy ekādaśa stheti
13.15.9	rugṇavatyarcā bhrātṛvyavato gṛhṇīyāt triṃśattrayaś ca gaṇino rujanta iti
13.15.10	āgrayaṇaṃ gṛhītvā trir hiṃkṛtvā vācaṃ visṛjate somaḥ pavate somaḥ pavate somaḥ pavate 'smai brahmaṇe pavate 'smai kṣatrāya pavate 'smai viśe pavate 'smai sunvate yajamānāya pavata iṣe pavata ūrje pavate 'dbhyaḥ pavata oṣadhībhyaḥ pavate vanaspatibhyaḥ pavate dyāvāpṛthivībhyāṃ pavate subhūtāya pavate brahmavarcasāya pavate yajamānāya pavate mahyaṃ jyeṣṭhāya pavata iti
13.15.11	śanair abhivyāharaty athoccair atha sūccair iti vijñāyate
13.16.1	tatas trīn atigrāhyān gṛhṇāty agna āyūṃṣi pavasa ity etais tribhir anuvākaiḥ
13.16.2	tata ukthyam upayāmagṛhīto 'sīndrāya tvā bṛhadvate vayasvata iti
13.16.3	tato dhruvaṃ mūrdhānaṃ divo aratiṃ pṛthivyā iti
13.16.4	yaṃ kāmayeta sarvam āyur iyād iti tasya pūrṇaṃ grahaṃ gṛhṇīyāt
13.16.5	hiraṇye 'dhi sādayed āyuṣkāmasya
13.16.6	rājaputro dhruvaṃ gopāyatīti vijñāyate
13.16.7	dhruve gṛhīte yajamāno na prasrāvayaty āvanayanāt
13.16.8	droṇakalaśe rājānam atipāvayati yāvantaṃ prātaḥsavanāyāptaṃ manyate
13.16.9	prapīḍya pavitraṃ pūtabhṛti vitatya maitrāvaruṇacamasīyā ekadhanāsu vyānayati
13.16.10	yathārtham ekadhanānām ādhavanīye 'vanīyādhavanīyāt pūtabhṛty ekadeśaṃ rājño 'vanayati
13.16.11	tatraiṣo 'tyantapradeśaḥ / yatra kva ca kiṃ ca pūtabhṛty avanayet tiraḥ pavitram evāvanayed anyatra droṇakalaśāt
13.16.12	pavamānagrahān gṛhṇāti / upayāmagṛhīto 'si prajāpataye tveti droṇakalaśam abhimṛśet / indrāya tvety ādhavanīyam / viśvebhyas tvā devebhya iti pūtabhṛtam
13.16.13	purastādupayāmā yajuṣā gṛhyanta upariṣṭādupayāmā ṛcā yajñasya dhṛtyā iti vijñāyate
13.16.14	vaipruṣān homān juhvati yas te drapsa skandatīty etābhis tisṛbhiḥ
13.16.15	saptahotāraṃ ca hutvodañcaḥ prahvā bahiṣpavamānāya prasarpanti
13.16.16	adhvaryuṃ prastotānvārabhate prastotāram udgātodgātāraṃ pratihartā pratihartāraṃ brahmā brahmāṇaṃ yajamānaḥ / yajamānaṃ brahmetyekeṣām
13.16.17	barhirmuṣṭiṃ dhūnvann adhvaryuḥ prathamaṃ sarpati gāyatraḥ panthā vasavo devatā vṛkeṇāparipareṇa pathā svasti vasūn aśīyeti vāg agregā agra etv iti ca
13.17.1	dakṣiṇena cātvālam upaviśanti
13.17.2	agreṇa prastotāram upaviśyādhvaryuḥ prastotre barhirmuṣṭiṃ prayacchan stotram upākaroti vāyur hiṃkarteti pratipadya te devāḥ prāṇabhṛtaḥ prāṇaṃ mayi dadhatu / somaḥ pavata ity antena
13.17.3	etenaiva sarvāṇi stotrāṇy upākaroti
13.17.4	upāvartadhvam ity anyatra pavamānebhyo 'nantaraṃ karoti
13.17.5	cātvālam avekṣamāṇāḥ stuvate
13.17.6	stotraṃ stūyamānaṃ catvāra ṛtvija upagāyanti / digbhya upagāyanti
13.17.7	yajamānapañcamā ṛtvija upagāyanti
13.17.8	nādhvaryur upagāyed iti vijñāyate
13.17.9	o ity anya ṛtvija upagāyanti / ho iti yajamānaḥ
13.17.10	stūyamānaṃ yajamāno 'nvārohaṃ japati śyeno 'si gāyatrachandā iti
13.17.11	stutam anumantrayate stutasya stutamasīti
13.17.12	etenaiva sarvāṇi stotrāṇy anumantrayate
13.17.13	stuta uttiṣṭhann āhāgnīd agnīn vihara barhiḥ stṛṇāhi puroḍāśāṁ alaṃkuru pratiprasthātaḥ paśunehīti
13.17.14	pratyetya rājānaṃ yajamāna upatiṣṭhate viṣṇo tvaṃ no antama iti
13.17.15	āgnīdhrād aṅgārān āhṛtya yathānyuptam āgnīdhro dhiṣṇiyān viharati
13.17.16	purastāt pratyaṅṅ āsīnaḥ pratiprasthātā dhiṣṇiyān vyāghārayati
13.17.17	droṇakalaśāt pariplavayā rājānam ādāyāhavanīyam āgnīdhrīyaṃ hotrīyam / pañcagṛhītenājyenetarān / somena mārjālīyam
13.17.18	ya eva nivapanamantrās te vyāghāraṇāḥ
13.17.19	savanīyānāṃ pātrāṇi prakṣālya prayunakti yāny auṣadhakāritāni bhavanti
13.17.20	pavitre kṛtvā saṃpreṣyati yajamāna vācaṃ yaccheti
13.17.21	vāgyataḥ pātrāṇi saṃmṛśati
13.18.1	tataḥ savanīyān nirvapatīndrāya harivate dhānā indrāya pūṣaṇvate karambhaṃ sarasvatyai bhāratyai parivāpam indrāya puroḍāśam aṣṭākapālaṃ prātaḥsavana ekādaśakapālaṃ mādhyaṃdine savane dvādaśakapālaṃ tṛtīyasavane / api vā sarvatraikādaśakapālam
13.18.2	manthaṃ karambha ity ācakṣate / lājān parivāpa iti
13.18.3	samānam āvapanāt
13.18.4	yavān opya lājārthaṃ kapālam upadhāya tasminn ardhaṃ vrīhīṇāṃ yajurutpūtābhir adbhiḥ saṃyutyāvapati
13.18.5	āvapann adhiśrayaṇamantraṃ japaty udvapann udvāsanamantram
13.18.6	bhrāṣṭrān lājān abhighāryodvāsayati
13.18.7	kāla evālaṃkaroti
13.18.8	samānam āvahananāt
13.18.9	yavān avahṛtya pāṇibhyāṃ lājān vituṣān karoti
13.18.10	tatrāvapanamantro 'vahananamantra udvapanamantro niṣpavanamantra iti kriyante
13.18.11	pāṇyor udūkhalamusalamantrāḥ kriyeran
13.18.12	tataḥ puroḍāśīyān avahanti
13.18.13	yat prāg adhivapanāt tat kṛtvā karambhārthaṃ kapālam upadhāya yavataṇḍulānām ardhaṃ karambhārthaṃ kapāla āvapati
13.18.14	vyākhyātaḥ saṃskāraḥ
13.18.15	piṣṭānām āvṛtā dhānāḥ piṃṣanti
13.18.16	samānam ā kapālopadhānāt
13.18.17	dhānārthaṃ kapālam upadhāya puroḍāśakapālāny upadadhāti
13.18.18	āmikṣāṃ karoti
13.18.19	nānāpātreṣu havīṃṣi saṃvapati / utpunāti
13.19.1	manthaṃ caiva puroḍāśaṃ ca saṃyauti
13.19.2	dhānā opya puroḍāśam adhiśrayati
13.19.3	evam eva dhānā udvāsya puroḍāśam udvāsayati
13.19.4	āgnīdhra evānupṛṣṭhyaṃ barhiḥ stṛṇāti
13.19.5	puroḍāśān alaṃkaroti
13.19.6	tata āśvinaṃ droṇakalaśāt pariplavayā gṛhṇāti yā vāṃ kaśā madhumatīty etenānuvākenottareṇa vā
13.19.7	droṇakalaśād evāta ūrdhvaṃ pariplavayā grahān gṛhṇāty anyatra dhārāgrahebhyaḥ
13.19.8	āśvinaṃ gṛhītvā trivṛtā yūpaṃ parivīyāgneyaṃ paśuṃ savanīyapaśum upākaroty agniṣṭome / aindrāgnam ukthye dvitīyam / aindraṃ vṛṣṇiṃ ṣoḍaśini tṛtīyam / sārasvatīṃ meṣīm atirātre caturthīm
13.19.9	vedisaṃmitāṃ vaikādaśinīṃ minoti
13.19.10	samānam ā vapāyā homāt
13.19.11	hutāyāṃ vapāyāṃ prasrapsyanto grahān avekṣante
13.19.12	dvau samudrau vitatāv ajūryāv iti droṇakalaśādhavanīyau
13.19.13	dve dradhasī iti pūtabhṛtam
13.19.14	sarvaṃ rājānam upatiṣṭhante paribhūr agniṃ paribhūr indram iti pratipadya tasya ta idam unmṛja ity antena
13.19.15	prāṇāya ma ity upāṃśupātram
13.19.16	apānāya ma ity antaryāmam
13.19.17	vyānāya ma ity upāṃśusavanam
13.19.18	vāce ma ity aindravāyavam
13.19.19	dakṣakratubhyāṃ ma iti maitrāvaruṇam
13.19.20	cakṣurbhyāṃ ma iti śukrāmanthinau
13.20.1	śrotrāya ma ity āśvinam
13.20.2	ātmane ma ity āgrayaṇam
13.20.3	aṅgebhyo ma ity ukthyam
13.20.4	āyuṣe ma iti dhruvam
13.20.5	tejase me // ojase me // varcase ma ity atigrāhyān
13.20.6	vīryāya ma iti ṣoḍaśipātraṃ yadi ṣoḍaśī bhavati
13.20.7	viṣṇor jaṭharam asīti droṇakalaśam
13.20.8	indrasya jaṭharam asīty ādhavanīyam
13.20.9	viśveṣāṃ devānāṃ jaṭharam asīti pūtabhṛtam
13.20.10	sarvaṃ rājānam upatiṣṭhante ko 'si ko nāmeti pratipadya tasya ta idam unmṛja ity antena
13.20.11	bubhūṣann avekṣeta brahmavarcasakāmo 'vekṣetāmayāvy avekṣetābhicarann avekṣeteti vijñāyate
13.20.12	tata itarāṇi dravyāṇy upatiṣṭhante
13.20.13	utkare vedikaraṇāni sphyaḥ svastir vighanaḥ svastir ity etair mantrair yathārūpam
13.20.14	yajñiyā yajñakṛta stha te māsmin yajña upahvayadhvam iti ca sarvāṇi
13.20.15	upa mā dyāvāpṛthivī hvayetām iti dyāvāpṛthivī
13.20.16	upāstāva ity āstāvam
13.20.17	kalaśa iti droṇakalaśam
13.20.18	soma iti somam
13.20.19	agnir ity āhavanīyam
13.20.20	upa devā upa yajña iti yajñam
13.20.21	upa mā hotrā upahave hvayantām iti hotrakān
13.20.22	hvayatāṃ hvayetāṃ hvayantām ity anuṣaṅgān
13.20.23	namo 'gnaye makhaghna ity āhavanīyam
13.20.24	namo rudrāya makhaghna ity āgnīdhrīyam
13.20.25	nama indrāya makhaghna iti hotrīyam
13.20.26	dṛḍhe sthaḥ śithire samīcī māṃhasas pātam iti dyāvāpṛthivī
13.20.27	sūryo mā devo divyād aṃhasas pātu ity ādityam
13.21.1	vāyur antarikṣād iti vāyum
13.21.2	agniḥ pṛthivyā ity agnim
13.21.3	yamaḥ pitṛbhya iti yamam
13.21.4	sarasvatī manuṣyebhya iti sarasvatīm
13.21.5	devī dvārau mā mā saṃ tāptam iti sadaso dvārau
13.21.6	namaḥ sadasa iti sadaḥ
13.21.7	namaḥ sadasaspataya iti yajamānam
13.21.8	namaḥ sakhīnāṃ purogāṇāṃ cakṣuṣa ity ṛtvijaḥ
13.21.9	namo diva iti divam
13.21.10	namaḥ pṛthivyā iti pṛthivīm
13.21.11	praviśya yatropavekṣyan bhavati tad upatiṣṭhate 'he daidhiṣavyod atas tiṣṭhānyasya sadane sīda yo 'smat pākatara iti
13.21.12	agreṇa praśāstrīyam atikramyopaviśaty un nivata ud udvataś ca geṣam iti
13.21.13	dyāvāpṛthivī samīkṣate pātaṃ mā dyāvāpṛthivī adyāhna iti
13.21.14	sadaso dakṣiṇārdhaṃ parekṣetāganta pitaraḥ pitṛmān ahaṃ yuṣmābhir bhūyāsaṃ suprajaso mayā yūyaṃ bhūyāsteti
13.21.15	savanīyān āsādya saṃpreṣyati prātaḥ prātaḥsāvasyendrāya puroḍāśānām anubrūhīti
13.21.16	juhvām upastīrya sarveṣāṃ haviṣāṃ samavadyati
13.21.17	āmikṣāyā avadāya vājinasyāvadyati / na vā vājinasya
13.21.18	avadāyābhighāryātyākramyāśrāvyāha prātaḥ prātaḥsāvasyendrāya puroḍāśān prasthitān preṣyeti
13.21.19	saṃpreṣyaty agnaye 'nubrūhi // agnaye preṣyeti sviṣṭakṛtaḥ
13.21.20	atraiveḍāṃ niravadyed ity ekam / uparitarām ity aparam
13.22.1	tato dvidevatyaiś carataḥ
13.22.2	vāyava indravāyubhyām anubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati
13.22.3	ādityapātreṇa pratiprasthātaindravāyavasyaikadeśaṃ gṛhṇāti upayāmagṛhīto 'si vākṣasad asi vākpābhyāṃ tvā kratupābhyām asya yajñasya dhruvasyādhyakṣābhyāṃ gṛhṇāmīti
13.22.4	droṇakalaśād gṛhyante 'sannā hūyanta ity ekeṣāṃ pratinigrāhyāṇāṃ vadati
13.22.5	aindravāyavam ādāyādhvaryur droṇakalaśāt pariplavayā rājānam ādāyāghāram āghārayati yatropāṃśur adhvaro yajño 'yam astu devā oṣadhībhya iti
13.22.6	tatraiṣo 'tyantapradeśaḥ / madhye 'gner ājyāhutīḥ paśvāhutīḥ puroḍāśāhutīś ca juhoti / ādyantayor āghārasya somāhutīḥ
13.22.7	yato manyetānabhikramya hoṣyāmīti tat tiṣṭhann āśrāvayet
13.22.8	atyākramyāśrāvyāha vāyava indravāyubhyāṃ preṣyeti
13.22.9	vaṣaṭkṛte juhoti
13.22.10	punar vaṣaṭkṛte juhutaḥ
13.22.11	hutam anumantrayate bhūr asi śreṣṭho raśmīnāṃ prāṇapāḥ prāṇaṃ me pāhi dhūr asi śreṣṭho raśmīnām apānapā apānaṃ me pāhīti
13.22.12	yady enaṃ pūrvaḥ san bhrātṛvyo 'bhiṣyād aṅgulyāṅguṣṭham upanigṛhṇīyād yady aparo 'ṅguṣṭhenāṅguliṃ yo na indravāyū abhidāsatīti
13.22.13	adhvaryupātre pratiprasthātā saṃsrāvam ānayati / adhvaryuḥ pratiprasthātuḥ pātre / pratiprasthātādityasthālyāṃ devebhyas tveti
13.22.14	hotre 'dhvaryur bhakṣaṃ prayacchati mayi vasuḥ purovasur vākpā vācaṃ me pāhīti
13.22.15	etenaiva hotā pratigṛhṇāti
13.23.1	evam evottarābhyāṃ yathādevataṃ pracarataḥ
13.23.2	etāvan nānā / uttareṇa mantreṇa pratinigrāhyaṃ gṛhṇāti / nātrāghāro bhavati / sakṛt sakṛj juhutaḥ / uttareṇottareṇāvabādhate / uttareṇottareṇādityasthālyāṃ saṃpātam avanayati
13.23.3	athainām etenaiva pātreṇāpidadhāti viṣṇav urukramaiṣa te somas taṃ rakṣasva taṃ te duścakṣā māva khyad iti
13.23.4	uttareṇottareṇādhvaryur bhakṣaṃ prayacchati / tena tenaiva hotā pratigṛhṇāti
13.23.5	ādhavanīyaṃ pūtabhṛty avanayati / nyupyādhavanīyam unnetā
13.23.6	saṃpreṣyati unnīyamānebhyo 'nubrūhīti
13.23.7	hotṛcamasam ukhyān nava camasān unnayaty anyatrāchāvākacamasāt
13.23.8	droṇakalaśād upastīrya pūtabhṛta unnīya droṇakalaśād evābhighārayati
13.23.9	tatraiṣo 'tyantapradeśaḥ / yatra kva ca camasān unnayed evamevonnetonnayet / sarvān sarvān evāta ūrdhvaṃ camasān unnayati
13.23.10	savanamukhīyeṣv eva camaseṣūnnīyamānasūktaṃ bhavati
13.23.11	parihita unnīyamānasūkte stuto 'si janadhāḥ / devās tvā śukrapāḥ praṇayantv iti śukram adhvaryur ādatte / stuto 'si janadhāḥ / devās tvā manthipāḥ praṇayantv iti manthinaṃ pratiprasthātā
13.23.12	sāvitreṇobhāv upariṣṭāt prokṣitābhyāṃ śakalābhyām apidhattaḥ
13.23.13	adhastād aprokṣitābhyāṃ pāṃsūn apadhvaṃsayataḥ
13.23.14	apanuttaḥ śaṇḍaḥ sahāmunety adhvaryuḥ / yaṃ dveṣṭi tasya nāma gṛhṇāti
13.23.15	apanutto markaḥ sahāmuneti pratiprasthātā / yaṃ dveṣṭi tasya nāma gṛhṇāti
13.23.16	hastābhyām apidhāya prāñcāv upaniṣkrāmata urv antarikṣaṃ vīhīti
13.24.1	agreṇa havirdhāne grahau saṃdhatto 'ratnī vā brahma saṃdhattaṃ tan me jinvatam / kṣatraṃ saṃdhattaṃ tan me jinvatam / iṣaṃ saṃdhattaṃ tāṃ me jinvatam / ūrjaṃ saṃdhattaṃ tāṃ me jinvatam / rayiṃ saṃdhattaṃ tāṃ me jinvatam / puṣṭiṃ saṃdhattaṃ tāṃ me jinvatam / prajāṃ saṃdhattaṃ tāṃ me jinvatam / paśūn saṃdhattaṃ tān me jinvatam iti
13.24.2	uttaravedyāṃ grahau sādayitvānādhṛṣṭāsi ity aṅguṣṭhābhyām uttaravedim ākramete
13.24.3	vyapariphantāv ivottaravediṃ viparikrāmataḥ
13.24.4	suvīrāḥ prajāḥ prajanayan parīhi / śukraḥ śukraśociṣā iti dakṣiṇenādhvaryuḥ / suprajāḥ prajāḥ prajanayan parīhi / manthī manthiśociṣetyuttareṇa pratiprasthātā
13.24.5	śukraṃ yajamāno 'nvārabhata indreṇa sayujo vayaṃ sāsahyāma pṛtanyata iti
13.24.6	agreṇottaravediṃ grahau saṃdhatto 'ratnī vā saṃjagmānau diva ā pṛthivyāḥ / āyuḥ saṃdhattaṃ tan me jinvatam / prāṇaṃ saṃdhattaṃ taṃ me jinvatam / apānaṃ saṃdhattaṃ taṃ me jinvatam / vyānaṃ saṃdhattaṃ taṃ me jinvatam / cakṣuḥ saṃdhattaṃ tan me jinvatam / śrotraṃ saṃdhattaṃ tan me jinvatam / manaḥ saṃdhattaṃ tan me jinvatam / vācaṃ saṃdhattaṃ tāṃ me jinvatam iti
13.24.7	athaināv adhvaryur abhimantrayata āyuḥ stha āyur me dhattam / āyur yajñāya dhattam / āyur yajñapataye dhattam / prāṇaḥ sthaḥ prāṇaṃ me dhattam / prāṇaṃ yajñāya dhattam / prāṇaṃ yajñapataye dhattam / cakṣuḥ sthaś cakṣur me dhattam / cakṣur yajñāya dhattam / cakṣur yajñapataye dhattam / śrotraṃ sthaḥ śrotraṃ me dhattam / śrotraṃ yajñāya dhattam / śrotraṃ yajñapataye dhattam
13.25.1	tau devau śukrāmanthinau / kalpayataṃ daivīr viśaḥ / kalpayataṃ mānuṣīḥ / iṣam ūrjam asmāsu dhattam / prāṇān paśuṣu / prajāṃ mayi ca yajamāne ceti
13.25.2	purastāt pratyañcāv uttaravedim ākramya bahirvedy aprokṣitau śakalau nirasyatas tenaiva mantreṇa
13.25.3	apa upaspṛśyāgnau prokṣitau prāsyataḥ / śukrasya samid asīty adhvaryuḥ / manthinaḥ samid asi iti pratiprasthātā
13.25.4	paścāt prāñcaś camasādhvaryavaś camasair avatiṣṭhante
13.25.5	āśrāvya pratyāśrāvite saṃpreṣyati prātaḥ prātaḥsāvasya śukravato manthivato madhuścuta indrāya somān prasthitān preṣya madhyataḥkāriṇāṃ camasādhvaryavo vaṣaṭkṛtānuvaṣaṭkṛtāñ juhuta hotrakāṇāṃ camasādhvaryavaḥ sakṛt sakṛd bhūtvā śukrasyābhyunnīyopāvartadhvam iti
13.25.6	vaṣaṭkṛte juhvati
13.25.7	śukrāmanthinau juhutaḥ / sa prathamaḥ saṃkṛtir viśvakarmā / sa prathamo mitro varuṇo agniḥ / sa prathamo bṛhaspatiś cikitvān / tasmā indrāya sutam ā juhomi svāhā // ity adhvaryuḥ / tasmai sūryāya sutam ā juhomi svāheti pratiprasthātā
13.25.8	sānuvaṣaṭkārāv eke śukrāmanthinau samāmananti / ananuvaṣaṭkārāv eke / anyataraṃ sānuvaṣaṭkāram eke
13.25.9	anuvaṣaṭkṛte madhyataḥkāriṇāṃ camasāj juhvaty apayacchantītarān
13.25.10	uttarataḥpurastād aṅgārān nirvartya pratiprasthātā manthinaḥ saṃsrāvaṃ juhoty eṣa te rudra bhāgo yaṃ nirayācathās taṃ juṣasva svāheti
13.25.11	sūdavacchukrapātram āyatane sādayitvā saṃpreṣyati praitu hotuś camasaḥ pra brahmaṇaḥ prodgātuḥ pra yajamānasyeti
13.25.12	ete madhyataḥkāriṇāṃ camasā bhavanti
13.26.1	tataḥ punar abhyunnītaiś caranti
13.26.2	droṇakalaśād abhyunnītā bhavanti
13.26.3	maitrāvaruṇacamasam ādāyādhvaryur atyākramyāśrāvyāha praśāstar yajeti / vaṣaṭkṛte juhoti
13.26.4	evam anupūrvaṃ yo yo yajate taṃ taṃ saṃpreṣyati brahman yaja / potar yaja / neṣṭar yaja / agnīd yajeti
13.26.5	eteṣām ete camasā bhavanti
13.26.6	sarvāsu somāhutīṣv anuvaṣaṭkāra āmnāto bhavati
13.26.7	ayāḍ agnīd iti hotra ācaṣṭe
13.26.8	sa bhadram akar yo naḥ somaṃ pāyayiṣyatīti hotā pratyāha
13.26.9	bhakṣam abhimantrayate bhakṣehi māviśeti
13.26.10	pratigṛhṇāty aśvinos tvā bāhubhyāṃ saghyāsam iti
13.26.11	avekṣate nṛcakṣasaṃ tvā deva soma sucakṣā ava khyeṣam iti
13.26.12	yatra kva ca bhakṣayed evam evaitān mantrāñ japet
13.26.13	athaitam upahavam iṣṭvā prāṇeṣūpaniyamya bhakṣayati mandrābhibhūtir iti
13.26.14	ye ke cānaindrā anārāśaṃsāḥ prātaḥsavana eṣa evaiteṣāṃ bhakṣamantro bhavati
13.26.15	vāg devī somasya tṛpyatv ity eke sārvatrikaṃ samāmananti
13.26.16	dvir aindravāyavaṃ bhakṣayati sakṛt sakṛd itarau / cakṣuṣor upanigrāhaṃ maitrāvaruṇam / śrotrayor upanigrāhaṃ sarvataḥ parihāram āśvinam
13.27.1	hotā prathamo bhakṣayaty athādhvaryur atha pratiprasthātā
13.27.2	yatra kva caikapātre bhakṣayeyur dvau vā bahavo vā vaṣaṭkartaiva prathamo bhakṣayet
13.27.3	ye ke caikakāle bhakṣayeyuḥ sarva eva mithaḥ karmanāmabhiḥ samupahvayeran
13.27.4	asāv asāv upahvayasvety āmantraṇaḥ / upahūta iti prativacanaḥ
13.27.5	bhakṣayitvātmānaṃ pratyabhimṛśati hinva me gātrā hariva iti
13.27.6	yatra kva ca bhakṣayed evam evātmānaṃ pratyabhimṛśet
13.27.7	bhakṣayitvā nānūtsṛjanty āvanayanāt
13.27.8	hotṛcamase dvidevatyasaṃpātān avanīya puroḍāśaśakalam aindravāyavasya pātre 'vadadhāti / payasyāṃ maitrāvaruṇasya / dhānā āśvinasya
13.27.9	athaitāni dakṣiṇasya havirdhānasyottarasyāṃ vartanyāṃ paścādakṣaṃ sādayati
13.27.10	evaṃ sannāny eva bhavanty ā tṛtīyasavanāt
13.27.11	niravadāya hotra iḍām ādadhāti
13.27.12	upahvayate hoteḍām
13.27.13	upodyacchanty asmai camasān
13.27.14	hotṛcamasaṃ saṃspṛṣṭaṃ dhārayati
13.27.15	upahūtām iḍāṃ prāśnanti ye prakṛtau
13.27.16	puroḍāśaśakalam acchāvākāya nidadhāti
13.27.17	yathācamasaṃ camasino bhakṣayanti
13.27.18	vasumadgaṇasya soma deva ta iti madhyataḥkāriṇaḥ
13.27.19	anaindrair evetareṣāṃ bhakṣamantro vyākhyātaḥ
13.27.20	sarveṣu camaseṣu hotā bhakṣayati
13.27.21	sarveṣu punar abhyunnīteṣv adhvaryuḥ mandrābhibhūtir iti
13.27.22	yataro 'dhvaryur juhuyāt sa vaṣaṭkartāraṃ pratibhakṣayet
13.27.23	bhakṣayitvāpyāyayati ā pyāyasva sametu ta iti
13.27.24	yatra kva cāpyāyayed etayaivāpyāyayet
13.27.25	sīdanti nārāśaṃsā āpyāyitā dakṣiṇasya havirdhānasyādhastād apālambe
13.28.1	sīdaty acchāvāko 'greṇa svaṃ dhiṣṇiyaṃ bahiḥ sadasaḥ
13.28.2	tasmai puroḍāśaśakalam ādadhad āhācchāvāka vadasva yat te vādyam iti
13.28.3	yatrābhijānāty upo asmān brāhmaṇān brāhmaṇā hvayadhvam iti tata āhācchāvāko vā ayam upahavam icchate taṃ hotar upahvayasveti
13.28.4	tam ṛcā hotopahvayate
13.28.5	yatrābhijānāty uta no gāva upahūtā upahūta iti tata āhonnīyamānāyānubrūhīti
13.28.6	unnītam acchāvākacamasam ādāyātyākramyāśrāvyāhācchāvāka yajeti
13.28.7	vaṣaṭkṛte juhoti
13.28.8	acchāvākāya bhakṣaṃ prayacchati
13.28.9	nāsminn acchāvāka upahavam icchate
13.28.10	naitena saṃbhakṣayet
13.28.11	yady asminn upahavam iccheta bhakṣayety enaṃ brūyāt
13.28.12	bhakṣitam acchāvākacamasam āpyāyitam antareṇa neṣṭuś cāgnīdhrasya ca camasau sādayati
13.28.13	atra savanīyānāṃ piṣṭalepaphalīkaraṇahomau juhoti
13.28.14	kapālāni vimuñcati
13.28.15	atraike vājinacaryāṃ samāmananti
13.29.1	tata ṛtugrahaiś carataḥ
13.29.2	dakṣiṇam ṛtupātram adhvaryur ādatta uttaraṃ pratiprasthātā
13.29.3	saha prathamau gṛhṇītaḥ sahottamau
13.29.4	gṛhṇāty adhvaryur upayāmagṛhīto 'si madhuś ceti / upayāmagṛhīto 'si mādhavaś ceti pratiprasthātā
13.29.5	upaniṣkramyādhvaryur atyākramyāśrāvyāhartunā preṣyeti
13.29.6	vaṣaṭkṛte juhoti
13.29.7	āvartate 'dhvaryuḥ
13.29.8	upaniṣkramya pratiprasthātātyākramyāśrāvyāhartunā preṣyeti
13.29.9	vaṣaṭkṛte juhoti
13.29.10	nānyo'nyam anuprapadyeta / dvāra eva vyatītaḥ
13.29.11	prasiddham evādhvaryur dakṣiṇena prapadyate / prasiddhaṃ pratiprasthātottareṇa
13.29.12	pratyañcaṃ yantam adhvaryuṃ pratiprasthātā graheṇa paripragṛhṇāti / prāñcaṃ yantaṃ pātreṇa
13.29.13	evam evottarair uttarair mantrair gṛhṇītaḥ
13.29.14	pūrveṇa pūrveṇādhvaryur uttareṇottareṇa pratiprasthātā
13.29.15	adhvaryur eva trayodaśaṃ gṛhṇāti upayāmagṛhīto 'si saṃsarpo 'sy aṃhaspatyāya tveti
13.29.16	dvādaśa gṛhyanta iti vijñāyate / trayodaśety ekeṣām / caturdaśety ekeṣām
13.29.17	saha prathamau juhuto yadi trayodaśa gṛhyante
13.29.18	saha prathamau sahottamau yadi caturdaśa
13.30.1	pūrveṣāṃ śeṣa uttarān abhigṛhṇītaḥ
13.30.2	asannā hūyante
13.30.3	ṛtunā preṣyeti trir adhvaryur āha / triḥ pratiprasthātā
13.30.4	paryāvṛtya pātram ṛtubhiḥ preṣyeti dvir adhvaryur āha / dviḥ pratiprasthātā
13.30.5	paryāvṛtya pātram ṛtunā preṣyeti sakṛd adhvaryur āha / sakṛt pratiprasthātā
13.30.6	yatrābhijānāty adhvaryū yajatam iti tad adhvaryur āha hotar etad yajeti
13.30.7	yatrābhijānāti gṛhapate yajeti tad yajamāna āha hotar etad yajeti
13.30.8	ananuvaṣaṭkārā ṛtugrahā bhavanti
13.30.9	adhvaryupātre pratiprasthātā saṃsrāvam ānayati / adhvaryuḥ pratiprasthātuḥ pātre
13.30.10	pratiprasthātā tena bhakṣam āharati
13.30.11	evam anupūrvaṃ yo yo yajati taṃ taṃ pratibhakṣayato mandrābhibhūtir iti / hotāram adhvaryuḥ / potāraṃ pratiprasthātā / neṣṭāram adhvaryuḥ / āgnīdhraṃ pratiprasthātā / brāhmaṇācchaṃsinam adhvaryuḥ / maitrāvaruṇaṃ pratiprasthātā / hotāram adhvaryuḥ / potāraṃ pratiprasthātā / neṣṭāram adhvaryuḥ / achāvākaṃ pratiprasthātā / hotāram evādhvaryuḥ / hotāraṃ pratiprasthātā
13.30.12	atraiva pātraṃ nidhāyādhvaryuḥ svena pātreṇa
13.31.1	sasaṃsrāveṇaindrāgnaṃ gṛhṇātīndrāgnī āgata sutam iti
13.31.2	śastram atra bhavati
13.31.3	agreṇa hotāram upaviśyādhvaryuḥ śastram upākarotīḍā devahūr ity anuvākaśeṣeṇa
13.31.4	etenaiva sarvāṇi śastrāṇy upākaroti
13.31.5	athainaṃ parāñcam ūrdhvajñum āsīnam abhyāhvayate hotā
13.31.6	śoṃsā moda iveti pradakṣiṇam āvartate
13.31.7	ṛtupātram ārabhyordhvas tiṣṭhan sadobile pratigṛṇāti prahvo vā
13.31.8	oyā moda ivety ardharceṣu
13.31.9	omothā moda iveti praṇaveṣu
13.31.10	nābhipratigṛṇīyāt / nārdharcāl lupyate
13.31.11	yatra yatra hotā viramed omothā moda ivety eva brūyāt
13.31.12	ubhayaṃ vyāhāve karoti śoṃsā moda ivothā moda iveti
13.31.13	paridhānīyāyā uttamena praṇavena saha praṇauti
13.31.14	evam eva sarvāṇi śastrāṇi pratigṛṇāty anyatra pātrārambhaṇāt
13.31.15	śastram anumantrayate śastrasya śastram asīti
13.31.16	etenaiva sarvāṇi śastrāṇy anumantrayate
13.31.17	śastraṃ pratigīryādatte graham adhvaryuḥ / ādadate nārāśaṃsān
13.31.18	atyākramyāśrāvyāhokthaśā yaja somasyeti
13.31.19	vaṣaṭkṛte juhoti
13.32.1	vaṣaṭkāraṃ cānuvaṣaṭkāraṃ cānu prakampayanti nārāśaṃsān
13.32.2	aindrair eva grahabhakṣamantro vyākhyātaḥ
13.32.3	nārāśaṃsān bhakṣayanti narāśaṃsapītasya soma deva ta iti
13.32.4	evam evottareṇottareṇa nārāśaṃsena savane savane nārāśaṃsān bhakṣayanti
13.32.5	asarvān bhakṣayitvāpyāyayanti
13.32.6	vyākhyātam āpyāyanaṃ sādanam
13.32.7	vaiśvadevaṃ śukrapātreṇa gṛhṇāty omāsaś carṣaṇīdhṛta ity etenānuvākena
13.32.8	stutaśastre atra bhavataḥ
13.32.9	śastraṃ pratigīryādatte graham adhvaryuḥ / ādadate nārāśaṃsān
13.32.10	atyākramyāśrāvyāhokthaśā yaja somasyeti
13.32.11	vaṣaṭkṛte juhoti
13.32.12	vyākhyātam anuprakampanam
13.32.13	vyākhyāto grahasya bhakṣamantraḥ
13.32.14	vyākhyāto nārāśaṃsānām
13.32.15	sarvān bhakṣayanti / nāpyāyayanti / mārjayante
13.32.16	sarvabhakṣā evāta ūrdhvaṃ prātaḥsavane camasā bhavanti
13.32.17	tata ukthyaṃ vigṛhṇāti
13.32.18	ukthyasthālyā ukthyapātre tṛtīyaṃ gṛhṇāty upayāmagṛhīto'si mitrāvaruṇābhyāṃ tveti
13.32.19	athainaṃ sādayaty eṣa te yonir mitrāvaruṇābhyāṃ tveti
13.32.20	punar havir asīti sthālīṃ pratyabhimṛśati
13.32.21	maitrāvaruṇacamasamukhyāṃś camasān unnayati
13.32.22	stutaśastre atra bhavataḥ
13.32.23	śastraṃ pratigīryādatte graham adhvaryuḥ / ādadate camasāṃś camasādhvaryavaḥ
13.32.24	atyākramyāśrāvyāhokthaśā yaja somānām iti
13.32.25	vaṣaṭkṛte juhvati
13.32.26	maitrāvaruṇacamase 'dhvaryuḥ saṃsrāvam avanayati devebhyas tvā devāyuvaṃ pṛṇajmi yajñasyāyuṣa iti
13.33.1	yadi kāmayetādhvaryur ātmānaṃ yajñayaśasenārpayeyam ity etad yathāsamāmnātam
13.33.2	yathācamasaṃ camasino bhakṣayanti mandrābhibhūtir iti
13.33.3	evaṃ pratiprasthātottarābhyām ukthyavigrahābhyām abhakṣayan pracarati
13.33.4	yo yo mukhyaś camasas tasmiṃs tasmin saṃsrāvam avanayati
13.33.5	brāhmaṇāchaṃsicamasamukhyo dvitīyaḥ / acchāvākacamasamukhyas tṛtīyaḥ
13.33.6	etena śastrayājyānām ānupūrvyaṃ vyākhyātam
13.33.7	etāvan nānā / indrāya tveti brāhmaṇāchaṃsino grahaṇasādanau bhavataḥ / aindro bhakṣamantraḥ / indrāgnibhyāṃ tvety acchāvākasya grahaṇasādanau bhavataḥ / mandrābhibhūtir iti bhakṣamantraḥ
13.33.8	uttamam ukthyavigrahaṃ gṛhītvā na sthālīṃ pratyabhimṛśati
13.33.9	nyupyokthyasthālīṃ ṣoḍaśinaṃ gṛhṇāty ā tiṣṭha vṛtrahan ratham ity etenānuvākenottareṇa vā
13.33.10	api cainaṃ dhārāgrahāṇām uttamaṃ gṛhṇīyāt
13.33.11	evam evottareṇānuvākena savane savane ṣoḍaśinam abhigṛhṇāti
13.33.12	ṣoḍaśinaṃ gṛhītvā saṃpreṣyaty uttamāṃś camasān unnaya droṇakalaśaṃ pūtabhṛty avanaya sarvaṃ rājānaṃ camaseṣūnnaya daśābhiḥ kalaśau mṛṣṭvā nyubjeti
13.33.13	ukthaśā ity āha prātaḥsavanaṃ pratigīrya
13.33.14	agniḥ prātaḥsavane pātv asmān ity āhutiṃ hutvā saṃpreṣyati praśāstaḥ prasuhīti
13.33.15	sarpatety āha praśāstā
13.33.16	saṃtiṣṭhate prātaḥsavanam
14.1.1	mādhyaṃdinaṃ savanaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
14.1.2	tasya prātaḥsavanena kalpo vyākhyātaḥ
14.1.3	vikārān anukramiṣyāmaḥ
14.1.4	tataḥ saṃpreṣyati pratiprasthātaḥ savanīyān nirvapeti
14.1.5	vasatīvarībhir hotṛcamasaṃ pūrayitvā nigrābhyāsu yajamānaṃ vācayati yathā prātaḥsavane
14.1.6	adhiṣavaṇacarmaṇi sarvaṃ rājānaṃ nyupya grāvastuta uṣṇīṣaṃ prayacchati
14.1.7	asaṃpreṣito grāvastotrīyā anvāha
14.1.8	mahābhiṣavam abhiṣuṇvanti yathā prātaḥsavane
14.1.9	etāvan nānā / ihābhya ihety abhiṣuṇvanti
14.1.10	uttamasyābhiṣavasya madhyame paryāye bṛhad ity abhiṣuṇvanti
14.1.11	athottamaṃ paryāyaṃ rādhayanta ivābhiṣuṇvantīhābhya iha ihābhya iheti
14.1.12	uttame paryāye 'bhiṣuto rājā bhavaty asaṃbhṛto 'tha pratiprasthātā grāvṇo 'numodate devā grāvāṇa indur indrety avādiṣuḥ / endram acucyavuḥ / paramasyāḥ parāvataḥ / āsmāt sadhasthāt / oror antarikṣāt / ā subhūtam asuṣavuḥ / brahmavarcasaṃ ma ā suṣavuḥ / samare rakṣāṃsy avadhiṣuḥ / apahataṃ brahmajyasyeti
14.1.13	samānam ā grahakālāt
14.1.14	śukrāmanthināv evāgre gṛhṇāti
14.1.15	āgrayaṇaṃ tisṛbhyo dhārābhyo gṛhṇāti
14.1.16	ya evāgrayaṇasthālyāṃ rājā tam anyasmin pātre paryāsicya dvitīyāṃ dhārāṃ kurute / udacanāt tṛtīyām
14.1.17	ukthyasyāvṛtokthyaṃ gṛhītvā
14.2.1	ṛtupātrābhyāṃ marutvatīyau gṛhṇāti / adhvaryupātreṇa pūrvaṃ marutvantaṃ vṛṣabhaṃ vāvṛdhānam iti / pratiprasthātreṇottaram indra marutva iha pāhi somam iti
14.2.2	droṇakalaśe rājānam atipāvayati yāvantaṃ mādhyaṃdināya savanāyāptaṃ manyate
14.2.3	samānam ā pavamānāt
14.2.4	pratyañcaḥ prahvā mādhyaṃdinaṃ pavamānaṃ sarpanti traiṣṭubhaḥ panthā rudrā devatā vṛkeṇāparipareṇa pathā svasti rudrānaśīyeti / vāg agregā agra etv iti ca
14.2.5	uttareṇa havirdhāne dakṣiṇena mārjālīyaṃ parītya pūrvayā dvārā sadaḥ praviśyāgreṇa hotrīyam adhvaryur avatiṣṭhate / agreṇa praśāstrīyam atikramyetare
14.2.6	mādhyaṃdinena pavamānena stuvate
14.2.7	stūyamāne yajamāno 'nvārohaṃ japati suparṇo 'si triṣṭupchandā iti
14.2.8	samānam ā saṃpraiṣāt
14.2.9	nātra paśuṃ pracodayati / na rājānam upatiṣṭhate / pratiprasthātar dadhigharmeṇānūdehīti saṃpraiṣāntaṃ namati
14.2.10	samānam ā savanīyānāṃ nirvapaṇāt
14.2.11	savanīyān nirvapsyann āgneyaṃ paśupuroḍāśaṃ nirvapaty agniṣṭome / aindrāgnam ukthye dvitīyam / aindraṃ ṣoḍaśini tṛtīyam / sārasvatam atirātre caturtham
14.2.12	tataḥ savanīyān nirvapati
14.2.13	etāvan nānā / nottarayoḥ savanayoḥ payasyā bhavati
14.2.14	vyākhyātaṃ savanīyānāṃ nirvapaṇaṃ barhistaraṇam alaṃkaraṇaṃ grahāvakāśopasthānaṃ sarpaṇam iti
14.2.15	dadhigharmeṇa carati
14.2.16	audumbaryāṃ srucyām āgnīdhrīye dadhi gṛhṇāti yāvatī dyāvāpṛthivī mahitveti
14.3.1	athaitad āgnīdhre 'dhiśrayati vāk ca tvā manaś ca śrīṇītām / prāṇaś ca tvāpānaś ca śrīṇītām / cakṣuś ca tvā śrotraṃ ca śrīṇītām / dakṣaś ca tvā balaṃ ca śrīṇītām / ojaś ca tvā sahaś ca śrīṇītām / āyuś ca tvā jarā ca śrīṇītām / ātmā ca tvā tanūś ca śrīṇītām / śṛto 'si śṛtaṃkṛtaḥ / śṛtāya tvā śrtebhyas tveti
14.3.2	tataḥ saṃpreṣyati hotar vadasva yat te vādyam iti
14.3.3	yatrābhijānāti yadi śrāto juhotana yady aśrāto mamattaneti tata āha śrātaṃ havir iti
14.3.4	atyākramyāśrāvyāha dadhigharmasya yajeti
14.3.5	vaṣaṭkṛte juhoti yam indram āhur varuṇaṃ yam āhuḥ / yaṃ mitram āhur yam u satyam āhuḥ / yo devānāṃ devatamas tapojāḥ / tasmai tvā tebhyas tvā svāhā / iti
14.3.6	anuvaṣaṭkṛte dvitīyaṃ hutvāvaśinaṣṭi
14.3.7	taṃ te bhakṣayanti ye pravargyam / tasyāraṇye 'nuvākye bhakṣamantraḥ
14.3.8	nāpravargye dadhigharmo vidyata ity aparam
14.3.9	tataḥ savanīyān āsādayati
14.3.10	paśupuroḍāśena pracarya savanīyaiḥ pracarati
14.3.11	etāvan nānā / mādhyaṃdinasya savanasyendrāya puroḍāśānām anubrūhi / mādhyaṃdinasya savanasyendrāya puroḍāśān prasthitān preṣyeti saṃpreṣyati
14.3.12	sarveṣāṃ sapaśupuroḍāśānāṃ samānaḥ sviṣṭakṛt praiṣavān samāneḍā
14.3.13	na savanīyasya paśupuroḍāśo vidyata ity aparam
14.3.14	ādhavanīyaṃ pūtabhṛty avanayati
14.3.15	samānam ā saṃpraiṣāt
14.3.16	etāvan nānā / mādhyaṃdinasya savanasya niṣkevalyasya bhāgasya śukravato manthivato madhuścuta iti saṃpraiṣādiḥ
14.3.17	samānam ā punarabhyunnītebhyaḥ
14.3.18	pūrva āgnīdhrād acchāvākaḥ saṃyajati
14.3.19	nātra puroḍāśaśakalam acchāvākāya nidadhāti
14.3.20	yathācamasaṃ camasino bhakṣayanti
14.3.21	rudravadgaṇasya soma deva ta ity eṣa eva mādhyaṃdine savane bhakṣamantro bhavaty anyatra nārāśaṃsebhyaḥ
14.3.22	asarvān bhakṣayitvāpyāyayanti
14.3.23	vyākhyātam āpyāyanaṃ sādanam
14.4.1	sanneṣu nārāśaṃseṣūttareṇa havirdhāna uttareṇāgnīdhrīyam uttareṇa sadaḥ parītya pūrvayā dvārā prāgvaṃśaṃ praviśyāpareṇa śālāmukhīyam upaviśya juhvāṃ caturgṛhītam ājyaṃ gṛhītvā darbheṇa hiraṇyaṃ niṣṭarkyaṃ baddhvāvadadhāti
14.4.2	amātyānāṃ saṃhvānaṃ samanvārambhaṇaṃ saṃpracchādanam iti vaisarjaneṣu vyākhyātam
14.4.3	vāsaso 'ntaṃ srugdaṇḍa upaniyamya juhoti dākṣiṇāni
14.4.4	ud u tyam / citram iti dvābhyāṃ gārhapatye juhoti
14.4.5	aparaṃ caturgṛhītaṃ gṛhītvā
14.4.6	divaṃ gaccha suvaḥ pateti hiraṇyaṃ hutvodgṛhṇāti
14.4.7	athainā dakṣiṇā dakṣiṇena vedim avasthitā bhavanti gavāṃ dvādaśaśataṃ tilā māṣā odano mantho 'jo 'vir vāso hiraṇyam ano ratho 'śvo hastī puruṣa iti / ekaviṃśatir ity ekeṣām / caturviṃśatir ity ekeṣām / aparimitā ity ekeṣām / sarvavedasam ity ekeṣām
14.4.8	hiraṇyaṃ cājyaṃ ca dhārayamāṇo yajamāno dakṣiṇā abhyaiti rūpeṇa vo rūpam abhyaimi vayasā vaya iti
14.4.9	tutho vo viśvavedā vibhajatv iti madhyam avakrāmati
14.4.10	athaināḥ kṛṣṇājinena vyuttrāsya vibhajya vāvibhajya vātyānayaty agreṇa prāgvaṃśaṃ jaghanena sado 'ntareṇa neṣṭuś cāgnīdhrasya ca
14.4.11	tā udīcīr antareṇa cātvālaṃ cāgnīdhraṃ cotsṛjati
14.4.12	atyāyatīṣv āhavanīyam abhimantrayata etat te agne rādha eti somacyutam iti pratipadya yajñasya pathā suvitā nayantīr ity antena
14.5.1	āgnīdhra etad ājyaṃ juhoty agne naya supathā rāye asmān ity etayā
14.5.2	vaneṣu vy antarikṣaṃ tatāneti vāruṇyā dvitīyayā juhuyād yady ano ratho 'śvo vāso 'pi vā dīyate
14.5.3	prājāpatyayā tṛtīyayā juhuyād yadi hastinaṃ puruṣaṃ vā dāsyan syāt
14.5.4	ātreyāya prathamāya hiraṇyaṃ dadāti madhyamāyety ekeṣām uttamāyety ekeṣāṃ brāhmaṇam adya rādhyāsam ṛṣim ārṣeyam iti
14.5.5	yady ātreyaṃ na vinded ya ārṣeyaḥ saṃhitas tasmai dadyāt
14.5.6	āgnīdhrāyāgra upabarhaṇaṃ sārvasūtraṃ dadāty ajaṃ ca
14.5.7	tato brahmaṇe yathānyāṃ dakṣiṇāṃ nātidhyāyed evaṃ dadyāt
14.5.8	tata udgātṛbhyo hotṛbhyaḥ
14.5.9	adhvaryubhyas tu havirdhāna āsīnebhyaḥ
14.5.10	antataḥ pratihartre dadāti
14.5.11	ardham ardhibhyas tṛtīyaṃ tṛtīyibhyaḥ pādaṃ pādibhyaḥ / te dvādaśāhe vyākhyātāḥ
14.5.12	ṛtvigbhyo dattvā prasarpakebhyo dadāti
14.5.13	ete dakṣiṇena pṛṣṭhyām antaḥ sadasy upaviṣṭā bhavanti
14.5.14	nānārṣeyāya viduṣe dadāti / nārṣeyāyāviduṣe / ārṣeyāyaiva viduṣe dadāti
14.5.15	na kaṇvakaśyapebhyo na jñātaye nartvije prasṛptāya na bhīto na yācamānāya / yāṃ yācamānāya dadāty enaṃ sā dakṣiṇā gacchatīti vijñāyate
14.5.16	brāhmaṇāya śrotriyāyāntarvedy āsīnāya dakṣiṇāṃ dadāti
14.5.17	apy abrāhmaṇāya vidyāvide deyam
14.6.1	yām anyo dīyamānāṃ na kāmayeta yaṃ dviṣyāt tasmai tāṃ dakṣiṇāṃ dadyād anyena dhanena saha
14.6.2	kuta etebhyo dadyāt / etasmād eva dvādaśācchatād ity ekam / anyata ity aparam
14.6.3	vi suvaḥ paśya vy antarikṣam iti sadaḥ prekṣeta
14.6.4	saṃnītā dakṣiṇā anumantrayate 'smaddātrā devatrā gacchatety anuvākaśeṣeṇa
14.6.5	āgnīdhre vaiśvakarmaṇāni juhoti yajñapatim ṛṣaya enasāhur iti pañca
14.6.6	cātvāle kṛṣṇaviṣāṇāṃ prāsyati / hariṇasya raghuṣyato 'dhi śīrṣaṇi bheṣajam / sukṣetriyaṃ viṣāṇayā viṣūcīnam anīnaśat // anu tvā hariṇo mṛgaḥ padbhiś caturbhir akramīt / viṣāṇe viṣyaitaṃ granthiṃ yad asya gulphidaṃ hṛdi mano yad asya gulphidam // ity etābhyām
14.6.7	tataḥ saṃpreṣyatīndrāya marutvate 'nubrūhīti
14.6.8	yadā marutvate 'nūktaṃ bhavaty atha na dīyata ānūbandhyāvapāyā homāt
14.6.9	pūrvagṛhītam adhvaryur ādatta uttaraṃ pratiprasthātā
14.6.10	atyākramyāśrāvyāhendrāya marutvate preṣyeti
14.6.11	vaṣaṭkṛte juhutaḥ
14.6.12	sānuvaṣaṭkārāv eke marutvatīyau samāmananti / ananuvaṣaṭkārāv eke / uttaraṃ sānuvaṣaṭkāram eke
14.6.13	vyavanayete yathartugraheṣu
14.6.14	pratiprasthānena bhakṣayanti
14.6.15	atraiva pātraṃ nidhāyādhvaryuḥ svena pātreṇa saṃsrāveṇottamaṃ marutvatīyaṃ gṛhṇāti marutvāṁ indra vṛṣabho raṇāyeti
14.6.16	śastram atra bhavati
14.6.17	ṛtupātram ārabhya pratigṛṇāti
14.6.18	śastraṃ pratigīryādatte graham adhvaryuḥ / ādadate nārāśaṃsān
14.6.19	atyākramyāśrāvyāhokthaśā yaja somasyeti
14.6.20	vaṣaṭkṛte juhoti
14.6.21	vyākhyātam anuprakampanam
14.6.22	vyākhyāto grahasya bhakṣamantraḥ
14.6.23	vyākhyāto nārāśaṃsānām
14.6.24	asarvān bhakṣayitvāpyāyayanti
14.6.25	vyākhyātam āpyāyanaṃ sādanam
14.7.1	māhendraṃ śukrapātreṇa gṛhṇāti mahāṁ indro ya ojasety etenānuvākenottareṇa vā
14.7.2	stutaśastre atra bhavataḥ
14.7.3	stotram upākṛtya saṃpreṣyaty abhiṣotāro 'bhiṣuṇutolūkhalān udvādayāgnīd āśiraṃ vinaya saumyasya vittād iti
14.7.4	atra tārtīyasavanīyakam abhiṣavam abhiṣuṇuyāt savanīyān saumyam iti nirvaped āśiraṃ vinayed ity ekam / tṛtīyasavana ity aparam
14.7.5	śastraṃ pratigīryādatte graham adhvaryuḥ / ādadate nārāśaṃsān / ādadate 'tigrāhyān
14.7.6	atyākramyāśrāvyāhokthaśā yaja somasyeti
14.7.7	vaṣaṭkṛte juhoti
14.7.8	vyākhyātam anuprakampanam
14.7.9	tato 'tigrāhyān juhvaty agne tejasvin ity etair mantrair yathārūpam
14.7.10	vyākhyāto grahasya bhakṣamantraḥ
14.7.11	tato 'tigrāhyān bhakṣayanti mayi medhāṃ mayi prajām ity etair mantrair yathārūpam
14.7.12	vyākhyāto nārāśaṃsānām
14.7.13	sarvān bhakṣayanti
14.7.14	nāpyāyayanti / mārjayante
14.7.15	sarvabhakṣā evāta ūrdhvaṃ mādhyaṃdine camasā bhavanti
14.7.16	tata ukthyaṃ vigṛhṇāti yathā prātaḥsavane
14.7.17	etāvan nānā / indrāya tvā // indrāya tveti sarvatra grahaṇasādanau bhavataḥ
14.7.18	aindro bhakṣamantraḥ
14.7.19	tasminn eva kāle ṣoḍaśinam abhigṛhṇāti
14.7.20	ṣoḍaśinaṃ gṛhītvā saṃpreṣyaty uttamāṃś camasān unnaya droṇakalaśaṃ pūtabhṛty avanaya sarvaṃ rājānaṃ camaseṣūnnaya daśābhiḥ kalaśau mṛṣṭvā nyubjeti
14.7.21	ukthaṃ vācīty āha mādhyaṃdinaṃ savanaṃ pratigīrya
14.7.22	viśve devā maruta indro asmān ity āhutiṃ hutvā saṃpreṣyati praśāstaḥ prasuhīti
14.7.23	sarpatety āha praśāstā
14.7.24	saṃtiṣṭhate mādhyaṃdinaṃ savanam
14.8.1	tṛtīyasavanaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
14.8.2	yadā bahavo 'ntarvedi syur athādityaṃ gṛhṇīyāt
14.8.3	yasya bhrātṛvyaḥ somena yajeta yāvad ādityaṃ gṛhṇīyāt tāvad bahirvedi tiṣṭhet
14.8.4	yasya prasṛpto bhrātṛvyaḥ syād antarvedi saty ādityaṃ gṛhṇīyāt
14.8.5	havirdhānayor dvāre apidhāyādityasthālyā ādityapātre tṛtīyaṃ gṛhṇāti kadā cana starīr asīty etābhis tisṛbhiḥ
14.8.6	somam agre gṛhṇāty atha śṛtātaṅkyaṃ dadhy atha somam / triṣṭubhā madhyato dadhi gṛhṇātīti vijñāyate
14.8.7	yā divyā vṛṣṭis tayā tvā śrīṇāmīti dadhnopariṣṭād vṛṣṭikāmasya śrīṇīyāt / na madhyato dadhi gṛhṇīyāt
14.8.8	sūdavadādityasthālīm āyatane sādayitvopāṃśusavanaṃ grahe 'vadadhāti vivasva ādityaiṣa te somapītha iti
14.8.9	tam udyamya vijñānam upaiti / yadi tājag binduḥ praskanded varṣukaḥ parjanyaḥ syāt / yadi ciram avarṣukaḥ
14.8.10	na sādayitvā graham ādāyādhvaryus tiṣṭhati sūryo mā devo devebhyaḥ pātv iti
14.8.11	tataḥ saṃpreṣyaty ādityebhyaḥ priyebhyaḥ priyadhāmabhyaḥ priyavratebhyo mahasvasarasya patibhya uror antarikṣasyādhyakṣebhyo 'nubrūhīti
14.9.1	ādityaṃ yajamāno 'nvārabhate 'haṃ parastād aham avastād iti
14.9.2	darbhair ācyāvayaty ā samudrād āntarikṣād iti
14.9.3	darbhair apidhāyopaniṣkrāmati kavir yajñasya vi tanoti panthām iti
14.9.4	atyākramyāśrāvyāhādityebhyaḥ priyebhyaḥ priyadhāmabhyaḥ priyavratebhyo mahasvasarasya patibhya uror antarikṣasyādhyakṣebhyaḥ preṣyeti
14.9.5	agnau darbhān prāsyati yās te viśvāḥ samidhaḥ santy agna ity etayā
14.9.6	vaṣaṭkṛte 'nyatrekṣamāṇo juhoti / nānuvaṣaṭkaroti
14.9.7	na hutvānvīkṣeta
14.9.8	unnambhaya pṛthivīm iti vṛṣṭikāmasya juhuyāt
14.9.9	sūdavadādityapātram āyatane sādayitvā saṃpreṣyati pratiprasthātaḥ savanīyān nirvapeti
14.9.10	vasatīvarībhir hotṛcamasaṃ pūrayitvā nigrābhyāsu yajamānaṃ vācayati yathā prātaḥsavane
14.9.11	upāṃśupātrād aṃśum ṛjīṣe 'pisṛjya mahābhiṣavam abhiṣuṇvanti yathā prātaḥsavane
14.9.12	samānam ā grahakālāt
14.9.13	nātra śukrāmanthinau gṛhṇāti
14.9.14	āgrayaṇaṃ catasṛbhyo dhārābhyo gṛhṇāti
14.9.15	ya eṣa āgrayaṇasthālyāṃ rājā tam anyasmin pātre paryāsicya dvitīyāṃ dhārāṃ kurute / ādityapātrāt tṛtīyām / ādityasthālyāś caturthīm
14.10.1	ukthyasyāvṛtokthyaṃ gṛhṇāti yady ukthyasaṃstho bhavati
14.10.2	āgnīdhre manthata āśiraṃ yajamānaḥ patnī ca / patny āśiraṃ manthatīty eke
14.10.3	pūrvayā dvārā yajamānaḥ prapadyate / aparayā patny āśiraṃ prapādayati
14.10.4	yat prāk pavamānagrahebhyas tat kṛtvā yajamānaḥ saha patnyāśiraṃ pūtabhṛty avanayaty asme devāso vapuṣe cikitsatety etābhiś catasṛbhiḥ
14.10.5	samānam ā pavamānāt
14.10.6	pratyañcaḥ prahvā ārbhavaṃ pavamānaṃ sarpanti jāgataḥ panthā ādityā devatāvṛkeṇāparipareṇa pathā svasty ādityān aśīyeti / vāg agregā agra etv iti ca
14.10.7	tasya mādhyaṃdinena pavamānena saṃcaro vyākhyātaḥ
14.10.8	stūyamāne yajamāno 'nvārohaṃ japati saghāsi jagatīchandā iti
14.10.9	samānam ā saṃpraiṣāt
14.10.10	pratiprasthātaḥ paśau saṃvadasveti saṃpraiṣāntaṃ namati
14.10.11	samānam ā dhiṣṇyānāṃ viharaṇāt
14.10.12	śalākābhir jvalato dhiṣṇiyān viharati
14.11.1	upariṣṭād vyāghāraṇaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
14.11.2	api vaitāṃs tatraiva viharet
14.11.3	vyākhyātaṃ savanīyānāṃ nirvapaṇaṃ barhiṣaḥ staraṇam alaṃkaraṇaṃ grahāvakāśopasthānaṃ prasarpaṇam iti
14.11.4	paśunā pracaratīḍāntena
14.11.5	sa eṣa sarveṣu savaneṣu śrāpyate tṛtīyasavane vā
14.11.6	paśunā pracarya savanīyaiḥ pracarati
14.11.7	etāvan nānā / tṛtīyasya savanasyendrāya puroḍāśānām anubrūhi // tṛtīyasya savanasyendrāya puroḍāśān prasthitān preṣyeti saṃpreṣyati
14.11.8	vyākhyātaḥ sviṣṭakṛt / tatheḍā
14.11.9	ādhavanīyaṃ pūtabhṛty avanayati
14.11.10	samānam ā saṃpraiṣāt
14.11.11	etāvan nānā / hotṛcamasam ādāya tṛtīyasya savanasyarbhumato vibhumataḥ prabhumataḥ paribhumato vājavataḥ savitṛvato bṛhaspativato viśvadevyāvatas tīvrāṁ āśīrvata indrāya somān prasthitān preṣyeti saṃpraiṣādiḥ
14.11.12	vaṣaṭkṛte juhvati śyenāya patvane svāheti
14.11.13	anuvaṣaṭkṛte dvitīyaṃ vaṭ svayam abhigūrtāya nama iti
14.11.14	evam eva punar abhyunnatānām uttarābhyām uttarābhyāṃ mantrābhyām uttaram uttaraṃ juhoti
14.11.15	sarvān hutān anumantrayate tṛmpantāṃ hotrā madhor ghṛtasyeti
14.11.16	samānam ā prāśanāt
14.11.17	upanyasanārthān puroḍāśaśakalān nidadhāti
14.11.18	yathācamasaṃ camasino bhakṣayanti / ādityavadgaṇasya soma deva ta ity eṣa eva tṛtīyasavane bhakṣamantro bhavaty anyatra nārāśaṃsebhyaḥ
14.11.19	ubhayīr devatāḥ punar abhyunnīteṣūpalakṣayanti
14.11.20	asarvān bhakṣayitvāpyāyayanti
14.11.21	vyākhyātam āpyāyanasādanam
14.12.1	svaṃ svaṃ camasam anū nyante trīṃs trīn puroḍāśaśakalān upanyasyanti
14.12.2	etat te tata ye ca tvām anv ity ete dānaprabhṛtayaḥ pratyāyanāntā mantrā āmnātā bhavanti yathā piṇḍapitṛyajñe
14.12.3	svebhyaḥ pitāmahebhyo dadyur ity ekam / yajamāna eva mantrāñ japet tūṣṇīm itara upanyasyeyur ity aparam
14.12.4	antaryāmapātreṇa sāvitram āgrayaṇād gṛhṇāti vāmam adya savitar ity etenānuvākena
14.12.5	na sādayati
14.12.6	tataḥ saṃpreṣyati devāya savitre 'nubrūhīti
14.12.7	atyākramyāśrāvyāha devāya savitre preṣyeti
14.12.8	vaṣaṭkṛte juhoti / nānuvaṣaṭkaroti

14.12.10	śastram atra bhavati
14.12.11	yatrābhijānāty ekayā ca daśabhiś ca svabhūta iti tat pratiprasthātā dvidevatyapātrāṇi prakṣālya khare sādayati
14.12.12	yatrābhijānāti pra dyāvā yajñaiḥ pṛthivī ṛtāvṛdhā iti tad anyataratomodaṃ pratigṛṇāti madā moda ivothā moda ivety āvyāhāvāt
14.12.13	śastraṃ pratigīryādatte graham adhvaryuḥ / ādadate nārāśaṃsān

14.12.20	nāpyāyayanti / mārjayante
14.12.21	sarvabhakṣā evāta ūrdhvaṃ tṛtīyasavane camasā bhavanti
14.13.1	tataḥ saumyaṃ caruṃ nirvapati / savanīyair vā saha
14.13.2	tam āsādya yathāgṛhītam ājyaṃ gṛhītvātyākramyāśrāvyāha ghṛtasya yajeti
14.13.3	vaṣaṭkṛte juhoti
14.13.4	atraivopaviśya prācīnāvītaṃ kṛtvā hastena saumyasya pūrvam avadānam avadyati mekṣaṇenottaram
14.13.5	abhighāryodaṅṅ atyākramyāśrāvyāha saumyasya yajeti
14.13.6	vaṣaṭkṛte dakṣiṇārdhe juhoti
14.13.7	atraivopaviśya yajñopavītaṃ kṛtvāpa upaspṛśya yathāgṛhītam ājyaṃ gṛhītvātyākramyāśrāvyāha ghṛtasya yajeti
14.13.8	vaṣaṭkṛte juhoti
14.13.9	anyatarataḥ parījyām eke saumyasya samāmananti
14.13.10	ājyena carum abhipūryodgātṛbhyo haranti
14.13.11	tam avekṣante satro ta etad yad u ta iheti
14.13.12	yady agatāsur bhavati paripaśyati / yadi gatāsuḥ syāt so 'vekṣeta yan me manaḥ parāgatam ity etayā
14.13.13	āmayāvinā prāśyo 'nnādyakāmena prāśyo yo 'lam annādyāya sann annaṃ nādyāt tena prāśya iti vijñāyate
14.13.14	juhvāṃ navagṛhītam ājyaṃ gṛhītvā jvalato dhiṣṇiyān vyāghārayati
14.13.15	vyāghāraṇasaṃpātaṃ nidhāyopāṃśupātreṇa pātnīvatam āgrayaṇād gṛhṇāty upayāmagṛhīto 'si bṛhaspatisutasya ta indo indriyāvataḥ patnīvantaṃ grahaṃ gṛhṇāmīti
14.13.16	vyāghāraṇasaṃpātena śrītvātyākramyāśrāvyāhāgnīt pātnīvatasya yajeti

14.13.18	sānuvaṣaṭkāram eke pātnīvataṃ samāmananty ananuvaṣaṭkāram eke / upāṃśv anuvaṣaṭkarotīty ekeṣām
14.14.1	bhakṣam āharan saṃpreṣyaty agnīn neṣṭur upastham āsīda neṣṭaḥ patnīm udānayonnetar hotṛcamasamukhyāṃś camasān unnaya hotṛcamase dhruvāyāvakāśaṃ kuru sarvaṃ rājānaṃ camaseṣūnnaya daśābhiḥ kalaśau mṛṣṭvā nyubjodgātrā patnīṃ saṃkhyāpayāpa upapravartayeti
14.14.2	yathācoditaṃ kurvanti
14.14.3	antareṇa neṣṭāraṃ dhiṣṇiyaṃ cāgnīdhro vyavasṛpya bhakṣayati / agnipītasyeti bhakṣamantraṃ namati
14.14.4	saṃprajvalayitvā dhiṣṇiyān yajñāyajñīyasya stotram upākaroti
14.14.5	sakarṇaprāvṛtā bhavanty ṛtvijo yajamānaś cāviriva nābhiṃ darśayantaḥ
14.14.6	udgātur hiṅkāraṃ pratyudgātrā patnīm ā tisṛbhyaḥ stotriyābhyaḥ saṃkhyāpayati viśvasya te viśvāvato vṛṣṇiyāvata iti
14.14.7	dakṣiṇaṃ nagnaṃ kṛtvoruṃ patny ūruṇā pannejanīr ā tisṛbhya upapravartayaty agan devān ity anuvākena vaṅkṣaṇān āviṣkurvatī
14.14.8	prācīr upapravartayaty udīcīr vā / prācīr udīcīr ity ekeṣām
14.14.9	parihite stotre śastram upākaroti
14.14.10	yatrābhijānāti svāduṣ kilāyaṃ madhumāṁ utāyam iti tad ubhayatomodaṃ pratigṛṇāti madā moda iva modā moda ivety ā vyāhāvāt
14.14.11	yatrābhijānāty uta no 'hirbudhnyaḥ śṛṇotv etasyāṃ vaiśvadevyām ṛci śasyamānāyāṃ paridhānīyāyāṃ vā sakṛcchastāyāṃ pratiprasthātā hotṛcamase dhruvam avanayiṣyann upatiṣṭhate bhūtam asi bhūte mā dhā iti
14.14.12	athainaṃ hastābhyāṃ parigṛhṇāti dyāvāpṛthivībhyāṃ tvā parigṛhṇāmīti

14.15.1	purastāt pratyaṅ tiṣṭhan hotṛcamase dhruvam avanayati dhruvaṃ dhruveṇety anuvākaśeṣeṇa

14.15.5	atyākramyāśrāvyāhokthaśā yaja somānām iti

14.15.10	atha yady ukthyaḥ sarvaṃ rājānaṃ camaseṣūnnaya daśābhiḥ kalaśau mṛṣṭvā nyubjeti lupyata etat saṃpraiṣasya
14.15.11	agniṣṭomacamasān unnayaṃs tribhyaś camasagaṇebhyo rājānam atirecayati
14.15.12	tata ukthyaṃ vigṛhṇāti yathā prātaḥsavane
14.15.13	etāvan nānā / indrāvaruṇābhyāṃ tveti maitrāvaruṇasya grahaṇasādanau bhavataḥ / indrābṛhaspatibhyāṃ tveti brāhmaṇācchaṃsinaḥ / indrāviṣṇubhyāṃ tvety achāvākasya / evam evaitān bhakṣamantrān namati
14.15.14	iti vai khalu yady ukthyaḥ
14.15.15	atha yadi ṣoḍaśy achāvākacamasān unnayann ekasmai camasagaṇāya sagrahāya rājānam atirecayati / tasminn eva kāle ṣoḍaśinam abhigṛhṇāti
14.15.16	api vainam atraivāgrayaṇād gṛhṇīyāt / na pūrvayoḥ savanayoḥ

14.15.20	stutaśastre atra bhavataḥ
14.16.1	samayāviṣite sūrye hiraṇyena ṣoḍaśinaḥ stotram upākaroti

14.16.4	harivat stotraṃ harivacchastraṃ harivatī yājyā bhavati
14.16.5	ṣoḍaśinam upatiṣṭhate / yasmān na jātaḥ paro anyo asti / ya āviveśa bhuvanāni viśvā / prajāpatiḥ prajayā saṃvidānaḥ / trīṇi jyotīṃṣi sacate sa ṣoḍaśī // iti

14.16.23	iti prathamacamasagaṇaḥ
14.17.1	evaṃvihitā apare trayaś camasagaṇāḥ / maitrāvaruṇacamasamukhyo dvitīyaś camasagaṇo brāhmaṇācchaṃsicamasamukhyas tṛtīyo 'chāvākacamasamukhyaś caturthaḥ
14.17.2	etena śastrayājyānām ānupūrvyaṃ vyākhyātam
14.17.3	iti prathamo rātriparyāyaḥ
14.17.4	evaṃvihitāv aparau dvau bhavataḥ
14.17.5	hotṛcamasamukhyān saṃdhicamasān unnayati
14.17.6	trivṛt stotraṃ bhavati

14.17.9	āśvinaṃ dvikapālaṃ nirvapati
14.17.10	yajurutpūtābhir adbhiḥ puroḍāśaṃ śrapayati
14.17.11	stīrṇa evaṃ barhiṣi piṣṭalepaṃ ninayati
14.17.12	śastraṃ pratigīrya puroḍāśam udvāsya saṃpreṣyaty aśvibhyāṃ tiroahniyānāṃ somānām anubrūhīti
14.17.13	ādatte graham adhvaryuḥ / ādadate camasāṃś camasādhvaryavaḥ / ādatte puroḍāśaṃ pratiprasthātā
14.17.14	atyākramyāśrāvyāhāśvibhyāṃ tiroahniyān somān prasthitān preṣyeti

14.17.18	atha yady aptoryāmaḥ saṃdhicamasān unnayaṃś caturbhyaś camasagaṇebhyo rājānam atirecayati
14.18.1	tatra catvāri stotrāṇi catvāri śastrāṇy āśvināni ca sayājyāny āmnātāni bhavanti

14.18.3	etāvan nānā / hotṛcamasamukhyaḥ prathamaś camasagaṇo maitrāvaruṇacamasamukhyo dvitīyo brāhmaṇācchaṃsicamasamukhyas tṛtīyo 'chāvākacamasamukhyaś caturthaḥ
14.18.4	etena śastrayājyānām ānupūrvyaṃ vyākhyātam
14.18.5	ukthaṃ vācīndrāyetyāha tṛtīyasavanaṃ pratigīrya
14.18.6	atichandaso 'śvipītasyeti bhakṣamantraṃ namati

14.19.1	avaśiṣṭā uttaravedyāṃ nivapanty āpūryā sthā mā pūrayateti

14.19.3	ekadhanapariśeṣeṣu hariṇī dūrvā avadhāya saṃplomnāya tīvrīkṛtya yathācamasaṃ vyānīyāpareṇa cātvālaṃ prāñco 'vajighranty apsu dhautasya soma deva ta iti
14.19.4	avaśiṣṭā antarvedi ninayati cātvāla ity eke / samudraṃ vaḥ prahiṇomi svāṃ yonim apigacchata / ariṣṭā asmākaṃ vīrā utte bhavantu mā parāseci naḥ svam // iti
14.19.5	ninītā anumantrayate / acchāyaṃ vo marutaḥ śloka etvā viṣṇuṃ niṣiktapām avobhiḥ / uta prajāyai gṛṇate vayodhā yūyaṃ pāta svastibhiḥ sadā naḥ // iti

14.20.1	avabhṛthasya tantraṃ prakramayati

14.23.6	te udavasānīyāyām adhvaryave dattaḥ
14.23.7	tata unnetāraṃ saṃpreṣyaty unnetar vasīyo na unnayābhi / ud ut te madhumattamā giraḥ stomāsa īrate / satrājito dhanasā akṣitotayo vājayanto rathā iva / kaṇvā iva bhṛgavaḥ sūryā iva viśvam iddhītam ānaśuḥ // iti
14.23.8	unnetā hotṛprathamān yajamānaprathamān vonnayati / udeta prajām uta varco dadhānā yuṣmān rāya uta yajñā asṛkṣata / gāyatraṃ chando 'nusaṃrabhadhvam athāsyā atha surabhayo gṛheṣu // iti
14.23.9	udgāhamānā udakāntaṃ pratyasyanti pratiyuto varuṇasya pāśa iti
14.23.10	samidhaḥ kṛtvāpratīkṣam āyanty unnetāraṃ puraskṛtya mahīyāṃ japanto 'pāma somam amṛtā abhūmety etām / yāny apāmityāny apratīttāny asmi yamasya balinā carāmi / ihaiva santaḥ prati tad yātayāmo jīvā jīvebhyo niharāma enat // anṛṇā asminn anṛṇāḥ parasmiṃs tṛtīye loke anṛṇāḥ syāma / ye devayānā uta pitṛyāṇāḥ sarvān patho anṛṇā ākṣīyema // iti
14.23.11	edho 'sy edhiṣīmahīty āhavanīye samidha ādhāyopatiṣṭhante 'po anvacāriṣam iti
14.23.12	evaṃ patnī gārhapatye 'bhyādhāyopatiṣṭhate
14.24.1	udayanīyāyās tantraṃ prakramayati
14.24.2	yaḥ prāyaṇīyaḥ sa udayanīyaḥ
14.24.3	etāvan nānā / prāyaṇīyasya niṣkāsa udayanīyam opya śrapayati / nātroddhṛtya carum āsādayati na ṣaḍḍhotrā
14.24.4	śālāmukhīya udayanīyena caranti
14.24.5	yāḥ prāyaṇīyasya puronuvākyās tā udayanīyasya yājyāḥ karoti
14.24.6	pathyāṃ svastim uttamām ājyabhāgānāṃ yajati
14.24.7	na yajamānaḥ prāśnāti
14.24.8	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
14.24.9	anūbandhyāyās tantraṃ prakramayati
14.24.10	samānam ā paśūpākaraṇāt
14.24.11	maitrāvaruṇīṃ vaśām anūbandhyām upākaroti
14.24.12	tisra eke samāmananti / dvirūpāṃ maitrāvaruṇīṃ bahurūpāṃ vaiśvadevīṃ rohiṇīṃ bārhaspatyām / upāṃśu vaiśvadevyā madhyataḥ pracaratīty ekeṣām
14.24.13	samānam ā vapāyā homāt
14.24.14	hutāyāṃ vapāyāṃ dakṣiṇasyāṃ vediśroṇyāṃ pariśrite yajamānaḥ keśaśmaśru vāpayate
14.24.15	anūbandhyāyāḥ paśupuroḍāśaṃ devikāhavīṃṣy anunirvapati dhātre puroḍāśaṃ dvādaśakapālam ity etāni
14.24.16	uttamaṃ dhātāraṃ karoti
14.24.17	yāsu sthālīṣu somā bhavanti tāsv etāṃś ca śrapayanti
14.24.18	praiṣavān paśupuroḍāśaḥ / anubrūhi // yajetītarebhyaḥ saṃpreṣyati
14.24.19	sarveṣāṃ sapaśupuroḍāśānāṃ samānaḥ sviṣṭakṛt praiṣavān / samāneḍā
14.24.20	siddhaḥ paśuḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
14.25.1	api vā maitrāvaruṇīm āmikṣāṃ paśukāmaḥ kurvītānūbandhyāyā vikalpārthām
14.25.2	purastāt tv eva keśaśmaśru vāpayate
14.25.3	agreṇa havirdhānam āsīno hotā yajati
14.25.4	devikāhavirbhiḥ pracaryāmikṣāyai devatena pracarati
14.25.5	havirāhutiprabhṛtīḍāntā saṃtiṣṭhate
14.25.6	tantram āmikṣāyai devikāhaviṣāṃ ca sviṣṭakṛdiḍam
14.25.7	sadohavirdhāne prathamakṛtān granthīn visrasya havirdhāne udīcī abhipravartayanti
14.25.8	āhavanīyād barhir upoṣati yat kusīdam apratīttaṃ mayīti
14.25.9	yadi miśram iva cared añjalinā saktūn pradāvye juhuyād viśvalopa viśvadāvasya tvāsañ juhomīti
14.25.10	tato devatā upatiṣṭhate 'yaṃ no nabhasā pura ity āhavanīyaṃ pradāvyaṃ vā / sa tvaṃ no nabhasaspata iti vāyum / deva saṃsphānety ādityam
14.25.11	yūpam upasthāya pṛthag araṇīṣv agnīn samāropayati prājahitaṃ dakṣiṇāgnim / śālāmukhīyaṃ tṛtīyaṃ gataśrīḥ samāropayate
14.25.12	antareṇa cātvālotkarāvatīmokṣān japanta udavasyanti yathā darśapūrṇamāsayoḥ
14.25.13	prāñca udavasyanty udañco vā / prāñcodañca ityekeṣām
14.26.1	āgneyaṃ pañcakapālam udavasānīyaṃ nirvapaty aṣṭākapālaṃ vā
14.26.2	paṅktyau yājyānuvākye bhavato yady aṣṭākapālaḥ / gāyatryau yadi pañcakapālaḥ
14.26.3	anaḍvān dakṣiṇā
14.26.4	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate yadi na tvareta
14.26.5	atha yadi tvareta juhvāṃ caturgṛhītam ājyaṃ gṛhītvā uru viṣṇo vi kramasvety āhavanīye juhuyāt
14.26.6	yat tatra śaknuyāt tad dadyāt
14.26.7	sa yāvad rātre ceṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate tāvad rātra eva sāyam agnihotraṃ juhuyāt / kāla eva prātar agnihotram
14.26.8	udayanīyāprabhṛti yajñapuccham
14.26.9	sadyaḥ sutyā saṃtiṣṭhate
14.26.10	atha yadi sutyā yadāgnihotrakālam abhyatīyāt sāyam agnihotraprabhṛtīny agnihotrāṇy atipannāni pratijuhuyāt / na vā pratijuhuyāt
14.26.11	yo rājā san rājyo vā somena yajate sa devasuvāṃ havīṃṣy anunirvapati
14.26.12	teṣāṃ rājasūya eva kalpo vyākhyāto 'nyatra hastigrahaṇādāvedanānmukhavimārjanād iti
14.26.13	vasante vasante jyotiṣṭomena yajeta / tasya tisro dakṣiṇā iti vijñāyate
14.26.14	saṃtiṣṭhate jyotiṣṭomaḥ saṃtiṣṭhate jyotiṣṭomaḥ
15.1.1	some vāsiṣṭho brahmā bhavati
15.1.2	apy avāsiṣṭhaṃ kurvīta yaḥ kaśca stomabhāgān vidyād iti vijñāyate
15.1.3	rājño mīyamānasya krīyamāṇasyeti dakṣiṇata āste
15.1.4	ohyamānasya dakṣiṇata eti
15.1.5	mahāvedyā uttaravedyā iti kriyamāṇāyā dakṣiṇata āste
15.1.6	yatra sadohavirdhānāni saṃmāsyanto bhavanti tad antareṇa cātvālotkarāv anvavetyottaraṃ vedyantam anuparītya pūrvayā dvārā prāgvaṃśaṃ praviśyāpareṇāhavanīyam atikramya pūrvayā dvāropaniṣkramya dakṣiṇaṃ vedyantam anuparītya dakṣiṇenottaravedim upaviśed ity āśmarathyaḥ / antareṇa cātvālotkarāv anvavetyāpareṇottaravedim atikramya dakṣiṇata upaviśed ity ālekhanaḥ
15.1.7	so'traivāsta ā vaisarjanānāṃ homāt
15.1.8	yatra vaisarjanāni hoṣyanto bhavanti dakṣiṇena havirdhāne dakṣiṇena mārjālīyaṃ dakṣiṇena sadaḥ parītya pūrvayā dvārā prāgvaṃśaṃ praviśyāgreṇa śālāmukhīyam atikramya dakṣiṇata upaviśed ity āśmarathyaḥ / apareṇottaravedim atikramyottareṇa havirdhāne uttareṇāgnīdhrīyam uttareṇa sadaḥ parītya pūrvayā dvārā prāgvaṃśaṃ praviśyāpareṇa śālāmukhīyam atikramya dakṣiṇata upaviśed ity ālekhanaḥ
15.2.1	upasthe brahmā rājānaṃ kurute
15.2.2	hute vaisarjane 'nvaṅṅ agneḥ pratipadyate
15.2.3	āgnīdhrīyaṃ prāpya pratiprasthātre rājānaṃ pradāya yathetaṃ pratiparītya pūrvayā dvāropaniṣkramya dakṣiṇena sado dakṣiṇena mārjālīyaṃ parītya dakṣiṇenāgnīdhrīyam upaviśed ity āśmarathyaḥ / etam evāgnim uttarataḥ parītya dakṣiṇata upaviśed ity ālekhanaḥ
15.2.4	upasthe brahmā rājānaṃ kurute
15.2.5	hute vaisarjane pūrvaḥ pratipadyate
15.2.6	havirdhāne prāpya pratiprasthātre rājānaṃ pradāya dakṣiṇena havirdhāne parītya dakṣiṇenottaravedim upaviśed ity āśmarathyaḥ / uttareṇa havirdhāne 'pareṇottaravedim atikramya dakṣiṇata upaviśed ity ālekhanaḥ
15.2.7	so 'traivāsta āgnīṣomīyasya vapāyā homāt
15.2.8	hutāyāṃ vapāyāṃ yatra mārjayante tan mārjayate
15.3.1	yatra vasatīvarīr gṛhīṣyanto bhavanti tad dakṣiṇata eti
15.3.2	gṛhyamāṇānāṃ dakṣiṇata āste
15.3.3	yatra prātaranuvākāya budhyante tad budhyate
15.3.4	tasya sa eva saṃcaro yaḥ sadohavirdhānāni saṃmāsyatsu
15.3.5	prātaranuvāka upākṛte vācaṃ yacchaty ā paridhānīyāyāḥ
15.3.6	yatra savanīyā apo gṛhīṣyanto bhavanti tad dakṣiṇata eti
15.3.7	gṛhyamāṇānāṃ dakṣiṇata āste
15.3.8	āhriyamāṇānāṃ dakṣiṇata eti
15.3.9	yatra rājānam abhiṣoṣyanto bhavanti tat pūrvayā dvārā havirdhānaṃ praviśyāgreṇa kharam atikramya dakṣiṇata upaviśati
15.3.10	rājño mīyamānasyābhiṣūyamāṇasyeti dakṣiṇata āste
15.3.11	graheṣu gṛhyamāṇeṣu vācaṃ yacchaty āgrayaṇāt
15.3.12	evam eva savane savane rājño 'bhiṣūyamāṇasya dakṣiṇata āste graheṣu gṛhyamāṇeṣu vācaṃ yacchati
15.3.13	yatra bahiṣpavamānaṃ sarpanti tat samanvārabdhaḥ sarpati
15.3.14	stoṣyamāṇānāṃ dakṣiṇata upaviśati
15.4.1	yatrainam āmantrayate brahman stoṣyāmaḥ praśāstar iti tat prasauti hiṃ deva savitar etat te prāha tat pra ca suva pra ca yaja bṛhaspatir brahmāyuṣmatyā ṛco mā gāta tanūpāt sāmnaḥ satyā va āśiṣaḥ santu satyā ākūtaya ṛtaṃ ca satyaṃ ca vadata stuta devasya savituḥ prasave / raśmir asi kṣayāya tvā kṣayaṃ jinvoṁ stuteti
15.4.2	evam eva stotre stotre prasauti
15.4.3	evaṃ stomabhāgānām uttaram uttaraṃ dadhāti
15.4.4	dvādaśāgniṣṭome / trayodaśātyagniṣṭome / pañcadaśokthye / ṣoḍaśa ṣoḍaśini / saptadaśa vājapeye / ekānnatriṃśatam atirātre / trayastriṃśatam aptoryāma iti vijñāyate
15.4.5	stute bahiṣpavamāne 'pareṇottaravedim atikramya dakṣiṇata upaviśati / so 'traivāsta ā savanīyasya vapāyā homāt
15.4.6	hutāyāṃ vapāyāṃ yatra mārjayante tan mārjayate
15.4.7	yatra prātaḥsavanāya saṃprasarpanti tad dakṣiṇena havirdhāne dakṣiṇena mārjālīyaṃ dakṣiṇena sadaḥ parītyāparayā dvārā sadaḥ praviśyāpareṇa praśāstrīyam atikramya dakṣiṇata upaviśed ity āśmarathyaḥ / apareṇottaravedim atikramyottareṇa havirdhāne dakṣiṇena mārjālīyaṃ parītya pūrvayā dvārā sadaḥ praviśyāgreṇa praśāstrīyam atikramya dakṣiṇata upaviśed ity ālekhanaḥ
